# Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cemetery: Hall of the Dead ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Riften%29)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Hall_of_the_Dead "Lore:Hall of the Dead")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RiftenMausoleum | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |

.jpg)

Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is a small gravesite below the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It serves as an embalming room where [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra"), the resident caretaker, works.

## NPCs Living Here

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") make peace with her dead father.

## Hall of the Dead

.jpg)

Interior of the Hall of the Dead

Upon entering the Hall of the Dead from Riften, to your right is a small nook with a coffin that contains minor loot, while to your left is a door leading up to the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"). If you came in through the temple, then to your right is the door to Riften.

In the central room is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") on a table. This is where you will most likely find [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra"), who tends to the dead. In one corner of the room is a [Shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay"), which bestows the [Blessing of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Blessing of Arkay") for eight hours when used, surrounded by three loose gold coins, two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and two [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). Branching out from the central room are corridors that lead to a few coffins with minor loot and the urns of any NPCs that have died recently. The urns contain the dead NPCs' belongings. Otherwise, the Riften Hall of the Dead is relatively empty.

## Notes

There is a small, square inaccessible area in the Hall immediately to the left (north) of the entrance from Riften, which can be seen on the local map. PC users can enter this area by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to [toggle collision](/wiki/Skyrim:Console#tcl "Skyrim:Console"), but the area is empty.

# Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cemetery: Hall of the Dead ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Solitude%29)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Hall_of_the_Dead "Lore:Hall of the Dead")) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SolitudeHalloftheDead | |
| Location | |
| In [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), southeast of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") and northwest of [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") | |

The Solitude Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is where [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s dead are brought to be prepared for burial.

.jpg)

The interior of Solitude's Hall of the Dead

Solitude's Hall of the Dead is tended by [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr"), a priest of Arkay. There is a [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") in front room, which will grant you the [Blessing of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessings#Blessing_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Blessings") for eight hours. The dead themselves are buried in [Solitude Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Catacombs "Skyrim:Solitude Catacombs"), which can be accessed through the door in the basement.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr") |

## Related Quests

- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

### Exterior

| Plants |
| --- |
| 1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")  7 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade")  8 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") |

### Solitude's Hall of the Dead

_02.jpg)

Shrine of Arkay

Upon entering you are in a small room with a small pillar, opposite is an unlocked door. In the right half of the room is a firepit with a stone wall around it. In the eastern corner there is a wooden bench and narrow table against the walls with a low table in front of them. On the tables are; a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese, a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a common book, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") in a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"). In the northern corner there is a small unit with an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") and the shrine to Arkay.

Around the central pillar there are several [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull"), including one [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") on a table. The left half of the room is dominated by a table and chairs in the center. The table is set for two, plates containing a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), as well as two goblets, a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), bread and cheese. Beside the table is an open crate containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding several random [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), including two [bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), a [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), two [battleaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). To the right of this against the southwest wall is a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") on a unit. In the western corner there is a barrel of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and a set of shelves against the northwest wall holding a potion of regeneration, a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and one of [minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), several wheels of cheese, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and six [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). To the left of the internal door is a small set of shelves holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow").

Through the door, on your right is a small wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a wall shelf above with a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower and common book on it. In the eastern corner is a round table with a goblet on top. Opposite the door, against the northwest wall is a narrow table holding a bowl of bread, a plate of [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a sack underneath. To the southwest are flights of stairs leading up and down. At the bottom of the stairs there are a pile of sacks containing foodstuffs and a corridor flanked by rows of lit braziers leading to a closed door that gives access to **Solitude's catacombs**.

Climbing the stairs to the top floor, you come to a landing with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush in a planter at the top of the stairs, a wardrobe containing clothes against the northwest wall with a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") on top. Opposite the top of the stairs on the northeast wall is the door to [Styrr's](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr") bedroom. Against the southeast wall is a large round wooden table holding three common books, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") and a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"). Next to this against the northeast wall is another narrow table holding bread and cheese in a bowl and on a plate respectively and a sack underneath. Above the narrow table is a wall shelf holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead").

Styrr's bedroom consists of a double owned bed in the northern corner and an open crate at the foot containing a potion of regeneration and [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"). To the right against the northeast wall is a tall wardrobe containing clothes. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") behind the door in the western corner to the left of a cupboard. Against the southwest wall there is a long unlocked chest, with a wall shelf above it holding a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves with two [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") and a basket containing two bunches of lavender. To the left of the unit is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), with a couple of sacks to the left of these. In the eastern corner in front of another cupboard is a low table and chair. On the table is a plate of bread and cheese, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a goblet.

## Overview

.jpg)

Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is the final resting place for many of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s late residents.

The building is located in the Wind District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is the second building on the right from the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree, between the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") and the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born"). There are two parts to the building, the *[Hall of the Dead](#Hall_of_the_Dead)*, and the *[Catacombs](#Whiterun_Catacombs)*.

The hall and catacombs are maintained by a single priest, [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs"). If a resident of Whiterun should die, their remains will be interred in the catacombs, in a coffin or urn, along with all of the items they carried in life.

## NPCs Living Here

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") |

## Related Quests

- **[Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet")**: Retrieve [Andurs'](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") from the catacombs.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") make peace with her dead father.

### Hall of the Dead

This first area serves as Andurs' living quarters and chapel. The middle section of the room contains six [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants and two benches, with the door to the catacombs at the far end. The section to the right is the chapel, and contains two benches and a [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay"). The section to the left contains two benches and three lavender plants, and the door to Andurs' bedroom.

Andurs' bedroom contains his owned bed, two wardrobes, a chest containing gold, and a chair by a table. On the table is a coin purse, a [Weak Aversion to Fire potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Fire "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Fire"), and three books. On the shelf above the table is a [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"). To the left of the table is a bookshelf containing various books.

### Whiterun Catacombs

The Catacombs are where the bodies of the dead are interred. It is guarded by three respawning skeletons: to the right is the first, at the bottom of the stairs is the second, and in the closed room to the left of the main door is the third. Also in this room is a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* and two coin purses. Down the stairs on the left, in the first bottom alcove on the left, is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). In the room behind the second skeleton is [Andurs' Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet"), which only appears once the quest [Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet") has begun and can be found on the small table to the right of the brazier.

NPCs that can be buried here are:

- [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam")

- There is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the entrance door. This is because the Whiterun Catacombs are inhabited by skeletons.
- There is an unused burial urn ref for the cut NPC [Terek](/wiki/Skyrim:Terek "Skyrim:Terek").

.jpg)

Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is the final resting place for many of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s late residents.

The building is located in the Wind District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is the second building on the right from the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree, between the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") and the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born"). There are two parts to the building, the *[Hall of the Dead](#Hall_of_the_Dead)*, and the *[Catacombs](#Whiterun_Catacombs)*.

The hall and catacombs are maintained by a single priest, [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs"). If a resident of Whiterun should die, their remains will be interred in the catacombs, in a coffin or urn, along with all of the items they carried in life.

## NPCs Living Here

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") |

## Related Quests

- **[Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet")**: Retrieve [Andurs'](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") from the catacombs.
- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") make peace with her dead father.

### Hall of the Dead

This first area serves as Andurs' living quarters and chapel. The middle section of the room contains six [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants and two benches, with the door to the catacombs at the far end. The section to the right is the chapel, and contains two benches and a [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay"). The section to the left contains two benches and three lavender plants, and the door to Andurs' bedroom.

Andurs' bedroom contains his owned bed, two wardrobes, a chest containing gold, and a chair by a table. On the table is a coin purse, a [Weak Aversion to Fire potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Fire "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Fire"), and three books. On the shelf above the table is a [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"). To the left of the table is a bookshelf containing various books.

### Whiterun Catacombs

The Catacombs are where the bodies of the dead are interred. It is guarded by three respawning skeletons: to the right is the first, at the bottom of the stairs is the second, and in the closed room to the left of the main door is the third. Also in this room is a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* and two coin purses. Down the stairs on the left, in the first bottom alcove on the left, is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). In the room behind the second skeleton is [Andurs' Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet"), which only appears once the quest [Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet") has begun and can be found on the small table to the right of the brazier.

NPCs that can be buried here are:

- There is an unused burial urn ref for the cut NPC [Terek](/wiki/Skyrim:Terek "Skyrim:Terek").

# Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is a small gravesite located in the north end of the graveyard in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Helgird](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgird "Skyrim:Helgird") |

## Related Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.

## Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)

Shrine of Arkay

The entrance to the Hall of the Dead is located on the north wall of the graveyard, which is north of Windhelm's small market area.
The entrance is a little dreary, as befitting a crypt, with only a couple of food barrels. Down the stairs, is a T-junction. Turning left you enter Helgird's chambers. The room is elongated, and candles provide some ambient lighting. Straight ahead is a small table, which is rather bare. Looking to the left, find a set of shelves with only a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Leaning against the shelves is a knapsack holding a random book, a leveled [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and some jewelry. To the right of the doorway, a low table holds [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Next is a wardrobe holding only clothes. Further into the room is the owned bed, but little else.
Exit the room, and head south to enter the crypts. At the bottom of the stairs the doorway to the right opens to the [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay"), which bestows the [Blessing of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Blessing of Arkay") for eight hours when activated. The crypts are honeycombed into multiple sections, but hold nothing of interest.

Once Blood on the Ice has progressed sufficiently, the body of [Susanna the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked") will be laid out on a table for autopsy by Helgird. The body will remain here for the rest of the game.

## Bugs

- When a resident of Windhelm dies, that person's belongings should be transferred to a named coffin or urn within the Hall of the Dead, but the NPC's name will not be attached to the container.

# Skyrim:Hall of the Elements

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Guild: Hall of the Elements ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Elements)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WinterholdCollegeHallofTheElements | |
| Region | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Location | |
| [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | |

The statue of [Shalidor](/wiki/Lore:Shalidor "Lore:Shalidor") at the front entrance

The **Hall of the Elements** is a large training and meeting chamber inside the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

Besides training spell casting, the chamber is also used for teaching classes, lectures, and meetings.

## Related Quests

- **[First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons")**: Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
- **[The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus")**: Reclaim the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and contain the Eye.

## Walkthrough

Inside the hall with the Eye of Magnus at the center

A pair of massive wooden doors serves as the main entrance. These open to the antechamber, which has two doors: one to the northwest that leads to the [Arch-Mage's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters"), and one to the southeast that leads to the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). The hall itself is a large circular room with a high ceiling supported by a ring of pillars. The hall is entered through a pair of large gates which have the College symbol worked into the design. Around the outside edge of the hall is a series of wooden benches, with small light spheres between every two benches. There is a large focus point in the center of the room, with magical energy rising from it up to the ceiling above. During most of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus") is kept in the hall, floating above the focus point.

## Notes

- It is impossible to [wait](/wiki/Skyrim:Waiting "Skyrim:Waiting") in the Hall of the Elements.
- Lectures are regularly held here. For details, see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place)#Lectures "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
- When the Eye of Magnus appears in the Hall of the Elements, there is an option to "Activate Eye of Magnus" when you point your crosshairs over it in close proximity, but doing so has no effect.

## Bugs

- The stone platform beneath the focus point may fail to render, leaving the hourglass shaped focus point and blue pillar of light floating in midair, revealing a triangular compound dodecagon (12 pointed star) in the center of some beautifully organized masonry resting within the surrounding outer circle where the stairs should be. No problems appear to be caused by this happening. **?**
- The main entrance of the hall may be in the opened animation from the outside and cause you to be unable to enter. **?**
  - A reload fixes this.

The Hall of the Vigilant

The **Hall of the Vigilant** is a secluded [lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), home to the [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr").

The [Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") are led by [Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Keeper Carcette"), who offers expert [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration").

### Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Keeper Carcette") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Restoration (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Restoration (Expert)") †  [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") † |

† They are all killed once you either reach level 10 with Dawnguard installed or start the quest [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

## Related Quests

- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

### Exterior

The path leading to the hall is off of the road between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and starts a short distance south of [Red Road Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Road_Pass "Skyrim:Red Road Pass"). At the front of the hall is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and small stable that is big enough for a single [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), while the rear of the building backs up to a rock face. There is a short flight of steps leading up to a covered porch with a few barrels and crates stacked at either side of the only entrance. If [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") can be found down the road north of the building.

### Hall of the Vigilant

Hall of the Vigilant

Entering the hall leads directly into a large common room with a long fire pit across the width of the room at the eastern end. There are two [venison chops](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop") on the edge of the pit and hanging above the far end is a rack holding five [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Behind the fire pit are a few barrels, one of which has a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") on top, while from the ceiling hang two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In the northeastern corner is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") and a [potion of the defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender") on top. At the western end of the room is a long wooden table with a [shrine to Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr") on top, along with a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"), a random, possibly enchanted [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), a couple of [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and some plates. All of these items are marked as owned, and taking them is considered stealing. There are three pairs of wooden benches facing the shrine.

Opposite the entrance is a practice dummy with some bales of straw behind it and a long wooden table to the left. On the table are two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") in a bowl. In the southeastern corner is a couple of barrels, with a tall wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") to the right and a narrow table against the south wall, to the left. In the northwestern corner is the top of a flight of stairs leading to the basement. Against the north wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, and four loaves of bread. To the right of this is a door to a larger bedroom used by [Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Keeper Carcette").

It contains an unowned single bed (see [bugs](#Bugs)) coming out from the north wall with an expert-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot and small bedside tables on either side. To the right is a narrow wooden table with three bottles of alto wine, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and an empty [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top and a food sack and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") underneath. Against the east wall is a dresser with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and some cheap crockery on top. In the southeastern corner is a long wooden table with another alchemy lab built in and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a medium coin purse, three bottles of wine, a bowl of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), four loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins and some bread on top.

The cellar

Along the south wall are two small bedrooms. The first contains a single bed in the southeast corner with an unlocked wooden chest and wardrobe at the foot of it and a round wooden table and chair to the right, with a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a bowl of [tomato soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato_Soup "Skyrim:Tomato Soup") on the table top. The second bedroom contains a single bed in the southwestern corner with an unlocked chest and dresser at the foot and a wooden table and chair to the left, with a bottle of alto wine on the table top. On the dresser is a basket containing three [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and a bowl containing a loaf of bread and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek").

The staircase leads down to a wooden door with another flight of stairs opening into a large room containing six empty weapon racks on the west wall with an unlocked chest to the left. Against the south wall is a set of shelves holding two [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") and four [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), two bunches of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), three [potions of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), one of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of the Knight](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Knight "Skyrim:Potion of the Knight"). To the left is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") with a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), and a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust") on top. In the southeastern corner is another practice dummy with bales behind it, and leaning against the east wall on top of a small unit is a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). In the northeastern corner is a low table and chair with a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Knights of the Nine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Knights_of_the_Nine "Skyrim:The Knights of the Nine")*, a medium coin purse and five loose gold coins. All of these items, including the book, are also owned by the Vigilants.

#### Dawnguard

.jpg)

The destroyed hall

.jpg)

The interior of the hall after being attacked

With the [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, the Hall of the Vigilant is destroyed by [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") once you reach level 10 or start the quest [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)"). As you approach you will see blood splatters on the ground, then the body of a [death hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"). The tanning rack and front porch will both have been destroyed, while inside will be a complete shamble, with the bodies of dead Vigilants, dead vampires and death hounds among the smoldering rubble, along with a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")* and miscellaneous clutter. There is an unlocked chest in the eastern corner, the long table where the shrine to Stendarr once stood, and a food barrel at the back of the room. Unlike when the Hall was operational, nothing will be owned by the Vigilants anymore, and everything will now be free to take. Nothing else of interest survived the fire, nor is the basement accessible any longer.

## Notes

- This location can be marked as cleared by killing all the Vigilants inside. With Dawnguard installed, this becomes impossible after level 10, due to the Hall's destruction.
  - Once killed, the residents will not respawn.
  -  The Hall can be reverted to its original form by entering the code `"xx003531".enable` into the console.
- If you ask the Vigilants stationed here who they are, only the "Yes. Our order was founded after the Oblivion Crisis. We dedicate our lives to facing the threat of Daedra wherever they appear." line will be heard.
- If Dawnguard is installed and your character is here when level 10 is reached, the Hall may not be destroyed until you travel far enough away. Fast traveling here immediately after reaching level 10 with Dawnguard installed may also yield the same results.
- With the Hall destroyed, none of its interior cells can be accessed anymore, as the ruin exists as an exterior cell only. If you were to use the console to teleport to these cells, you will find that they remain unaltered.
-  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the searchable barrel outside as owned by the Vigilants. This will, of course, no longer be the case once the building is destroyed.
- Even if the Hall is destroyed, the wood chopping block outside will remain unscathed and fully functional.

## Bugs

- Loading a save made in the cellar after installing *Dawnguard* will corrupt that save and/or cause several errors due to the area being broken. It will be locked with no way in or out. **?**
- Even after the Hall is destroyed, Vigilants may still tell you about its location, and also say that Keeper Carcette runs it, even though she is already dead by then. **?**
- Two of the beds are incorrectly marked as owned by the [Riverwood Sleeping Giant Inn Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions_R#Riverwood_Sleeping_Giant_Inn_Faction "Skyrim:Factions R"), and the other is incorrectly marked as unowned.[[1]](#cite_note-1) **?**
  -  This is fixed by version 3.0.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), which marks all three beds as owned by the Vigilants. This will, of course, no longer be the case once the building is destroyed.
- The four barrels in the main hall are incorrectly marked as owned by the Riverwood Town Faction, meaning they can be looted freely.[[2]](#cite_note-2) **?**
  -  This is fixed by version 4.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), which marks them as owned by the Vigilants. This will, of course, no longer be the case once the building is destroyed.

# Skyrim:Hall of Valor

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Building: Hall of Valor | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Sovngarde01 | |
| Location | |
| [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") | |

The Hall of Valor

The **Hall of Valor** is a massive stone mead hall in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") where dead Nord heroes are rewarded by [Shor](/wiki/Lore:Shor "Lore:Shor") with an eternity of revelry.

Roasted oxen

It is the gathering place of the heroes who plot to defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") and end his reign of terror. It can only be entered after defeating [Tsun](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsun "Skyrim:Tsun"), the shield-thane of Shor, in a duel.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Honored Souls | | --- | | **[Erlendr](/wiki/Skyrim:Erlendr "Skyrim:Erlendr")**  **[Felldir the Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Felldir_the_Old "Skyrim:Felldir the Old")**  **[Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt")**  **[Hakon One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Hakon_One-Eye "Skyrim:Hakon One-Eye")**  **[Hunroor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunroor "Skyrim:Hunroor")**  **[Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Jurgen Windcaller")**  **[Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas "Skyrim:Nikulas")**  **[Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye")**  **[Ulfgar the Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfgar_the_Unending "Skyrim:Ulfgar the Unending")**  **[Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor")** | |

In addition to these famous heroes, the honored souls of **[Heroes of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:Hero of Sovngarde")** whose names have been lost to time also walk the Hall of Valor.

## Related Quests

- **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") within [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
- **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the [World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### Exterior

The exterior of the huge mead hall is Sovngarde. The whalebone bridge leading to the hall is guarded by Tsun. You must battle him to prove your worth and be allowed to proceed across the bridge. On the far side, a paved terrace features two curved flights of stairs ascending to a row of four doors that all lead into the hall.

### Hall of Valor

East Feasting Wing

Central Feasting Area

West Sparring Wing

Although the interior of the Hall consists of only one zone, it can be visually divided into three areas. The entrance leads into the central area, with huge chambers to the west and east. Throughout the hall are many [Heroes of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:Hero of Sovngarde"), as well as several important people from Skyrim's history. When you first enter, [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor") will approach and greet you, stating that three heroes have awaited your arrival to aid you in the battle with Alduin. These are the three you saw defeat Alduin in a vision from the past when using the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Dragon) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Dragon)"): [Felldir the Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Felldir_the_Old "Skyrim:Felldir the Old"), [Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt"), and [Hakon One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Hakon_One-Eye "Skyrim:Hakon One-Eye").

The central area is mainly for feasting. A huge raised fire pit is in the middle of the area, with two whole oxen turning on a spit. A long table is on the south side of the fire pit near the entrance, while another is on the north side on a raised section in front of Shor's empty throne. Both tables are laid with golden plates, platters, and goblets; the [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and drink found on these tables and elsewhere in the hall is listed below. Many small empty barrels and three large mead kegs line the walls. Heroes come here to feast and enjoy the music of the [Hero Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:Hero of Sovngarde"), who mainly plays the [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute").

The west wing is a vast bare chamber reserved for sparring matches. Heroes who belong to the [Sovngarde Sparring Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:MQSovngardeSparringFaction "Skyrim:MQSovngardeSparringFaction") come here to quench their thirst for battle, uncertain why Shor has forbidden engaging Alduin in combat. Raised sections along the north and south walls with tables and rows of benches allow spectators to watch the matches. Stairs to the west allow access to the raised sections, and two large mead kegs are against the west wall.

The east wing is also for feasting, with large mead kegs against the walls and two small tables and a horseshoe of longer tables in the middle. All of the tables are laid with more golden crockery. Heroes come here to feast and enjoy the music of the [Hero Drummer](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:Hero of Sovngarde"), who prefers this hall for his performances.

| Food and Drink | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - 4 [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") - 3 [Apple Pies](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") - 1 [Baked Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") - 14 [Bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") - 4 [Cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") | - 2 [Eidar Cheese Wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") - 7 [Green Apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") - 2 [Grilled Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") - 5 [Goat Cheese Wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") - 1 [Goat Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") | - 5 [Gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") - 1 [Honey Nut Treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") - 2 [Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") - 8 [Potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") - 10 [Red Apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") | - 2 [Roasted Ox Legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Roasted_Ox_Leg "Skyrim:Roasted Ox Leg") ‡ - 1 [Roasted Ox Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Roasted_Ox_Head "Skyrim:Roasted Ox Head") ‡ - 2 [Salmon Steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") - 1 [Seared Slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") - 1 [Sliced Eidar Cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") | - 3 [Sliced Goat Cheeses](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") - 4 [Sweet Rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") † - 10 [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") † |
| ‡ Only available in this location. Categorized as miscellaneous items rather than food.  † (see [bugs](#Bugs)) | | | | |

## Notes

- If you attempt to cross the bridge to the hall without dueling Tsun, you will be killed by lightning strikes on the bridge, even in [god mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"). You will also automatically die if you fall into the chasm beneath the bridge, though not in god mode.
- Inside the hall, you are unable to sneak, wait, or draw or equip your weapon. (Unless you use `coc Sovngarde01` to teleport there, since the effect is triggered by interacting with the door.)
- Inside the hall, none of the golden crockery can be taken.
- After slaying Alduin, the hall will be locked, and you cannot reenter.

## Bugs

- You may not be able to interact with one of the bottles of wine and a sweet roll on a bench.
- One named hero may be missing from the hall; this missing hero will be different upon each entry. (You must reload a previous save to enter the hall again.) **?**

# Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Halldir's Cairn ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halldir%27s+Cairn)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |

Halldir's Cairn

**Halldir's Cairn** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost"), and the powerful undead mage [Halldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir "Skyrim:Halldir"). It contains only one zone, *[Halldir's Cairn](#Halldir.27s_Cairn)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The path from the road west of Falkreath twists and turns through the rocks and past an unmarked [hunter's camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Bear_Hunter.27s_Camp "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath") before reaching the cave entrance. There are two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), one on either side of the entrance, and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") to the right of the entrance.

### Halldir's Cairn

Halldir's cairn

There are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") in the first chamber of the dungeon, one on the left as you descend into the chamber, and the other on a ledge north of the cairn. There are over fifty samples of various fungi in this chamber alone, comprising [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), fly amanita, [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"). The entire dungeon contains 9 bleeding crown, 10 blisterwort, 12 fly amanita, 21 imp stool, 21 Namira's rot, and 22 white cap (though see [bugs](#Bugs) regarding one of the white cap patches).

In the first chamber, a cairn emanating magical energy is surrounded by the dead bodies of three [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"): [Agrius](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrius "Skyrim:Agrius"), [Raen](/wiki/Skyrim:Raen "Skyrim:Raen"), and [Vidgrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidgrod "Skyrim:Vidgrod"). Next to the cairn and the three bandit corpses are three bedrolls. On a nearby pedestal is *[Agrius's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Agrius's Journal")*, which tells the bandits' story, and the [key to Halldir's Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Halldir%27s_Crypt "Skyrim:Key to Halldir's Crypt"), which unlocks the nearby adept-locked iron door, permitting further adventure into the cairn.

*Agrius's Journal*

Just past the door, there is a stone bowl on the floor containing an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). The corridor ends in a wooden spiral staircase, with a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") at the bottom. At the top, the corridor continues to the south into a flooded section, past a stone table on the left. On the sideboard to the left of the table is another empty random soul gem and a set of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"). Continue right past a burial urn on the left and two bookcases; an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") is farther along to the right. Two ghosts will appear and attack you just in front of an adept-locked wooden door. The crypt key will open this door as well.

Through the door are three thrones, one in front, and one to each side of you. A melee and magic-user ghost attack as soon as you enter. The path forks north and south here, with the north fork having a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") in the dead end to your right. There is a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") in an alcove, and behind the spike wall is a broken table with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on top.

The path continues to the south past a sideboard with two empty soul gems on top, then turns to the west and past some [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") that are fairly difficult to avoid and will alert a melee ghost ahead. To the right as you continue down the path is a broken sideboard with a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") on top. Around the corner to the left is a dead end containing a slumbering draugr that will be alerted by any fighting, lying in an alcove with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground. To the right up the staircase is an archer ghost standing next to a plinth holding a *[Spell Tome: Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Raise Zombie")*.

A draugr on a throne

Continue past the plinth to see a draugr sitting on a throne. There is an urn on the left-hand side of the path; just past it is another draugr in an alcove. Two burial urns flank the throne, to the left is a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") leaning against the wall, and in the northwest corner are two [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") that can be looted. The path to the east is blocked by a gate that can be opened with the lever behind the throne. Just before the gate, to the right is a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") stuck in the rubble.

Symbol totems

Through the gate, ascend a short flight of stairs to a small catacomb. To the left at the top of the stairs, you can see a small room with loot, but cannot reach it yet. Instead, turn right into the catacombs. It consists of four rooms in a square. The starting room contains a lever, and each of the other rooms has a [symbol totem](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Symbol "Skyrim:Spinning Symbol") with a symbol on the opposite wall. The "eagle" room contains two ghosts, with a medium coin purse on the ground. The "whale" room contains a large coin purse, a leveled filled soul gem, and a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") on shelves in small alcoves. The "snake" room contains a slumbering draugr standing in an alcove to the right of an iron door, and a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") and random gauntlets on a sideboard under the symbols of the snake. To the south is an apprentice-locked iron door behind which is an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a random shield, and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka").

To progress, simply match the symbols and pillars, then pull the lever in the starting room. A rotating gate will open the way to a natural cavern with many fungi growing and a pool of water, in which can be found a medium coin purse and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Continue down the path heading west to more catacombs, where two ghosts will attack. Farther to the west is an urn. The path to the left here leads to the area seen previously, but beware of the [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"). The treasure consists of a random warhammer and helmet, a filled random soul gem, a random healing potion, two burial urns, and a chest with an adept [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that sets off a [flamethrower statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") behind you.

Approaching Halldir

Retrace your steps to stairs heading north to continue onward. Once you pass through the gate at the top, it will close, blocking your retreat. Halldir himself is a powerful draugr caster, who uses several [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells. He'll begin to speak in an ancient [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") tongue as you start to take away his health. At about 66% health, he will disappear and split into three different elemental versions of himself. All three are casters, and are spread out enough to make this part rather difficult; as such, [magic resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") is recommended. The cold and fire casters are close to the room's entrance, while the lightning version is over by the throne at the back of the room. His [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball") spell can cause massive damage. Once you have defeated his three clones, he will rematerialize back in the room, ready to be killed.

Once he has been defeated, make sure you loot his remains and also claim his [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Staff "Skyrim:Halldir's Staff") from the floor (see [bugs](#Bugs)). To the right of his throne is a boss chest. To the left of the entrance is a sideboard with a random pair of gauntlets; on the right sideboard is a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). In the northeast corner of the room, you can find a burial urn, helm, armor, and warhammer (all random) on a table, and a medium coin purse and an urn on the bookshelves. The shelves in the southeast corner of the room contain an empty random soul gem, with another burial urn in the rubble to the right of the shelves. Finally, in the center of the room is a trapdoor that can be opened by activating it directly. It is above the cairn in the first chamber, which is now reduced to a pile of rubble.

## Notes

- Halldir's clones are kept in a small room unconnected to the rest of the dungeon. You can see them by using the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") in the first chamber of the dungeon. If you happen to kill Halldir before he summons his clones, you can still reach them by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and typing `tcl`, then "flying" into their room. The clones can then be killed and looted.

## Bugs

- If not taken, the journal and key on the pedestal may disappear after the magical cairn collapses.
- One or more of the three named bandit corpses may disappear after the magical cairn collapses.
- One of the white cap patches in the catacombs cannot be harvested.
- Sometimes the puzzle totems will not activate.
  - This can be fixed by reloading a save or exiting and reentering the dungeon.
- Picking up Rjorn's Drum before you receive the related quest may render it unable to be completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Halldir's Staff duplicates when you kill him. It is possible to find one copy on the ground and another on his remains.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- You may be given a quest by the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear this location. However, some enemies may spawn out of reach outside the walls.
  - They may be killed by using the Aura Whisper shout in the first open chamber, then using [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spells when looking through the wall closest to the auras to summon creatures able to destroy the enemies.
  -  The console command `killall` may be used to kill the enemies. Halldir's clones will then be able to spawn in the hidden room, thus activating Halldir.
- The ghosts here incorrectly drop physical loot instead of ghost loot like all the other ghosts in the game.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.4, fixes this bug.
  - Halldir himself will not be flagged this way due to his dropping unique loot that would otherwise be lost.
- If [Trouble in Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Trouble_in_Skyrim "Skyrim:Trouble in Skyrim") sends you here, it's possible it will have selected the wrong actor as the "leader".
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.6, addresses this issue. A brute force solution was created to force the alternate draugr boss into the quest's alias so that you'll get credit for killing the right one.
- At times, invisible ghosts will appear. They can detect you, causing the eye to open when sneaking, while seemingly no one is there. The option to talk to them can appear when hovering over them, you can pickpocket them (they have nothing in their inventory), and when attacked, they respond like regular ghosts do. When killed, they will drop ghostly remains. This happens e. g. when you pass the bone chimes shortly after the first 4 ghosts and manage not to trigger them. It seems that triggering some loud objects will then make the ghosts appear.

# Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp

## Overview

Halted Stream Camp

**Halted Stream Camp** is a small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It contains only one zone, *[Halted Stream Camp](#Halted_Stream_Camp)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Ups and downs of poaching

The camp is surrounded by a palisade wall, with the north side protected by a rocky hill. There is a gap in the palisade to the east with a rope strung set of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") blocking quiet access. There is also an unlocked gate in the south wall. The bandits are poaching and butchering [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") here as evidenced by a shack with a mammoth's skeleton. Four bandits keep watch over the camp, using raised platforms around the perimeter. One is on a raised platform to the south with an additional four [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") in a bucket, one sits on a bench next to the campfire, one sits on a chair on a raised platform to the southwest and the final one is normally on the highest level above the main entrance to the mine, to the north. On this level is also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and two barrels with two [woodcutter's axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against them.

Entering through the eastern gap there is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") on your right and a ramp up to the first platform on your left with an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") underneath. In front of you is the shack used for butchering their kills. The shack only has a wall to the west with the other three completely open. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") by the wall and to the right is a long wooden table. On the table is a mead barrel, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [mammoth snout](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Snout "Skyrim:Mammoth Snout") and a wooden plate with [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). There are several mammoth bones in the shack and hanging from the eastern roof strut is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

To the north of the shack is the campfire with two benches around it. To the west is the second much larger platform. This platform has a ramp that leads to a junction with a barrel and several sacks, turning left over a bridge to a lookout point and to the right, up some steps to the highest level. The mine entrance is on your right at the bottom of the ramp and under the ramp is an apprentice-trapped chest and two barrels; on one of these are two potions, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a leveled potion of health. The potions don't seem to respawn. The [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") activates a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace").

### Halted Stream Camp

A bandit mining an ore vein

Upon entering, a well-lit wide tunnel leads down to the north. There is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [falling boulder](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap about half way down before reaching the first [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). There is a crate on your right with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") on top of it. To your left is a cart containing three [mammoth tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") and a mammoth snout and growing beside it is a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus. Ahead you will see a bandit mining who carries a [key to Halted Stream Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Halted_Stream_Mine "Skyrim:Key to Halted Stream Mine"). In this area there is a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and another fly amanita growing on either side of a tunnel that is blocked by a novice-locked gate that can be unlocked by using the mine key obtained from the bandit. The tunnel heads farther down to the east. To the right of the gate is a stack of barrels and crates with a pickaxe on top. There are two more iron ore veins on the ground and one at the end on the wall, a barrel with a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on top and a table holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a potion of minor healing.

Descending through this much narrower tunnel will take you past a total of six iron ore veins, one on each wall and three on the ground. Past a bleeding crown fungus and a fly amanita fungus you come to the top of a wooden structure with a path to the right descending down a ramp to the mine floor. There is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a large pile of sacks along the edge in front of you and on your left is a string of bone chimes hanging from the ceiling and a bench. Following the path to the right, on your right is a long wooden table. On the table is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a lockpick, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a potion of minor stamina, a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random potion, two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of Nord mead and a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*. To the left of the table are more sacks, another barrel, a bench with a coin purse on the ledge behind it, and an iron ore vein on the wall. The ramp down heads to the northeast.

Oily mine

At the bottom there is an iron ore vein on your right and a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") on your left, with a set of shelves beside it containing five mammoth tusks and three mammoth snouts. A small square wooden table is beside the shelves and has a copy of the key for this mine. Behind this is a hidden area with an empty set of shelves on your right and a corridor under a wooden structure with barrels and crates along the length and a novice-locked chest against the south wall of the mine. To the north of the hidden area is a tanning rack, and at its entrance is a coin purse. Two bandits can be heard having a short conversation:

**Bandit #1**: *"Gotta have a sharp axe to cut through all that fat..."*
**Bandit #2**: *"Hurry up with it, we've got a merchant in the pit to take care of after we carve this thing up."*

To the north is a raised area with a ramp. At the top of the ramp on the left is a single bed, a boss level chest and a large pile of sacks. At the foot of the bed on the wall is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). Against the north wall of the mine is a long wooden table containing a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), two bottles of alto wine, a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a potion of minor healing, a random potion, an iron dagger, two bottles of Nord mead, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a large coin purse, a copy of *[Report: Disaster at Ionith](/wiki/Skyrim:Report:_Disaster_at_Ionith "Skyrim:Report: Disaster at Ionith")* and a *[Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Transmute_Mineral_Ore "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore")*. To the east, against the wall is a dresser with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top and a set of shelves containing a copy of *[The Ransom of Zarek](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ransom_of_Zarek "Skyrim:The Ransom of Zarek")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")* and *[The Cake and the Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*. There is also a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), three pieces of iron ore, a bottle of alto wine, a random potion and a potion of strength in the area.

Underneath the raised area, to the right of the ramp is an iron ore vein. In the middle of the room is a dead [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") next to a grindstone. The mammoth can be harvested for another snout. There is an oil pool on the floor, and there are [oil lantern traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") strung all over the ceiling.

Mammoth ram

There is a tunnel to the southeast with two iron ore veins on your immediate left. There are two fly amanita fungi in the tunnel. Be careful as this tunnel is full of a variety of traps. There is a pressure plate that activates a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") trap made from the skull of a mammoth, a string of bone chimes hanging from the ceiling, a bear trap on the ground on the left and an oil lantern trap that is activated by a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire"). Farther toward the exit is a third iron ore vein on your left.

Do you get the point?

The exit takes you outside to a [spike pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit") with several mammoth bones, three coin purses (one large, one medium, and one small), a dead [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf_(NPC) "Skyrim:High Elf (NPC)"), and a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer").

## Notes

- The [Poacher's Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Poacher%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Poacher's Axe") can be found on one of the bandits in the mine. It can be used to chop wood and has a unique enchantment. If you don't pick it up during your first visit, the axe will respawn with the rest of the dungeon.
- A mammoth tusk for [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") or [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") can be found here, as the bandits have already killed several mammoths using the nearby pit traps. There are five tusks in the main chamber and three on a cart in the first hallway.
- The first bandit may be seen sitting in a chair next to mine entrance instead of mining.
- It is possible (with a bit of care to not to land on the spikes) to enter the mine via the pit trap, thus allowing you to explore the location in reverse.
- Killing the bandit boss clears the camp, but you may wish to avoid this, as it will force a 30-day waiting period for the ore veins to respawn. If you leave the boss alive, you can visit the mines every ten days for more iron ore, making the camp a prolific source of iron ore. Some quests that send you here only require an item to be retrieved, which can still be done without killing the boss, though the target chest is beside the boss.
- The spike pit is a good place to practice the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill, as you can lower your health quickly in a more controlled environment than in combat.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this dungeon is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Bugs

- Attempting to fast travel from the pit trap may cause the game to crash.
- Sometimes, the ore veins will respawn, but the bandits won't.
- The placement of one of the iron ore veins here can result in the camera colliding with the mammoth skull trap.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.
