Halted Stream Camp

**Halted Stream Camp** is a small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It contains only one zone, *[Halted Stream Camp](#Halted_Stream_Camp)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Ups and downs of poaching

The camp is surrounded by a palisade wall, with the north side protected by a rocky hill. There is a gap in the palisade to the east with a rope strung set of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") blocking quiet access. There is also an unlocked gate in the south wall. The bandits are poaching and butchering [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") here as evidenced by a shack with a mammoth's skeleton. Four bandits keep watch over the camp, using raised platforms around the perimeter. One is on a raised platform to the south with an additional four [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") in a bucket, one sits on a bench next to the campfire, one sits on a chair on a raised platform to the southwest and the final one is normally on the highest level above the main entrance to the mine, to the north. On this level is also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and two barrels with two [woodcutter's axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against them.

Entering through the eastern gap there is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") on your right and a ramp up to the first platform on your left with an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") underneath. In front of you is the shack used for butchering their kills. The shack only has a wall to the west with the other three completely open. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") by the wall and to the right is a long wooden table. On the table is a mead barrel, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [mammoth snout](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Snout "Skyrim:Mammoth Snout") and a wooden plate with [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). There are several mammoth bones in the shack and hanging from the eastern roof strut is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

To the north of the shack is the campfire with two benches around it. To the west is the second much larger platform. This platform has a ramp that leads to a junction with a barrel and several sacks, turning left over a bridge to a lookout point and to the right, up some steps to the highest level. The mine entrance is on your right at the bottom of the ramp and under the ramp is an apprentice-trapped chest and two barrels; on one of these are two potions, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a leveled potion of health. The potions don't seem to respawn. The [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") activates a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace").

### Halted Stream Camp

A bandit mining an ore vein

Upon entering, a well-lit wide tunnel leads down to the north. There is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [falling boulder](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap about half way down before reaching the first [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). There is a crate on your right with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") on top of it. To your left is a cart containing three [mammoth tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") and a mammoth snout and growing beside it is a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus. Ahead you will see a bandit mining who carries a [key to Halted Stream Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Halted_Stream_Mine "Skyrim:Key to Halted Stream Mine"). In this area there is a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and another fly amanita growing on either side of a tunnel that is blocked by a novice-locked gate that can be unlocked by using the mine key obtained from the bandit. The tunnel heads farther down to the east. To the right of the gate is a stack of barrels and crates with a pickaxe on top. There are two more iron ore veins on the ground and one at the end on the wall, a barrel with a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on top and a table holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a potion of minor healing.

Descending through this much narrower tunnel will take you past a total of six iron ore veins, one on each wall and three on the ground. Past a bleeding crown fungus and a fly amanita fungus you come to the top of a wooden structure with a path to the right descending down a ramp to the mine floor. There is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a large pile of sacks along the edge in front of you and on your left is a string of bone chimes hanging from the ceiling and a bench. Following the path to the right, on your right is a long wooden table. On the table is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a lockpick, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a potion of minor stamina, a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random potion, two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of Nord mead and a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*. To the left of the table are more sacks, another barrel, a bench with a coin purse on the ledge behind it, and an iron ore vein on the wall. The ramp down heads to the northeast.

Oily mine

At the bottom there is an iron ore vein on your right and a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") on your left, with a set of shelves beside it containing five mammoth tusks and three mammoth snouts. A small square wooden table is beside the shelves and has a copy of the key for this mine. Behind this is a hidden area with an empty set of shelves on your right and a corridor under a wooden structure with barrels and crates along the length and a novice-locked chest against the south wall of the mine. To the north of the hidden area is a tanning rack, and at its entrance is a coin purse. Two bandits can be heard having a short conversation:

**Bandit #1**: *"Gotta have a sharp axe to cut through all that fat..."*
**Bandit #2**: *"Hurry up with it, we've got a merchant in the pit to take care of after we carve this thing up."*

To the north is a raised area with a ramp. At the top of the ramp on the left is a single bed, a boss level chest and a large pile of sacks. At the foot of the bed on the wall is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). Against the north wall of the mine is a long wooden table containing a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), two bottles of alto wine, a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a potion of minor healing, a random potion, an iron dagger, two bottles of Nord mead, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a large coin purse, a copy of *[Report: Disaster at Ionith](/wiki/Skyrim:Report:_Disaster_at_Ionith "Skyrim:Report: Disaster at Ionith")* and a *[Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Transmute_Mineral_Ore "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore")*. To the east, against the wall is a dresser with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top and a set of shelves containing a copy of *[The Ransom of Zarek](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ransom_of_Zarek "Skyrim:The Ransom of Zarek")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")* and *[The Cake and the Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*. There is also a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), three pieces of iron ore, a bottle of alto wine, a random potion and a potion of strength in the area.

Underneath the raised area, to the right of the ramp is an iron ore vein. In the middle of the room is a dead [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") next to a grindstone. The mammoth can be harvested for another snout. There is an oil pool on the floor, and there are [oil lantern traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") strung all over the ceiling.

Mammoth ram

There is a tunnel to the southeast with two iron ore veins on your immediate left. There are two fly amanita fungi in the tunnel. Be careful as this tunnel is full of a variety of traps. There is a pressure plate that activates a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") trap made from the skull of a mammoth, a string of bone chimes hanging from the ceiling, a bear trap on the ground on the left and an oil lantern trap that is activated by a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire"). Farther toward the exit is a third iron ore vein on your left.

Do you get the point?

The exit takes you outside to a [spike pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit") with several mammoth bones, three coin purses (one large, one medium, and one small), a dead [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf_(NPC) "Skyrim:High Elf (NPC)"), and a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer").

## Notes

- The [Poacher's Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Poacher%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Poacher's Axe") can be found on one of the bandits in the mine. It can be used to chop wood and has a unique enchantment. If you don't pick it up during your first visit, the axe will respawn with the rest of the dungeon.
- A mammoth tusk for [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") or [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") can be found here, as the bandits have already killed several mammoths using the nearby pit traps. There are five tusks in the main chamber and three on a cart in the first hallway.
- The first bandit may be seen sitting in a chair next to mine entrance instead of mining.
- It is possible (with a bit of care to not to land on the spikes) to enter the mine via the pit trap, thus allowing you to explore the location in reverse.
- Killing the bandit boss clears the camp, but you may wish to avoid this, as it will force a 30-day waiting period for the ore veins to respawn. If you leave the boss alive, you can visit the mines every ten days for more iron ore, making the camp a prolific source of iron ore. Some quests that send you here only require an item to be retrieved, which can still be done without killing the boss, though the target chest is beside the boss.
- The spike pit is a good place to practice the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill, as you can lower your health quickly in a more controlled environment than in combat.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this dungeon is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Bugs

- Attempting to fast travel from the pit trap may cause the game to crash.
- Sometimes, the ore veins will respawn, but the bandits won't.
- The placement of one of the iron ore veins here can result in the camera colliding with the mammoth skull trap.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest

## Overview

Hamvirs Rest

**Hamvir's Rest** is a small outdoor graveyard and [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr").

## Walkthrough

The graveyard is just north of [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"). Three skeletons patrol the area, and a draugr sleeps in the upright sarcophagus. A master-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is beside the sarcophagus, with a random enchanted [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") behind the grates to its left. Eight [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants, two [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and two [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants grow among the tombstones and in the immediate area.

This is the final destination of the [Headless Horseman](/wiki/Skyrim:Headless_Horseman "Skyrim:Headless Horseman") on his nightly travels; once he reaches this area, he will disappear regardless of the time of day.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is west-southwest of the ruin.

# Skyrim:Hard Answers

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") |
| Location(s): | [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") |
| Reward: | [Nightingale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Blade "Skyrim:Nightingale Blade") |
| ID: | TG06 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Speaking with Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence") | **Next →** [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Speaking with Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence") | | → Next | [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") | | |

The Falmer language inscribed on a tablet

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") at [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") or [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment").
2. Speak to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep").
3. Enter the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum").
4. Copy the Falmer Translation Guide.
5. Bring the copy of the Guide to Enthir.
6. Speak to [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") in The Frozen Hearth.

## Detailed Walkthrough

First go speak with [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") at [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). After speaking with Enthir, you'll be directed to the wizard [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") at [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

:   *Note:* There is a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers#Bugs "Skyrim:Hard Answers") that prevents you from talking to Enthir if you have started but not completed the quests [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") or [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus"), as Enthir believes Winterhold to be in danger and will continually repeat *"This is going to be terrible for business."*

### Calcelmo, the Wizard

You can find Calcelmo overseeing the excavation site in Understone Keep. He's not happy to be disturbed and no matter what you choose to do, will not be interested in helping you translate the journal—at best, he will grant you access to his museum. You have several options on how to proceed:

- You can go straight to the museum and pick the lock.
  - Using this method causes the guards in the museum to be hostile, and as they are city guards you will incur a bounty if you kill them.
- You can simply steal his key, which should be right next to him on the table.
  - This option will cause the guards to be hostile, unless you are successfully hidden.
- If you ask to visit the archaeological site, you will be asked to kill [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe") (a giant frostbite spider). After you have done this task you will be given the key to the museum, and can walk past the city guards without sneaking.
- Solving Calcelmo's love problems during [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") will add additional dialogue where he will hand over the key to the museum, and allow you passage (the guard at the door will still tell you you can't enter, but the guards in the museum won't bother you).
- If you can pass a hard [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech"), you can persuade him to give you the key to the museum.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Even after slaying your troublesome spider? | I've already provided you a key to the museum. You should consider it an honor. Few are allowed to browse my collection. I'm sorry, but that's as far as my generosity extends. | | | | No progress |
| Even after everything I did for you and Faleen? | Well, I'm not blind to the fact that you've been instrumental in improving my affairs of the heart. If you wish, you may enter my tower to view the museum section, but I'm afraid the laboratories are still off limits. That's the best I can offer. | | | | No progress |
| But I'm a great admirer of your work. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: What kind of a mentor would I be if I denied a potential student a glimpse at his master's ingenuity! Here, this key will provide access to my museum. Feel free to browse for as long as you wish. However, I must insist that my laboratory remains strictly off limits. **Failed**: While I appreciate the sentiment, I still have to decline. Being an admirer, I'm sure you can appreciate the need to keep my research a secret. | | | | **Passed**: Get the key **Failed**: Nothing |
| What will it cost to change your mind? **(Bribe)** | **Failed**: I'm not certain how many scholars you're accustomed to dealing with, but I can assure you that personal wealth is our lowest priority. | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |
| Grant me access or you'll regret it. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: Do you realize that at a snap of my fingers I can bring the entire Markarth city guard to my defense? You best rethink this course of action or you may find yourself on the executioner's block. | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |
| Forget it. Maybe I'll come back later. | Very well. Perhaps when my research is complete, I'll feel more comfortable discussing my findings with you. | | | | Nothing |

### Enter the Museum

Whatever you chose to do, it's clear you're going to have to break into Calcelmo's laboratory in order to retrieve the Falmer Translation Guide, so head for the Dwemer Museum. There are a lot of random Dwemer artifacts and books in the museum, but most notably, there is a gate on the south side protecting a room containing an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem")—the gem is located on a table to your right as you enter the first room on the left. Make your way to the far end of the museum to find the entrance to Calcelmo's Laboratory. As you enter the lab, you can find the [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod") in the room to the left, which you can use to help clear out the guards ahead (note that the rod only works in the lab).

There are two types of guards in the museum and laboratory: [Markarth City guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") and Calcelmo's personal guards. The city guards here will not be hostile (provided you didn't pick the Museum lock), but Calcelmo's personal guards in the lab will confront you if they spot you, no matter what (though they will not give you a bounty if they are harmed). It's possible to sneak past all the guards in the lab without any combat, but you can also employ the various traps around the lab to dispatch them quickly. Whatever you choose, make your way to the end of the laboratory.

As you make your way through, beware the hall with the poison gas; your health will drain rapidly until you reach the other side, and it is not possible to prevent the damage with poison resistances, even with items such as [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(item) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (item)"). Putting 40 pounds of weight (either the body of a dead guard or a heavy item such as [Dwarven armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven Armor")) on the pressure plate at either end of the hall will depress the plate and stop the gas from spreading, allowing you to comfortably loot the corpses. You can also [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") and not suffer the poison for the duration of the shout (though be warned, this may alert nearby guards). The poison gas hall can be avoided entirely by taking a different higher route eastwards.

At the end of the lab, you'll find [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar")'s study, where Calcelmo's nephew is busy with his research. Activating the trap here will send Aicantar into a panic and he and his guards will make a run for it (or you can just sneak past him). Near the exit, you can find the [Dwemer Puzzle Cube](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Puzzle_Cube "Skyrim:Dwemer Puzzle Cube") for [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny") quest. Exit out onto the Wizard's Balcony and head up the stairs to the right into Calcelmo's Tower. In the tower, follow the hall to the left to find a room with a desk. Beyond the room is the Falmer Translation Guide, which turns out to be a massive stone tablet. There's no way you're taking the whole thing back to Enthir, so grab a piece of charcoal and paper from the previous room and use them to create a rubbing of the tablet.

### Return to Enthir

After you copy the text, two [Wizards' Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Wizards%27_Guard "Skyrim:Wizards' Guard"), [Captain Aquilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aquilius "Skyrim:Captain Aquilius"), and Aicantar will enter the tower to hunt you down. You may fight them if you wish, but you can also simply sneak past them after they split up. Distracting the remaining guard with an arrow is a good way to aid a stealthy approach. For the quickest escape, look towards the exit from the tablet and you'll notice a small ledge on either side of the wall over the door. Move from behind the tablet onto the platform to your left, then jump onto the little "chimney" at the end of the platform. From there, you can jump onto the small ledge and proceed directly to the door.

Once outside, a waypoint will indicate your exit route: simply hug the right wall of the balcony to find a gap leading to a small cliffside path, terminating at a waterfall. Carefully jump into the pool at the base of the waterfall to complete your escape. It's also possible to "climb" down from the balcony by looking left and down when you reach the waterfall—there will be a path of sorts where you can make very small drops to multiple rocks (you can use Become Ethereal to avoid damage with either method). Alternatively, you can retrace your steps back through the museum and exit the keep the same way you came in.

Once you've escaped, return to Winterhold, where Karliah and Enthir are waiting in the cellar of the Frozen Hearth. Enthir will use the rubbing of Calcelmo's tablet to translate Gallus's journal, confirming that [Mercer](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") used the Guild's funds and desecrated the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher"), the secret shrine to [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal") that the [Nightingales](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales") are sworn to protect. Karliah will also give you the [Nightingale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Blade "Skyrim:Nightingale Blade") as a token of appreciation, and ask that you meet her at [the Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). After talking with Enthir and Karliah, the quest ends and [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") begins.

:   *Note:* Completing this quest will lock the back door from [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s graveyard to [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern") until later in the next quest.

## Guild Trinket

The trinket in this quest is the [Dwemer Puzzle Cube](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Puzzle_Cube "Skyrim:Dwemer Puzzle Cube"). It can be found in the Calcelmo's Laboratory zone, in the room where [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") is reading. The Cube is on a table to the right, after going past Aicantar's table but before the door to the balcony. Once you've collected the trinket, it can be returned to Delvin Mallory for some leveled gold.

## Notes

- After successfully creating the rubbing, just before the guards storm the laboratory, [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to the platform across from the level with the stone tablet. Casting [Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)") here, or using a potion, enables you to scale the scaffolding all the way over their heads, eliminating the need to sneak around or fight them. You have to do this quickly, within a second or two of them entering or they might notice where you are.
- The highest level version of the Nightingale Blade is untemperable (levels 46+), making the level 36-45 blade the best version. However, all versions lack a [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") perk, so they will quickly fall behind other swords when you start tempering.
- If you kill [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") prior to creating the rubbing, he will not arrive alongside the guards and the captain. Instead, there will be one extra guard in his place.
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") reveals at least one NPC who could conceivably translate the Falmer language, but doesn't add a way to ask him to do so.
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* states that you receive [Gallus's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Journal") upon quest completion. However, this is incorrect, and said item cannot be obtained under normal circumstances.

## Bugs

- It is possible to obtain two copies of the museum key. If you proceed with the bribe/persuade dialogue options, Calcelmo will give you the first key. However, this doesn't disable the dialogue about killing Nimhe, which allows you to receive another key upon completion.
- You can exit the dialogue right after Persuade speech check before advancing quest stage. Therefore it can be repeated for leveling Speech up. **?**
- Picking up the museum key after the quest has finished restarts the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- The quest item flag on [Gallus's Encoded Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal") is not cleared on completion of the quest, leaving it permanently stuck in your inventory.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  -  Enter the [console command](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") `player.removeitem CEDA6 1` after completing the quest.
- Enthir may be stuck saying *"This is going to be terrible for business"* if the quests [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") or [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") are active. Both of these quests may have to be completed in order to talk to him.
  - Another possible solution is to leave and wait for normal store hours when Enthir opens for business.
  - Sometimes leaving the building and reentering will get his correct dialogue running. His dialogue changing to a store (fence) shows his script has been completed and he is out of the picture for this quest.
- In Calcelmo's Lab, there may be a Markarth city guard who gives you a bounty regardless of your standing towards the Reach faction. All talk options except going to prison or fighting fail. The only way you will be able to get rid of this bounty is by gaining another bounty in another city and going to jail.
  - A possible workaround is to sneak into the room with the guard and use a bow to kill him. Even if he is running towards you, it seems if you kill him before he starts his formal dialogue, the bounty is not added and you can play on as normal.
  - Another possible workaround is to remain hidden and kill the guard by activating the traps.
- Calcelmo's Tower is supposed to unlock during this quest but doesn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Karliah sometimes returns to Snow Veil Sanctum without giving you the following quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - This seems to have to do with having Mercer's plans in your inventory. This is an important quest item for the next quest and the quest fails to load as long as this item is in your inventory. You should drop the plans somewhere and retrieve them when you want to finish The Pursuit. Use command `Startquest TG07` then `Set stage TG07 0` to start and add the quest to the journal while keeping Mercer's plan, when they're "quest items" and it doesn't allow you to get rid of them.

## Quest Stages

| Hard Answers (TG06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Karliah believes the only proof that could expose Mercer's treachery can be found within the pages of Gallus's journal which she recovered from Snow Veil Sanctum. Unfortunately, the journal is written in some sort of code that needs to be deciphered. Our only hope is Enthir, one of Karliah and Gallus's former acquaintances who is a wizard at the College of Winterhold. *Objective 10:* Speak with Enthir |
| 20 |  | Enthir has informed me that Gallus's Journal is written in Falmer. He's directed me to seek out Calcelmo, the Court Wizard in Markarth who is the foremost authority on them in hopes of obtaining a translation. *Objective 20:* Speak with Calcelmo |
| 25 |  | *Objective 25:* Gain entry to Calcelmo's Museum  *Objective 27:* (Optional) Obtain the key to Calcelmo's Museum |
| 30 |  | Calcelmo has proven to be extremely stubborn and refuses to allow me access to his materials regarding the Falmer language. I'm left with little choice other than taking matters into my own hands and stealing his notes. *Objective 30:* Obtain Calcelmo's Falmer Translating Guide |
| 40 |  | Calcelmo's "notes" on the Falmer language are actually derived from a massive stone slab in his tower! It will be impossible to bring this item to Enthir to have him translate Gallus's Journal. I'll have to discover a way to make the information more portable. *Objective 40:* Duplicate the writing on Calcelmo's Stone |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Return to Enthir |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Speak to Enthir |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Speak to Karliah |
| 200 | ☑ | After Enthir successfully translated Gallus's journal, I've discovered that Mercer's motivations transcended simple greed or murder. As a member of the Nightingales, Mercer was tasked with guarding a place called The Twilight Sepulcher, the Temple of Nocturnal. According to Gallus, he defiled the temple and betrayed the Thieves Guild. Karliah insists we bring this information to Brynjolf immediately. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 27, 55.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG06`.

# Skyrim:Harmugstahl

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Harmugstahl ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Harmugstahl)) | | |

Harmugstahl

**Harmugstahl** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing the warlock [Kornalus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kornalus "Skyrim:Kornalus") and his enchanted [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). It contains only one zone, *[Harmugstahl](#Harmugstahl)*.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance is up a flight of stone stairs marked by a lit brazier at the foot of the stairs, with the wooden entrance door at the top. The stairs lead up from a path that links [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt") across the confluence of two tributaries of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") to the northeast with [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") to the west-northwest and [Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater") to the southwest (the latter two locations reached via spurs from the main path). The only part of the fort visible from the outside is this entrance; the rest is buried under a cliff face. A lit brazier can be seen on your right near the bottom of the stairs. Another one can be seen on your left at the top of the stairs.

### Harmugstahl

The entrance leads into a natural tunnel leading to the first chamber, which is lit by two lit braziers and candles. As you approach, you will hear the voice of an [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer#Adventurer1 "Skyrim:Adventurer") and sounds of a battle. In the chamber you will find the adventurer finishing off an enchanted frostbite spider. He will spot you even if you are sneaking, and start a conversation with you. After you ask him what was going on with the spiders, he will say: *"I don't know, but this place is full of them. Every one I've encountered has been enchanted or the like. Look, I'm getting out of here. Normally, spiders make my skin crawl, but magic spiders? Blech."* He will then promptly leave. If you talk to him before he leaves, he will say *"Is there anything more revolting than spiders? Too many legs..."*

The chamber contains two further dead frostbite spiders, which when harvested will briefly be surrounded with magical flames similar to a cloak effect. To the south is a corridor, which after a few paces turns east and descends a flight of stairs. At the bottom, the passageway continues south, passing some food barrels on the right before leading into a room. There is a balcony on the right which you cannot reach due to the stairs having collapsed; this will be your way out later. To the left as you enter is a set of spears blocking a corridor, with the lever which lowers them on the left. On your right, against the north wall is a set of shelves holding a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") among some clutter, and in the southwestern corner is a wooden table with another dead spider, which also has the enchantment, a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire") on top.

Past the spears, the passage leads to a cavernous chamber containing little of interest except four levers in front of another passage blocked by spears with a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") growing to the right of them. Once you lower all four of the upright spears, the remaining jumble behind will retract. To lower the spears, start by facing the passage; from the left, pull lever 1 and wait until the two spikes on the left descend, then pull lever 4 and the gate will open. There are no negative repercussions for moving them in an incorrect order.

Beyond the spears, the passage continues south. As you reach a turning to the east, there are numerous human bones in an alcove, and you can hear a spider moving about ahead. To the east is a flight of stairs ascending before the passage turns south again. Shortly thereafter, there's another turn to the west, and after a few paces more, the passage opens into another room. As you enter, there are two sets of shelves on your right holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"). There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") on your left, with a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_(Harmugstahl) "Skyrim:Journal (Harmugstahl)") on top, which describes the results of experiments carried out on the frostbite spiders. There is also a large hole in the south wall and a wooden table in the southwestern corner holding a dead spider and a [potion of resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock"), with a potion of resist fire on the floor nearby (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Against the west wall is a bookcase holding five common books, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and a cheap plate under a candle. To the right of this is a level-locked wooden door on the north wall.

Behind the door is a smaller room containing the frostbite spider you heard, some food barrels on the right, and in the northwestern corner, an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). There are two sets of shelves in the northeastern corner holding rare [glazed candles](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Glazed_Candles "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"), a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*, two common books, four resist element potions (one of shock, two of fire, and one of [cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold")), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), two [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flowers, a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and two sprigs of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear").

As you pass through the hole to the south into a larger room, a frostbite spider will descend from the ceiling, and two more will be released from small, barred cells. There are five small cells in this room, with three in a row against the south wall and two opposite against the north wall. The middle cell on the south wall has had its bars bent and broken, and contains an egg sac containing a [spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), a random shield, and a standing dessicated corpse in the opposite corner behind some webbing. In the third southern cell are the remains of a frostbite spider. The other three cells are now empty. To the west is a doorway that is blocked by thick cobwebs, and in front on the ground is a dessicated corpse that can be looted. Burn or chop your way through the webbing to continue. There is a pickaxe on the ground by a turn to the north, and at the end an ascending flight of stairs. At the top, there is a cave-in to the east, a cupboard holding a woodcutter's axe opposite, several barrels to the left, and more stairs rising to the west. At the top, the passage continues, passing a long wooden table holding a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and another [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), before turning north and ending with a closed door.

Through the door is a balcony overlooking the main room where you will encounter the mage who has been completing the experiments on the frostbite spiders. As soon as you enter, you will overhear him talking to himself. The experimenter, Kornalus, is standing to the right of a cell containing three frostbite spiders. On the balcony, in front of you is an unlocked chest and some barrels with a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on top. There are stairs leading down to the right. Either attack Kornalus directly, or sneak down to pull the lever on the outer corner pillar of the cell. This releases the spiders, which will then proceed to attack Kornalus. The spiders will not generally cause him much of a problem, but will provide a distraction for you. There is a doorway in the middle of the north wall and a table to the right with a dead spider on top.

Through the doorway is a short corridor with a level-locked door opposite leading to Kornalus's quarters and a pair of double doors to the east that requires a key. Both of these doors can be opened using the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Kornalus_Frey%27s_Key "Skyrim:Kornalus Frey's Key") carried by Kornalus. Through the level-locked door is a flight of stairs that lead up to his quarters, which contain an unowned single bed coming out from the north wall and a dresser to the left containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a [shrine of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrine of Julianos") on top. This grants the [blessing of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Blessing of Julianos"), a 25-point bonus to the amount of magicka you have for the next seven hours. Against the east wall is an unlocked boss level chest, while opposite is a wooden table with a dead spider, a basket containing five spider eggs, a potion of resist cold, and a potion of resist fire on top. To the right is a set of shelves holding another dead spider on top, three more spider eggs, a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), and two bowls of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts").

Through the double doors back in the corridor is a room containing two giant frostbite spiders. However, they are too big to fit through the door, so they can be killed with ranged attacks. There is a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") behind the second of three spider egg sacs on the north wall of the room, just inside the doorway through which you entered. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is in the southeastern corner, near the foot of some stairs. These lead up to a doorway onto the balcony previously passed near the entrance. Before dropping down, there is a chest straight ahead beside a table holding only clutter on the left. Exit the same way you came in.

## Notes

- Looting the spider corpses in the area will initiate a brief elemental effect (fire, frost, or shock) on the corpse. The effect does not seem to harm you.
- If [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") is with you when you meet the adventurer at the entrance, Barbas may attack and kill the adventurer.
- After the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") is completed, a dead [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") may spawn outside in front of the fort when the area respawns, providing you with free hagraven loot. She may have been tossed over the mountain by the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") that reclaimed nearby Dragontooth Crater.

## Bugs

- When in the room with three caged frostbite spiders, if you attack them through the bars and a kill animation initiates, you can end up behind the cage bars with no way out, or the spiders could end up outside the cage with you.
  - If you end up trapped inside the cage, use the console command `tcl` to move through the gate.
- When entering the cave in [Werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form") or [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form, the adventurer will talk to you and leave as normal, and you will be able to talk to him as normal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to take the potion of resist fire from the table near the alchemy lab.
  - Click on the potion from the console, then enter `disable` followed by `enable`.
- The spike puzzle may not work at all (the spikes don't move whatsoever). This may prevent you from completing any quests here.
  - Try reloading or, if that doesn't work, leaving and re-entering the cave, or jump through (see next bug).
- When in the room with the four levers, it is possible to jump past the bars between the wall and the far left bar. This is a solution if the four levers do not work.

Kjar wants you to teach someone a lesson

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which will send you to one of the following bandit camps: [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"), [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"), [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post"), [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp"), [Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") onboard his ship at the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks.
2. Travel to the random location and kill the bandit leader.
3. Return to Kjar for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar"), ship master of The North Wind currently anchored at the docks in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), will ask you to hunt down and kill a runaway crew member. The sailor had formed a group of bandits, who are currently hiding out in one of seven random locations. Travel to the location and kill the bandit leader there. Return to Kjar, who will give you a year's salary (a leveled gold reward).

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- The quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader") can have identical quest objectives.

## Bugs

- This quest is known to generate the boss NPC prior to actually getting it from Kjar, which would result in you killing the boss NPC and then being told to return to someone you never visited.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If you have completed the mission and later reenter the same location once it is repopulated, it can give you the completion again, allowing you to collect a bounty for re-killing the rogue crewman.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The bandit boss is prematurely made available to kill before Kjar actually offers the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.
- If you are sent to Uttering Hills Cave, and have already completed [Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), you will be unable to complete this quest, as the bandit leader is replaced by [Linwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe "Skyrim:Linwe") and the former is nowhere to be seen.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  -  You can return the cave to its previous occupants by typing `prid c5675` in the console, followed by `disable`.
  -  You can still progress through the quest by typing `"c5688".kill` in the console.
  -  You can progress through the quest by typing `SetStage FreeFormShipsWindhelm 15` in the console.
- Oddly, since the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") is marked as being owned by the Winterhold crime faction, once you finish the quest, you will have helped someone in the hold, allowing you take things from the longhouse without it being considered theft.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19319)) Kjar is now part of the Eastmarch crime faction, and a new faction was created specifically for the residents of the longhouse in order to set ownership correctly.

## Quest Stages

| Harsh Master (FreeformShipsWindhelm) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the leader of <Alias=BanditCamp> |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to Kjar |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformShipsWindhelm stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformShipsWindhelm`.

The Harstrad River headwaters

**Harstrad River** is a river in northern [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). A cave can be found at the [Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad").

For more information, see the [lore page](/wiki/Lore:Harstrad_River "Lore:Harstrad River").

# Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Clearing.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Clearing.png) | Clearing: Headwaters of Harstrad ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Headwaters+of+Harstrad)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2HarstradCave01, DLC2HeadwatersofHarstradExterior01, DLC2HeadwatersofHarstradExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") Northeast of [Snowclad Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowclad_Ruins "Skyrim:Snowclad Ruins") | |

Headwaters of Harstrad

The **Headwaters of Harstrad** are the source of the [Harstrad River](/wiki/Skyrim:Harstrad_River "Skyrim:Harstrad River").

It can be found a short distance downhill to the southeast from the entrance to [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"), or by following the river upstream from the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone") to the west-southwest.

## Related Quests

- **[Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House")**: Help [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") repair the tower of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

## Exterior

The cave entrance is found behind the waterfall cascading down a rock face just below the entrance to Benkongerike. On the bank as you approach the waterfall is a leveled [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") that will attack as soon as it detects you. There is a [pearl oyster](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") next to a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") downstream on the south shore, another on the north shore just before you reach the first large rock that is partially in the water and a third can be found underwater on the river bed between these two.

## Harstrad Cave

Headwaters of Harstrad

The entrance places you in a naturally lit, shallowly flooded cave, with a rock pillar directly in front of you. There is a waterfall descending the wall to the southeast, and a leveled spriggan standing on a raised area to the right of you, which will attack as soon as you are detected. At the top of the dry bank on the right is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") in front of an unlocked boss level chest. If you are here as part of the relevant quest, you may activate the headwaters by looking at and "activating" the shallow pool. There is nothing else of interest in the cave.

# Skyrim:Healing a House

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") repair the tower of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") |
| Location(s): | [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"), [Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad") |
| Reward: | Two [leveled potions of well-being](#Reward) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren")) |
| ID: | DLC2TTF2 |
| Suggested Level: | 25 |

The withered part of Tel Mithryn tower

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").
2. Find three [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") and bring them to the [Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad").
3. Return to Elynea and plant the taproots in the tower of Tel Mithryn.
4. Receive your reward from Elynea.

### Elynea Mothren

The founder of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"), the eccentric and bossy [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") is rumored to be a nightmare to work for. When you visit [the apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary") you will find an unhappy proprietor, [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren"), wandering around badmouthing Neloth: *"That ash eating wizard is always on me about his tower. It's not my damn fault the thing withered overnight."* She then explains the problem. Apparently, something went wrong inside [the tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") and Neloth wants it fixed right away and will have no qualms firing Elenya if that can speed things up. When asked what she needs she will say: *"Three [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") soaked in the headwaters of the Harstrad river. I'm an old woman. I can't possibly make that trip. It's way too dangerous. If you get some taproots, I'll pay you to dip them in the headwaters and bring them to me."*

### Hunting for Taproot

A map marker for the Headwaters of Harstrad will be added once you talk to Elynea, but two taproots can be acquired there, so you only need one. On Solstheim, taproots can be found in the following locations:

- Elynea herself may have some (15% chance).
- Two samples are found near the [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") inside [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- There are three samples inside [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm") in Raven Rock.
- On an unmarked island north of [Frossel](/wiki/Skyrim:Frossel "Skyrim:Frossel") you will find three [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), all of them carrying taproot.

Once you have at least one taproot, travel to the headwaters, which are hidden between [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") and the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone").

**Note**: A bug fix in the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") allows spriggans to have either taproots or [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), so neither the headwaters nor the unmarked island are guaranteed locations of taproot.

### Headwaters of Harstrad

A Spriggan Matron in Harstrad Cave

The Headwaters of Harstrad is a small landmark and consists of a waterfall that empties into a small lake. There will be a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") of some type here, either alive and on the shore near the lake, or dead and floating around in the lake. Kill the spriggan if needed, claim the taproot from the body, then dive headfirst into the waterfall and enter the hidden cave [Harstrad Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Harstrad_Cave "Skyrim:Harstrad Cave"). Once inside, you will immediately be attacked by another spriggan, so dispose of it and claim the taproot if you need it. After the battle, the Headwaters will activate so follow the map marker and soak three taproots in the water. Before you leave, make sure to search the boss-leveled chest for some extra goodies, then return to Tel Mithryn.

### Healing a House

The new room in Tel Mithryn

Back in the apothecary, Elynea Mothren will be quite happy when you tell her the mission is accomplished. Hand her the three soaked taproots and she will, surprisingly, keep two samples for herself, saying: *"I'll just keep two of them for myself. No need for Neloth to know. Take that last taproot and plant it into the wall of the withered house."*

Head over to the [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") where Neloth will wander around and complain as always. Find the withered area in the northwestern part of the laboratory and plant the taproot in it. Return to Elynea Mothren for a reaction and a small reward: *"Good. Now maybe Neloth will get off my back about it. I suppose you think you should get paid for helping an old woman. Here. Take these. I'll sell you more if you come back later."* She will then hand you two [leveled potions of well-being](#Reward). You are also free to take most of the ingredients displayed in her shop for free. Lastly, pay a visit to the tower where Neloth has built an entire new room, a testing area for [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), complete with two trapped spriggans in cages. Back in the apothecary, Elynea will also have [a new job](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_and_Gathering "Skyrim:Hunting and Gathering") for you.

### Reward

| Level | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 1-7 | [Potion of Minor Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Well-being") |
| 8-15 | [Potion of Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Well-being") |
| 16-23 | [Potion of Plentiful Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Well-being") |
| 24-31 | [Potion of Vigorous Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Well-being") |
| 32-39 | [Potion of Extreme Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Well-being") |
| 40+ | [Potion of Ultimate Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Well-being") |

## Bugs

- You may not be able to soak the taproot in the headwaters.
  -  Use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and enter the following commands (replacing xx with the [mod ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")):

    ```
    player.additem xx01aad6 3
    setstage DLC2TTF2 200
    ```
  -  When playing on PS4 with the Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch (USSEP) installed, temporarily deactivating the USSEP and reloading the game can fix the issue.
  -  v4.3.6b (2025-12-29) Fixed for PS4/PS5 users by Vexona.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTF2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTF2`.

# Skyrim:Heart of Crimson

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked* |

| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Started by reading *[Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Tyra_Blood-Fire "Skyrim:Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire")* |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| Reward: | Set of [enchanted Ebony plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate_Items#Ebony_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate Items"); ability to craft [Ebony plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Ebony Plate Armor") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE063\_Quest, ccBGSSSE063\_MiscQuest |

| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate") |

The leader of the Crimson Dirks is ready to face you

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Wait for a courier to deliver the *[Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Tyra_Blood-Fire "Skyrim:Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire")*.
2. Speak with the [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(person) "Skyrim:Beggar (person)") at [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks.
3. Confront [Tyra](/wiki/Skyrim:Tyra_Blood-Fire "Skyrim:Tyra Blood-Fire") at the shrine of Talos southwest of Windhelm.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Once you've reached level 32, head to a settlement and a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will deliver the *[Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Tyra_Blood-Fire "Skyrim:Letter from Tyra Blood-Fire")*. It is addressed to you personally, from a notorious leader of a bandit gang named [Tyra Blood-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tyra_Blood-Fire "Skyrim:Tyra Blood-Fire"). Her gang has disbanded, and she now seeks the judgment of the Divines to atone for her past crimes. She believes that facing you in combat is the only way to receive this divine judgment, but first you must prove your character to her.

The letter instructs you to go to the docks in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and give alms to a local [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(person) "Skyrim:Beggar (person)"). He sits on a mat down the end of the docks, near the [East Empire Company offices](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)"). You will have the option to give him 1 gold, 100 gold, some [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), or to give him nothing and pray for his prosperity. Your choice is irrelevant, as you will be given the opportunity to face Tyra no matter which option you choose.

With this done, you will be directed to a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") southwest of Windhelm, at the top of a small mountain overlooking the bridge next to the [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=128799&y=24553&zoom=17&legacy=true). Tyra is praying there, and as promised she will be hostile upon your approach. She is a dangerous enemy, as she possesses a full set of [Ebony Plate Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Ebony Plate Armor") bearing powerful enchantments and dual wields two [ebony swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Sword "Skyrim:Ebony Sword") in combat. Defeat her and loot her corpse for the valuable enchanted set of armor; with this quest completed, you will begin to find Ebony Plate items as random loot throughout Skyrim. You can also loot her for a single [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v1 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v1")* explaining her origins, and a letter titled *[To (Player)](/wiki/Skyrim:To_(Player) "Skyrim:To (Player)")*. The contents of this final letter is dependent on the choice you made when speaking with the beggar.

The letter received has 5 different middle parts.

Prayer for the Beggar - "You chose to pray for the beggar, putting your faith in the Divines. After all, maybe it isn't food or water people need, but hope in something greater than themselves. But the world is not a place where hope alone will save you. My advice to you is to seize your destiny. Don't wait for an idle god. Then you'll be a worthy judge and executioner for your enemies, just as you were for me."

Give 1 gold - "You gave the beggar a single septim. I like the amount. you did what you could without placing a burden on yourself. and yet, on its own a single piece does nothing for him. It's only when the entire town does their part, each one placing a septim, that the beggar has enough to eat. So my advice to you is to remember the value of company. Whether you're a bandit or a hero, no one can do it alone. You have to work together, one gold piece at a time, to do what needs to be done."

Give 100 Gold - "You gave the beggar a full purse of gold. You're someone who goes above and beyond, putting the lives of others above your own. But not even a thousand septims can save the life of every man, woman, and child. So my advice to you is to not fall victim to your kindness. There are people like me who will take advantage of it. And there are times when you'll have to make a hard decision for the greater gain. Save who you can, but do what you must."

Give Bread - "You gave the beggar bread, a choice I agree with. Gold can be wasted. Wine can be a poison. But a meal can never be squandered. Perhaps if I had been given a similar gift, my life would have been different. As such, I deem you a worthy judge. Hopefully you will be a swift executioner. Either way, I thank you."

Give Wine - "You gave the beggar wine. It'll help him forget his troubles; give him a reprieve. But such gifts can quickly sour. Come morning, the beggar may regret your choice, or worse yet, he might repeat it. So my advice to you is to view every action in its entirety. Only then can you make your choices with clear eyes."

## Notes

- When giving the beggar alms, wines include [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Food"), [Argonian Bloodwine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Argonian_Bloodwine "Skyrim:Food")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), [Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Food"), [Surilie Brothers Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Surilie_Brothers_Wine "Skyrim:Food")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Wine "Skyrim:Food").

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE063_Quest, ccBGSSSE063_MiscQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE063_Quest, ccBGSSSE063_MiscQuest`.

# Skyrim:Heart of Gold

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Get Mila a pet goldfish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | 1 Gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_WhiterunPartOne |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") | **Next →** [No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest"), [Two of a Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Two_of_a_Kind "Skyrim:Two of a Kind") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") | | → Next | [No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest"), [Two of a Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Two_of_a_Kind "Skyrim:Two of a Kind") | | |

The pet goldfish

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Bounty: Goldfish!](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Goldfish! "Skyrim:Bounty: Goldfish!")*.
2. Obtain a goldfish for [Mila Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Mila_Valentia "Skyrim:Mila Valentia") in Whiterun.
3. Speak to Mila Valentia.
4. Follow Mila Valentia.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can be started after [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"You're headed to Whiterun. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Goldfish! "Skyrim:Bounty: Goldfish!") from Mila requesting a goldfish. Once you have obtained a goldfish, head to Whiterun and speak to Mila:

:   **I heard that you'd like a pet goldfish. What do you think of this one?**
:   *"Could I keep him? Please?"*
:   **Sure. Here you go.**
:   *"You're the best! Thanks!"*

You will then have to follow Mila to her house, where she will place the goldfish in a trough of water. She will then reward you with 1 gold.

## Notes

- Making a full loop around [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond"), southwest of Windhelm, can net you 3-6 Goldfish. If none are present, wait an hour and dive back in.
- Three Goldfish spawn in the pond located outside of [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") which is only a short distance from Whiterun, making this an easy option for completing the quest.
- After you give Mila the Goldfish, it's possible that she will wander around Whiterun, following her mother all day. Or it could happen that she doesn't snap out of her playing, if you told her about the Goldfish while she was playing catch with the other kids. If you don't want to wait use the console: `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_WhiterunPartOne 40` then talk to her to finish the quest. On PS4, try disabling immersive citizen AI mods and reloading.
- If the quest does not move forward once you give the goldfish, you might want to attack Mila with the Bow of Shadows equipped to help advance the quest.

## Quest Stages

| 20 |  | I brought Mila a goldfish. I should follow her to make sure she's going to take care of it. *Objective 40:* Follow Mila |

| 200 | ☑ | I gave Mila a goldfish. She seemed very happy with her new pet. In exchange, she handed me a single septim. It's not much, but at least I helped brighten a child's day. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_WhiterunPartOne stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_WhiterunPartOne`.
