# Skyrim:Heart Stones

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") |
| Location(s): | [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") |
| Reward: | 250 gold |
| ID: | DLC2TTR2 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Any time after speaking to Neloth during [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") except when finding him a new steward | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Any time after speaking to Neloth during [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") except when finding him a new steward | | |

A Heart Stone Deposit

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
2. Find a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") deposit on the southern coastline of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").
3. Return to Neloth for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

If you ask Neloth if he needs help with his research, he may ask to buy a Heart Stone from you. If you have one on you, you can simply sell it to him. Otherwise, they can be mined from [deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") nearby. He will reward you with 250 gold.

## Notes

- This quest is radiant, and may be completed multiple times, particularly at low levels.

| 200 |  | *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ |  |

- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR2`.

# Skyrim:Heartwood Mill

## Overview

Heartwood Mill

**Heartwood Mill** is a struggling lumber mill on the shores of [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich"), west of [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate").

The mill is run by [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta") and her husband [Leifnarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifnarr "Skyrim:Leifnarr"), although Leifnarr has disappeared leaving her to run it by herself. She lives here with her young son [Gralnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Gralnach "Skyrim:Gralnach") who helps as much as he is able.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta")  [Gralnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Gralnach "Skyrim:Gralnach") | | | [Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") | | --- | | [Rift Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Guard "Skyrim:Rift Guard") | |

## Related Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Flight or Fight](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_or_Fight "Skyrim:Flight or Fight")**: Help [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta") at Heartwood Mill locate her missing husband.

### Exterior

A [Rift Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Guard "Skyrim:Rift Guard") patrols into the mill and towards the bridge keeping them safe. There is a [chicken coop](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") with two nests outside of the house, a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") and many mountain flowers that can be found in the immediate area. Between the house and saw mill is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") and a bucket containing a [Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod"), a [Blue Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing"), and three [Orange Dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") can be found here. Fish from [Temperate Lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is just south of here.

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  4 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  4 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg")  1 [Birds' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") |

### Heartwood Mill

It is a small single story house consisting of a main living room and a single bedroom. Entrance leads straight into the living area with a set of shelves to the left, against the east wall holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several pieces of cheese. In the southeastern corner is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel, a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") is to the right, along the south wall, with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top. A small square wooden table with two chairs in the southwestern corner holds a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a loaf of bread and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Under the table is a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). Against the west wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, with a wall shelf to the right holding clutter. Hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). The door to the bedroom is on the north wall.

The bedroom contains two single owned beds, one in the southeastern corner and the other in the northwestern corner. There is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the left of the first bed and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the floor between them. To the right of the second bed is a food barrel with a copy of *[Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Hagravens "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens")*. Against the north wall is a fireplace.

## Notes

- You can buy [sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") here after installing [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") by speaking to [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta"). You can also cut your own for free if she has given permission to do so.
- Version 1.2.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") adds a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") here.

## Bugs

- Some nodes in the mill's exterior may not be grounded properly which can likely contribute to Grosta and Gralnach being unable to enter and/or exit their home consistently.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

Heimskr's House

**Heimskr's House** is a small house in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by the priest [Heimskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr"). It is located beside the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree, between [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") and the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"). It consists of one area, *[Heimskr's House](#Heimskr.27s_House)*.

During the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") rubble lands in front of the house, making it impossible to access the house for the rest of the game. Heimskr will then be forced to move to a small camp near Jorrvaskr, or be thrown into jail if you sided with the Imperials.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Heimskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr") |

## Heimskr's House

Inside Heimskr's house

The house is small and bare-bones, although four chairs facing a homemade podium on the northwestern wall suggest that Heimskr doesn't only preach near the Gildergreen outside. Next to the chairs is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), while a total of five [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") can be found near the front door. To the southeast is Heimskr's bedroom which contains a chest with a few gold coins and a small dinner table dressed with some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a [potion of vigorous magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Magicka"). The owned bed stands along the northeastern wall, while a dresser with [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") has a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and a [potent lingering poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potent_Lingering_Poison "Skyrim:Potent Lingering Poison") on top. There are a total of four human skulls decorating his shelves and floors with no explanation given.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Heimskr's House") to which is carried by Heimskr.
- There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the right of the entrance door, even though the Thieves Guild [considers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") his house to be a wealthy house. The house will not be empty if you are sent here on one of [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex")'s thievery jobs.

## Bugs

- If given a Thieves Guild radiant mission with Heimskr's house as your target location after the Battle of Whiterun, it will be impossible to complete the objective due to his house being inaccessible.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - You may simply return to the quest giver and quit the current job without any penalties.
  -  Another possible fix is to type `coc WhiterunHeimskrsHouse` into the console to get teleported inside Heimskr's House. To get back outside, you can simply use the door of the house.

# Skyrim:Hela's Folly

## Overview

Hela's Folly, shipwreck and campsite

**Hela's Folly** is a [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") northeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). The fast travel point is just to the south of the bow of the wreck. The camp is a few paces to the west-southwest.

[Salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") and [Arctic Chars](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Arctic Char")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") can be found swimming in the waters here.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus")**: Slay an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus") looting a shipwreck.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Hela's Folly

Deekus' campsite

There is a makeshift camp next to the wreck which is the home of an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") named [Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus"). Everything in the camp is marked as owned and is counted as stealing if taken, even after you kill him. The camp consists of a lean-to, beneath which are a bedroll, a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue"), and an open crate containing two [amethysts](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), and a filled [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). To the right of the lean-to is a novice-locked chest "protected" by two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap")—one in front and one behind. There are three crates between the chest and a campfire, which has three [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") [cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") over it. To the north is another crate with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an amethyst, and an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald") on top. There are two barrels by the crate, and on top of one of them are a [soul gem fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment") and a sapphire. On the shore, to the east of the wreck is a [clam](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") that can be harvested for [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat").

Another chest can be found underwater in the northwest part of the ship. There are also several gems underwater, almost directly underneath the chest. This includes one [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") and one sapphire on the lower deck of the submerged half, between some crates near a plant.

## Notes

- If you are sent here to retrieve the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold") for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl_Korir "Skyrim:Jarl Korir"), it will be in the chest owned by Deekus, and thus considered theft. Korir will still accept it to complete the quest, however.

## Bugs

- You can become stuck between rocks and the wrecked ship just a few paces forward from the fast-travel spawning point. **?**
  - Fast-traveling back to Hela's Folly seems to fix this.

Helgen Keep

**Helgen Keep** is a keep used to escape [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") in the aftermath of the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack. There is a single interior zone to the keep: *[Helgen Keep](#Helgen_Keep)*.

During [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), you must escape a dragon attack on the town of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") by making your way through the keep and its subterranean caves.

After Helgen is abandoned, the town and keep become inhabited by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.

### Helgen Keep

Tower

There are two entrances to the keep, one enters the barracks and the other enters the base of the tower. There is a small difference depending on who you followed into the keep. If you followed Hadvar into the barracks there will be two living Stormcloak soldiers (a male and a female) to the right of the entry from the tower, and the corpse of [Gunjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunjar "Skyrim:Gunjar") by a table to your left. The male Stormcloak is equipped with a two-handed iron weapon, and the female is equipped with either another two-handed iron weapon or a one-handed iron weapon and a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"); they both wear a [Stormcloak cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Cuirass "Skyrim:Stormcloak Cuirass"), [fur boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Boots "Skyrim:Fur Boots"), and [fur gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Fur Gauntlets"). Gunjar has an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and wears the same clothes minus the gauntlets. If you follow Ralof the two living Stormcloaks will be replaced by an Imperial soldier and an [Imperial captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Captain "Skyrim:Imperial Captain") who rush in from the barracks. The captain carries the [Helgen Keep key](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep_Key "Skyrim:Helgen Keep Key"), needed for a locked gate, and is equipped with an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She wears a set of heavy [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"), including [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots") and [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers"), and she wears an [Imperial officer's helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Officer%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Officer's Helmet"). The soldier is equipped with the same weapons, but wears [studded Imperial light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Imperial Armor") and standard light [Imperial boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Light Bracers"), and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet").

Barracks

The barracks are the easternmost section of the keep. There are four beds by the eastern wall and two dining sections by the western wall. There are two chests by the beds, one is empty and the other holds an [Imperial light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet") and some gold. In the northwest corner of the room there is a long table with two chairs, and two sets of shelves. On the table are four gold coins and a copy of *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")* and under the table is a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")*, which is inaccessible. The southwest part of the room holds two round small tables—one with one chair and the other with two—two weapon racks, a set of shelves, and the warden's chest. Each weapon rack holds an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and the chest contains another iron sword, [Imperial light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"), [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"), and a Helgen Keep key. There are two bottles of wine on the set of shelves, a bottle of standard [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a bottle of [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). There is a pull chain to the right of the corridor that activates a wooden gate to the corridor, and another again to the right that opens the gate to the tower.

Kitchen

There is a locked gate to the west leading further into the keep. Through the gate is a cart with two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). To the right is a bench with two sacks to the side of it. To the left is a set of stairs winding down further into the tower. After following the corridor until it becomes a dead-end, there is a door to the left leading to a kitchen. There are two soldiers in here. Hanging from the center pillar are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and two leaves of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Hanging in front of the fireplace is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the right of the fireplace is a [kettle pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Kettle "Skyrim:Kettle") with three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") in it. On the other side of the center pillar is a small round table with a bottle of Alto wine.

Opposite the entrance is a large dining table with two chairs. Around the table are three sets of shelves. Among the utensils on the table is a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a bottle of Alto wine. On the left-hand shelves is a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). On the right-hand shelves is a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a bottle of wine.

Through the connecting archway is a storage area. There is a barrel to the left that contains five potions, three of minor healing, one of minor magicka, and one of minor stamina. There are three sacks underneath the overhanging shelf, and another on the other side of the steps up to that shelf. There is a table to the right with a salt pile and a potion of minor healing. Above that hang two more rabbits. Just in front of the table is a basket with four [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). The door by your companion leads to a corridor going down further into the keep.

Torture Room

The next room is a torture room. The [Torturer](/wiki/Skyrim:Torturer "Skyrim:Torturer") and [Torturer's Assistant](/wiki/Skyrim:Torturer%27s_Assistant "Skyrim:Torturer's Assistant") can be found here in combat with two Stormcloak soldiers. Against the far wall are three novice-locked cells. The side ones are empty and the middle one contains a dead [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage "Skyrim:Mage"), who carries 25 gold pieces, two potions of minor magicka, a [novice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Hood "Skyrim:Novice Hood"), and [novice robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Robes "Skyrim:Novice Robes"). Alongside him in the cell are four gold pieces, another potion of minor magicka and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Sparks "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Sparks").

By the second of the center pillars is a small table with a knapsack, an iron dagger, and a copy of *[The Book of the Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_the_Dragonborn "Skyrim:The Book of the Dragonborn")*. The knapsack contains four lockpicks and a potion of minor healing. In the northeast corner of the room is the torturers cell. It contains a weapon rack and a long L-shaped shelf that has two lockpicks and a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")* on the southern half. There is an iron mace hanging on the rack, an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") lying beside it, and a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")* under the shelf by the door.

The exit to the room is in the northwest corner, and along the corridor are four prison cells—two on each side. The first on the right is open and empty, as is the second on the left. The first on the left is novice-locked but empty, and the second on the right is novice-locked and contains minor loot—a lootable skeleton and a coin purse. The corridor leads to another torture chamber, though this one is in considerably worse condition, having massive cobwebs in the corners and along the edges. There are two hanging cells to the left, one with a skeleton, the other with a dead Stormcloak soldier. There are another two hanging cells to the right of the entrance, but only one is occupied with a skeleton. There is a third skeleton in-between these two, by two disused hanging cells on the ground.

Caves

The way forward is through the broken wall and into the natural caves that have been utilized by the Legion as a hidden entrance to Helgen. The first room is guarded by five soldiers, one across the mini-bridge, two in the sunken middle area, and two archers on the far side of the room. The archers are equipped with [long bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and also stand over an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"), which can be ignited using the spell [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"). After that there is a raised wooden bridge blocking the way. There is a lever just before it to the right to lower it.

Once the bridge has been lowered and crossed it will collapse under some falling rocks. A tunnel is revealed and it leads to a small stream. On the opposite bank is a skeleton, and beside that is a coin purse and a potion of minor healing. The stream leads back to the same room that the normal route was taking; it joins with another stream and flows through another tunnel. The room is empty of any loot. A short distance along the next tunnel it turns right as the stream flows under some rocks. The remains of a skeleton can be seen on a ledge along with a coin purse.

The tunnel shows signs of what is in the next room, [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). There are three spiders around the room and two larger spiders descend from holes in the ceiling as you enter the room. There are two web sacs around the area where the spiders are, and a dessicated corpse hanging to the right. There are a total of seven egg sacs around the room containing [spiders eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"). On a ledge to the left of the entrance is an iron mace by the remnants of a corpse.

There is a tunnel to the east that leads back to the stream which has re-emerged from the rocks. There is a lit brazier across the stream on a ledge. By it is a potion of health and an iron dagger. Back on the path there is a cart with three bottles of Alto wine and a coin purse, and on the ground behind it, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). In the gloom to the south is a uniquely weak [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). If you manage to get above the bear and on top of the area overlooking it, you'll find a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") on the fallen tree trunk. There is nothing else of interest to find. The exit is along a winding path to the southeast.

### Bandits

There are a number of minor differences once the bandits take over. Any loot missed before will still be there as the area does not respawn.

- **Kitchen**: two bandits sitting at the big table.
- **Torture room**: it has been redesigned as a bar, with the torturer's cell acting as the bar itself. A bandit occupies the cell and another patrols the next corridor. On the shelf in the cell there is now an iron dagger, two lockpicks, a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*, two coin purses, a random potion, six bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arrow, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arrow,_v2 "Skyrim:The Black Arrow, v2")*.
- **Caves**: in the first room after the torture rooms are three bandits, one of whom is a bandit chief. The chief stands in the middle of the cave, near a chest, while the other two patrol the far walkway. The bandits have replaced the collapsed bridge with a permanent walkway, and another bandit sits on it. Finally, there is a frostbite spider near where the unique bear is.

## Notes

- The keep will be occupied by rival forces to whomever you followed into the keep, with the exception of the troops in the Torture room (they will always be the same with only the hostility transferred from one group to the other). If you chose [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") the troops will be [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), if you followed [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") they will be [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldiers.
- Though the Keep has a technical minimum level of 6, scripts prevent this being applied during Unbound. Instead most soldiers are, at a maximum, level 2, and most creatures are level 1. The minimum level does apply to the bandits that take over afterwards.

## Bugs

- A duplicated book on the barracks bookshelf is visible, but not accessible, due to chair and table placement.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. The table has been moved and the duplicate book replaced with one useful to a beginning player: *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")*.
- Gunjar's body doesn't disable with the other bodies.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- A third stormcloak (actually #1) was supposed to attack the torturer (and vice versa). Instead, it was "initially disabled" in the quest, causing various script lines to fail, and sometimes causing the whole scene to hang.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The bandits and items in the exterior area respawn despite being in a "no-respawn" zone.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Helgen

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Town.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Town.png) | Town: Helgen ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Helgen)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Helgen "Lore:Helgen")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | See [Notes](#Notes) |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Imperial Legion Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| HelgenExterior | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") North of [Greywater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Greywater_Grotto "Skyrim:Greywater Grotto") | |

Helgen before the dragon attack

**Helgen** is a [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in eastern [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold").

Helgen after the dragon attack

It is the location where you begin the game, as you are transported there to be executed. Largely run by the [Imperial military](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), the town features several fortified towers and buildings. Shortly after your arrival, the settlement comes under attack by the ancient [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"), and you are forced to escape through [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep").

If you return to the town after visiting [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), the ruins will be inhabited by a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.

## Notes

- During the introductory sequence before the initial quest [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") remembers [Vilod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilod "Skyrim:Vilod"), who used to make [mead with juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mead_with_Juniper_Berry "Skyrim:Mead with Juniper Berry"). If you later return to Helgen, bottles of this mead may be found on the second floor of the partly destroyed inn you jumped into during Unbound.
- Two additional residents are present during the introductory sequence; these unnamed NPCs are referenced only as `MQ101GenericCivilianNordMale` and `MQ101GenericCivilianNordFemale` in the game data. They're seen carrying firewood and a bucket inside the gate when the carriage enters town, but are never seen again.
- Helgen doesn't count as a discovered location, and therefore won't count toward the [Explorer](/wiki/Skyrim:Explorer "Skyrim:Explorer") achievement.
- Helgen is the default destination for bad AI targets, meaning that bugged NPCs may end up wandering nearby.
- Approximately halfway down the road to [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"), a small group of bandits has set up camp under an overhanging ledge. The bandits guard a novice-locked chest and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")*.
- The locked gate, bandits, barrels, chest, potions, mead bottles, Cast Iron Pot, Wooden Bowl, Kettle, Basket, Wooden Ladle and Tankard respawn; burnt corpses, the wardrobe, and the end table don't respawn.
- The double bed at the inn is considered “owned”; however, if you choose to escape Helgen with Hadvar, you will be allowed to sleep in the bed after becoming friends with his uncle Alvor.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays Helgen in its original state; the previous one displayed Helgen in its destroyed state.

## Bugs

- The mead with juniper berries isn't properly enabled during your arrival and will only appear upon your later return to Helgen.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- Vilod and Matlara are left alive after the dragon attack and can be seen wandering Helgen after its destruction.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- When [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar") is assigned as a Housecarl for [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor"), he may be found here instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Bandits, containers, and items don't have their encounter zone set and will respawn despite being in a "no reset" zone.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Town.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Town.png) | House: Heljarchen Hall ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Heljarchen+Hall+%28HF%29)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Heljarchen_Hall "Lore:Heljarchen Hall")) | | |
| Added by | [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BYOHHouse3Exterior | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm")  South of [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Heljarchen Hall

**Heljarchen Hall** is a piece of property in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), north of [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm") and south of [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad"). It is one of three potential homes available with the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on.

Heljarchen Hall as seen from the west

After installing Hearthfire, you may purchase this plot of land at [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). If [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") is still the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), speak with him; if Skald won't sell you the land, speak to [Bulfrek](/wiki/Skyrim:Bulfrek "Skyrim:Bulfrek"); if the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") has control of the hold, speak with the new jarl, [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis"). You will have to complete the quests [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") and [Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)") before being allowed to purchase land if Skald is jarl; the latter quest is not made available until level 22. Brina, however, will allow you to purchase land out of gratitude for your help in installing her. When you ask if you can buy a house in the hold, you will be told that there are no houses for sale at that time, but a new plot of land is available. It will cost 5,000 gold.

Your new property, Heljarchen Hall, will be marked as an undiscovered location on your map, located on the southern border of The Pale, where the northern mountains give way to the great plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). The property is southeast of the [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"); a short distance to the east is the giant camp [Blizzard Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard_Rest "Skyrim:Blizzard Rest"), and you can see [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") rising behind Loreius Farm to the south. It is also located almost directly over the central ruin in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

When you arrive on your new plot of land, you will find a drafting table, carpenter's bench, [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and chest on the outcropping on the south edge of the property; a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is a few feet beyond the chest to the south, in the outcropping itself. The "[Log Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")" is on the western border, and there are two [clay deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit"); one is south of the log pile, next to the wood chopping block, and the other is just a few feet south of the stone quarry.

You can begin [building](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") your home immediately, with materials provided in the chest when you first arrive. A unique feature at Heljarchen Hall is you have the option to build a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling"). Once built, the grain mill will appear along the house's western wall. It can be used to convert [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") into a [sack of flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour"). The hall's entrance will face Dragonsreach once construction begins, and standing on its steps will offer an impressive view of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").

Like the other player-built homes, you will have the option to expand onto your home with a [Main Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Hall "Skyrim:Main Hall"), cellar, and three wing additions. See [this page](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing_Options "Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing Options") for a list of pages detailing the furnishing options in each part of your home.

Should you become a [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale"), [Gregor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gregor "Skyrim:Gregor") will become your [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). He will move to Heljarchen Hall upon construction of the [small house](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_House_Layout "Skyrim:Small House Layout") layout.

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gregor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gregor "Skyrim:Gregor") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Markus](/wiki/Skyrim:Markus "Skyrim:Markus")  [Oriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Oriella "Skyrim:Oriella") |

## Related Quests

- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**: Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")**: [Construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a house for yourself.
- **[Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")**: Relieve the people of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") from [Vaermina](/wiki/Lore:Vaermina "Lore:Vaermina")'s curse.
- **[Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Notes

- Heljarchen Hall may be named after [Helarchen Creek](/wiki/Arena:Helarchen_Creek "Arena:Helarchen Creek"), a settlement located roughly in the area, which appeared in [Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena").
  - A village named Heljarchen, located in The Pale, was originally planned to be in the game but only [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") made it into in the finished game.
- [Adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") children sometimes remark *"Look at all the snow! I want to go sledding! Or skating!"* (girls) or "*It's so c-c-cold here! If I play outside for too long, I'm going to freeze solid!"* (boys)
  - For the reactions given by your spouse, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Spouse_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue").

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses, see the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- After purchasing the land and beginning construction, the house may not appear.
- When completing the Small House, a weapon may be removed from your inventory and placed in the chest inside the house. You can go inside the house and retrieve it. See the [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Heljarchen_Hall#Weapon_disappears_when_finishing_Small_House "Skyrim talk:Heljarchen Hall") for details. **?**
- If [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") is Jarl of Dawnstar, you may be ask her if Herjarchen Hall is still available, even if she hasn't mentioned it before.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- If a kitchen is built here, the chimney next to the fireplace may not appear outside.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.
- You cannot mount fish on either of the two fish plaques added by the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") if you have already done so in another house. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing#Bugs "Skyrim:Fishing") for details.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Helping Hand

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | **Help [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") cure her [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") addiction.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | Leveled unenchanted ring |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften12 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid") | | |

Lend a "helping hand."

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") about her job.
2. Give her a healing potion.

## Detailed Walkthrough

If you walk near [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta"), she will cry about losing her job and beg for help. Talk to her, and she will reveal that she has an addiction to [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") and that she wants to cure herself. She will ask for a healing potion in order to heal herself. If you probe further she will mention where she got the skooma from, *"I got mine off of a [merchant ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")"*, which ties in with another [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload").

You have three options: agree to give her a potion, agree to find one for her, or refuse to help. If you refuse to give her a potion, the option remains to agree to give her one. If you agree to give her a potion, the lowest type of standard healing potion (e.g. [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing")) in your inventory will be removed, and she will reward you with a leveled unenchanted ring while thanking you, *"Your kindness will never be forgotten"*.

Dialogue is closed at this point and the first part of the [next quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid") is immediately added to the miscellaneous quests.

## Notes

- Healing spells do not work and she does not recognize crafted healing potions. She can only take a standard healing potion.
- This is the first of three quests that are required to unlock the option to become [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") for [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") or [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"). There are additional requirements noted on that quest's page.
- Raising Wujeeta's disposition with this quest will allow you to freely take items from the fish barrels inside Riften Fishery and around the nearby fishing boats.

## Bugs

- Wujeeta is not essential, and if she dies before this quest and the next are complete, you cannot become Thane of the Rift unless the Imperials take control of the Rift, either through [negotiation](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or [force](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)").

## Quest Stages

| Helping Hand (FreeformRiften12) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Give Wujeeta a healing potion |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 25, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften12 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften12`.

# Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)

## Overview

Hendraheim

**Hendraheim** is a Nordic hall player home in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), north of [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine"). It lies west of [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge"), southwest of [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), and northeast of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt").

The interior layout, books on the shelves, and two of the [previous owner's](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydvina_Shield-Hearth "Skyrim:Eydvina Shield-Hearth") weapons reference [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk "Skyrim:Thirsk") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). Outside of the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons"), this is the one guaranteed place to find Nordic Weapons and certain books.

## Related Quests

- **[Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(quest) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim"): Earn the deed to an ancient Nordic hall.

### Exterior

- Small stables with multiple sacks and barrels.
- Multiple harvestable items hanging directly outside the door ([salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant")).
- Forge, smelter, workbench, grindstone, and wood chopping block near the rear of the home, accompanied by a chest and some barrels.

### Interior

Hendraheim interior

[(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")
The interior consists of two floors, a large open ground floor and a basement behind a door. On entering, weapon racks flank either side of the entrance. A raised level with rails runs along three sides of the room, with an armory area (mannequins, display cases, weapon plaques) to the right and a dining area (dining table with plates and food, and a hanging rack and shelves of food beyond). There is a single drawer on the right at the back of the room, if one wishes to use it.
Down the center, an alchemy table and arcane enchanter stand in the front right corner, with a cupboard that has shelves of ingredients and potions plus an empty drawer below.
On the left, stairs lead down to the trophy room cellar.
The center of the main room has a large flat square dais with no known purpose. Just beyond that is the cooking spit. In the right back corner is a bar counter, with sweet treats and beverages on the shelves behind it. In the right back corner is a baking area, including an open box with vegetables and a sack, another bar shelf, and the oven itself.

The back room is a small but well-furnished family bedroom. On the left is the children's area, with two owned beds and drawers plus a Child's Doll atop a chest. The back wall is taken up by a writing desk, with a Shrine of Akatosh on a shelf to the left. On the right are a Nordic burial urn and a bookcase. The right third of the room has a double bed with a bench at its foot, a shelf with drawers (named as "drawers"), and wardrobe closely packed into the space.

Several books come with the furnishings, such as [Thirsk, A Revised History](/wiki/Lore:Thirsk,_A_Revised_History "Lore:Thirsk, A Revised History").

The hall features a downstairs trophy room in the basement filled with display cases, mannequins, weapon racks, weapon plaques, and holders for various unique items. There are two sets of weapon racks on either side of you as you come in, and a total of twelve mannequins positioned around the room. On the left as you come in, there is shelving where you can display all ten [dragon claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Dragon Claw"). On the back wall you will find busts to hold all 14 [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask"). To the left of the busts are three weapon plaques, which belong to [Dragonbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbane "Skyrim:Dragonbane"), [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker") and the [Mace of Molag Bal](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_of_Molag_Bal "Skyrim:Mace of Molag Bal"). To the right are more plaques for holding the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade"), [Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:Rueful Axe"), and [Volendrung](/wiki/Skyrim:Volendrung "Skyrim:Volendrung"); beside them, against the righthand wall, are plaques for [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield"), and [Harkon's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Harkon%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Harkon's Sword"), and a single plaque above them for the [Dawnguard Rune Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Hammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Hammer"), [Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Shield"), and [Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Axe"). Further along the righthand wall is a set of shelves: the bottom shelf holds the [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer"), [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key"), [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key"), and the unique "[Kolbjorn Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Skull (Dragonborn)")"; the middle shelf holds the five [bugs in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"); and the top shelf has receptacles for the five [Paragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Unique_Items "Skyrim:Other Unique Items") from the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). Finally you will come to a display board for holding the [Dwarven Black Bow of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate"), [Champion's Cudgel](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Cudgel "Skyrim:Champion's Cudgel"), [Bloodskal Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Blade "Skyrim:Bloodskal Blade"), [Glass Bow of the Stag Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow_of_the_Stag_Prince "Skyrim:Glass Bow of the Stag Prince"), [Bloodscythe](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodscythe "Skyrim:Bloodscythe"), [Soulrender](/wiki/Skyrim:Soulrender "Skyrim:Soulrender"), and [Hoarfrost](/wiki/Skyrim:Hoarfrost "Skyrim:Hoarfrost"). Above it is a plaque for [Miraak's Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak%27s_Staff "Skyrim:Miraak's Staff") and [Miraak's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Miraak's Sword"). In the center of room lies several display cases on a set of drawers and a wooden divider; on the divider, you can place the [Shield of Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Ysgramor "Skyrim:Shield of Ysgramor") and [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad") on one side, and [Spellbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellbreaker "Skyrim:Spellbreaker"), the [Aetherial Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Shield "Skyrim:Aetherial Shield"), and the [Targe of the Blooded](/wiki/Skyrim:Targe_of_the_Blooded "Skyrim:Targe of the Blooded") on the other.

## Notes

- This location is the only one to make use of the wooden castle map icon, which is present but [unused](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#Unused_Map_Markers "Skyrim:Test Cells") in the base game. It was originally designed to be used by [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"), [the White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"), and the [Falkreath Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)").

## Bugs

- A fallen log clips into the wall behind the house.
- Items on top of the table right from the front door may fall off when the cell loads.
- Multiple weapon racks may not let you retrieve weapons once placed on them.
  -  Workaround: use the console to select the item on the rack and use `moveto player` to take the item from the frame and place it at the players feet.
  -  Workaround: use the console to turn collisions off, using `tcl` to toggle, and go around the other side of the wall to retrieve the weapon.
  - Workaround: dual wield daggers, position yourself so you are right in front of the weapon you want to retrieve. Aim your cursor right about where the four nails are on the rack and double power attack into the wall. While in the animation, mash the retrieve button and you should be able to get your weapon back.
- Some dragon claw racks may glitch and cause claw to place incorrectly, and sometimes sink towards the floor each time you enter the home.
- Placing some of the unique weapons on the plaques such as the Dawnguard Rune Hammer may cause them to disappear and be lost forever.
- Children and followers may refuse to enter the home.
- The Ebony Blade will not place correctly and will fall from the display every time you enter the house.
- If you place the Wooden Mask on its bust, remove it, leave the house, and replace it, it may disappear, not showing up on the bust or in your inventory. **?**
- The mannequins in the home may constantly cycle through idle animations, only stopping briefly when interacted with. **?**
- After putting items onto racks and plaques, the game will crash during the loading screen when attempting to re-enter the building.
- Putting armor on a certain mannequin, leaving and re-entering, moving the helmet to a different mannequin, and leaving and re-entering again, will result in the armor not only being on the mannequin you left it on, but also the original mannequin as well. No known workaround.
- Loading from a save, Hendraheim reloads as an enclosed stone box with only recently dropped loose items available for pick up, does not load on map, no items available, cannot exit or enter, nothing to interact with. Unknown resolution.

# Skyrim:Hendraheim (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Earn the deed to an [ancient Nordic hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") |
| Location(s): | [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)") |
| Reward: | Access to Hendraheim |
| ID: | ccEEJSSE004\_Quest |
| Required Level: | 10 |
| Added by: | [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim") |

Eydvina wishes for a true warrior's death

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a major city and await a delivery from a courier.
2. Read the [Warrior's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:Warrior's Challenge") and go to [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)").
3. Accept [Eydvina Shield-Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydvina_Shield-Hearth "Skyrim:Eydvina Shield-Hearth")'s challenge and loot the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Hendraheim "Skyrim:Key to Hendraheim") from her corpse.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You must await a courier's delivery when you reach level 10, likely within a hold capital, and read [the note](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:Warrior's Challenge") given to you. It will direct you to [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)"), an ancient Nordic warrior's hall marked on your map, which can be yours if you prove your worth in battle to the current owner. The hall is just north of [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine") and southwest of [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"). The climb is quite steep if approaching directly from the north, so it's advisable to approach from the Sungard side (climb the slope to the east, passing the Bilegulch Dragon Mound as you go, and circle around from the rear of the house to reach the front).

Once you arrive at the property, you will meet a rather unassuming Nord woman called [Eydvina Shield-Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydvina_Shield-Hearth "Skyrim:Eydvina Shield-Hearth") sweeping the stables. She is responsible for the challenge you have received, and will gear up for battle after a brief conversation. Kill her to claim the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Hendraheim "Skyrim:Key to Hendraheim") to the property. On her corpse you will also find a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydvina%27s_Note "Skyrim:Eydvina's Note") explaining her motivation for seeking a warrior's death in order to enter [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

Head inside the house to complete the quest and investigate your new [player home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses").

## Notes

- This quest originally started upon installation of the Hendraheim Creation, or upon exiting [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") after the tutorial. This was changed in an update on November 11, 2021.

## Quest Stages

| Hendraheim (ccEEJSSE004\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | Couriers often deliver notices to travelers across Skyrim. If I head to a major hold, perhaps I will receive information that may concern me. *Objective :* Await news from a courier |
| 10 |  | Couriers often deliver notices to travelers across Skyrim. I received one such letter and should read it to find out more. *Objective :* Read the Warrior's Challenge |
| 20 |  | I've received a letter regarding a warrior home nestled in the mountains north of Bilegulch Mine. The owner seems interested in bequeathing the home to me, but has first asked that I prove my worthiness in battle. *Objective :* Speak to the warrior at Hendraheim |
| 30 |  | I've received a letter regarding a warrior home nestled in the mountains north of Bilegulch Mine. The owner seems interested in bequeathing the home to me, but has first asked that I prove my worthiness in battle. *Objective :* Defeat the warrior |
| 40 |  | I received a letter regarding a warrior home nestled in the mountains north of Bilegulch Mine. I defeated the owner in single combat, and should now search her body for a key. *Objective :* Take the key to Hendraheim |
| 50 |  | I received a letter regarding a warrior home nestled in the mountains north of Bilegulch Mine. I defeated the owner in single combat and took the key to the house. *Objective :* Enter Hendraheim |
| 100 | ☑ | I received a letter regarding Hendraheim, a warrior home nestled in the mountains north of Bilegulch Mine. After defeating the owner in single combat, I took the key to the house and claimed it for myself. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEEJSSE004_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. # Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. Priest Drureth has a plan to gain more converts

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Receive this quest from [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") in [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear").
2. Get the *[Propaganda Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Propaganda_Letter "Skyrim:Propaganda Letter")* from [Priest Drureth](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Drureth "Skyrim:Priest Drureth").
3. Speak with [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi") and give her two hours to translate the letter.
4. Disseminate translated Propaganda Letters to the public.

### A Task for the Goddess

This quest is offered as part of the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)") quest if you choose to disguise yourself as [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan") before entering [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear"). Doing so will allow you to speak with the normally hostile [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan"). Offer to serve the Goddess Almalexia, and Drevlan will give you this quest along with [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware") and [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"). These quests are all optional and can be completed in any order, although you must do them if you intend to remain aligned with the [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").

For this quest, you will be instructed to speak with [Priest Drureth](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Drureth "Skyrim:Priest Drureth"). He can be found in one of the side rooms within the temple in Ashfall's Tear. He will hand you a transcribed *[Propaganda Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Propaganda_Letter "Skyrim:Propaganda Letter")* which will need to be translated from the original [Daedric text](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Alphabet "Lore:Daedric Alphabet") before it can be distributed.

### Information Campaign

The Raven Rock Temple would be very interested in knowing about this letter

Return to Raven Rock with the untranslated letter and speak with [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi"). She is a former Temple priestess and will agree to secretly translate the text of the letter. If you have not yet encountered Aphia, she can initially be found just inside the entrance to [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"). It will take her two hours to translate the document.

With the translated letters in hand, you will be presented with two options on how to progress the quest:

- Give the letters to the [Reclamation Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest") within the Raven Rock [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple"). He will reward you with a leveled amount of gold.

- Distribute four copies to the general public, You will need to persuade, intimidate or bribe them to read the letter or to show the letter to their patrons. Plenty of individuals can be targets to take the letter, both in Skyrim and Solstheim, even those random encouters, a small example are listed in below table.

| Name | Home | [Speech challenge level](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") |

Completing either of these options will complete the quest and will progress your list of tasks for Matriarch Drevlan. When all three tasks are completed, she will give you the quest [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart").

### Reward

The outcome of this quest depends on whether you chose to distribute the propaganda or alert the New Temple authorities, there're 4 circumstances in total, either no upgraded Ashfall's Tear, level 1 upgraded Ashfall's Tear, level 2, level 3.

If you chose to distribute the material to the public, you will return to Ashfall's Tear to find a number of new occupants. These new converts will have cleaned the temple's living areas, replacing the destroyed furnishings previously found there, all planters are now sprouting plants. Talk to [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") for gold reward, and she will give you [Letter from Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Letter from Matriarch Drevlan"), both the letter, the gold rewarded and the upgraded Ashfall's Tear have 3 versions depending on whom you disseminated the translated propaganda letters to.

- No upgrading and [large gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), if you give all four translated propaganda letters to the [Reclamation Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest") for gold reward.
- Level 1 upgrading and [small gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), if you give all four letters to non-business people, there will only be one new [Ordinator](/wiki/Skyrim:Ordinator "Skyrim:Ordinator") and one new [Temple Priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Priestess "Skyrim:Temple Priestess"), and the forge will be still obsolete without [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith").
- Level 2 upgrading and [medium gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), if you give at least one letter to business people except [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), there will be 4 new [Ordinators](/wiki/Skyrim:Ordinator "Skyrim:Ordinator") and 2 new [Temple Priestesses](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Priestess "Skyrim:Temple Priestess"), a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith_(NPC) "Skyrim:Blacksmith (NPC)") vendor will appear along with a now-functioning [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and his merchant chest under the floor by the forge.
- Level 3 upgrading and [large gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), if you give at least one letter to [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), on top of level 2 upgrading, [Caretaker Ineril](/wiki/Skyrim:Caretaker_Ineril "Skyrim:Caretaker Ineril") will appear as a new general goods vendor in the alchemical garden.

If you have ever given at least one of the translated propaganda letters to the [Reclamation Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest"), after you complete [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart") and return to [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") once again, he will appear in the company of three members of the [Redoran Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") and attempt to kill the heretics within, you are free to join in if you so choose, however they four are much weaker than the whole heretic, the Reclamation Priest carries [Reclamation Priest's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest's Journal").

## Notes

- You needn't disseminate all four letters, only one is enough to upgrade Ashfall's Tear, the rest three can be given to [Reclamation Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest"), however [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") is the best target because of the appearance of [Caretaker Ineril](/wiki/Skyrim:Caretaker_Ineril "Skyrim:Caretaker Ineril").

## Quest Stages

| Her Word Against Theirs (ccASVSSE001\_QuestB) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

| 20 |  | I have a propaganda letter from Priest Drureth that requires a translation. I should speak to his contact in Raven Rock to have the translation done. *Objective 20:* Deliver the propaganda letter to the translator |

| 40 |  | I delivered a propaganda letter to a contact in Raven Rock in hopes of getting it translated. Having waited a few hours, I need to pick up the translated letters. *Objective 40:* Retrieve the translated letters |
| 50 |  | I delivered propaganda letters to a contact in the city and waited a few hours for her to translate them. After retrieving the letters, I can now disseminate them to the general public, or give them to a Reclamation Priest. *Objective 50:* Distribute the letters (0/4)  *Objective 60:* Give the letters to the Reclamation Priest |
| 100 | ☑ | I delivered propaganda letters to a contact in the city and waited a few hours for her to translate them. After retrieving the letters, I finished the task as I saw fit. |
| 1000 | ☑ | At a hidden temple in Raven Rock, I gained possession of a propaganda letter that required a translation. I delivered the letters to a contact in the city and waited a few hours for her to translate them. I then retrieved the letters and finished the task as I saw fit. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 60, 70, 80, 90, 500.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccASVSSE001_QuestB stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccASVSSE001_QuestB`.

# Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)

## Overview

This article is about the game you can play with children. For the Dawnguard quest, see [Hide and Seek (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(quest) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (quest)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Play a round of Hide and Seek with some [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children") in town.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Any child |
| Location(s): | Any major town and some other locations |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | WIGamesHideAndSeek |

.jpg)

Hide and Seek (game)

## Walkthrough

Hide and Seek is an [activity](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities#Interactions "Skyrim:Activities") that can be played with children in Skyrim. Once you have agreed to play with a child, all of the children in the area will run and hide; you must find them all to complete the quest. Most of the children will hide behind buildings or in shadowy areas, but they should all be relatively easy to find. If you have not found the children after a certain amount of time, the quest will end automatically.
Hide and Seek has no purpose other than for roleplaying, although it could be used to help level [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"). No rewards are given.

If you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") loaded, children you have adopted will also occasionally ask you to play with them. This version of the game only involves that one child.

## Notes

- Games are only playable from 8am until 9pm.

## Quest Stages

| Hide and Seek (WIGamesHideAndSeek) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
|  |  | *(Assigned as appropriate during the game)* *Objective 10:* <Alias=PlayerIsIt> is it. Hide from <Alias=PlayerIsIt.PronounObj>  *Objective 20:* You're it! Find someone. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIGamesHideAndSeek stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIGamesHideAndSeek`.
