# Skyrim:Hide and Seek (quest)

## Overview

This article is about the Dawnguard quest. For the game you can play with children, see [Hide and Seek (game)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(game) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Kill a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") masquerading as a citizen.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") |
| Location(s): | Radiant city or town |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted item |
| ID: | DLC1RH01 |

.jpg)

Vampire masquerading as a Traveling Bard

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard").
2. Dispose of the target ([Traveling Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Bard "Skyrim:Traveling Bard"), [Traveling Pilgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Pilgrim "Skyrim:Traveling Pilgrim"), or [Visiting Advisor](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Advisor "Skyrim:Visiting Advisor")).
3. Report back to Gunmar.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak with [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") and tell him you are ready to offer some help. He has located the whereabouts of a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") masquerading as a common citizen, and wants you to track him down and dispose of him.

Your target would be a [Traveling Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Bard "Skyrim:Traveling Bard"), [Traveling Pilgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Pilgrim "Skyrim:Traveling Pilgrim"), or [Visiting Advisor](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Advisor "Skyrim:Visiting Advisor") (see [Bugs](#Bugs)) at a radiant city or town. This can include [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") if [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed. However, as the law is unaware of the danger, you will be treated as a criminal if you're caught.

Travel to your destination and identify your target. If you talk to him and expose him as a vampire, he will initially deny it. *"I beg your pardon, sir/ma'am. I don't know what you're getting at, but whatever it is, it's not appreciated."*

You can then either attempt to [stealthily](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") dispose of him, or try to convince him to follow you, which allows you to lead him to a secluded location for elimination. To do this, you will need to pass a speech check requiring a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") level of at least 75 (Persuasion) or 50 (Intimidate):

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Come with me. **(Persuade)**  - I'll take you to the monster you're hunting. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Monster? What monster? Don't know what you're *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* game is, but I'll humor for a moment. Lead the way. Take me to this "monster" of yours. But I'm warning you, do anything funny, and you'll regret it. **Failed**: What are you talking about? I don't know anything about any monsters. | | | | **Passed**: Make the target follow you **Failed**: Nothing |
| Follow me, or you'll regret it. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Settle down. No need for threats. Lead the way. But I'm warning you, I'm not afraid to fight you if I have to. **Failed**: I'm no so easily coerced. I've got my eye on you. Try anything, and you will be the one who regrets it. | | | | **Passed**: Make the target follow you **Failed**: Nothing |

Once you return to Gunmar with the good news, he will reward you with a leveled enchanted item and note his satisfaction: *"Very good. That's one less monster we need to worry about. Though there's plenty more where he came from. Be ever watchful."*

## Notes

- Attacking the vampire before he is hostile and killing him will increase your murder count statistic in your journal, regardless if you are detected or receive a bounty. One way to avoid this is to cast a [Frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(spell) "Skyrim:Frenzy (spell)") spell on him first if he is low enough level to be affected. You can alternatively kill him as a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf"), or if [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") shout to command a dragon to kill him.
- ([DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")) If your quest arrow does not appear, your target may be on Solstheim. Traveling to Solstheim will make the arrow appear in the relevant location.

## Bugs

- Sometimes after killing the target without being seen, a single nearby Hold guard will become hostile. They won't attempt to stop you for a bounty (since there isn't one) and no other guards will be hostile to you.
- The quest was intended to go to a [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Bard "Skyrim:Traveling Bard"), [merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Merchant "Skyrim:Traveling Merchant"), or [pilgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Pilgrim "Skyrim:Traveling Pilgrim"), but instead of a merchant, a visiting advisor will be chosen. If so, there won't be any dialogue to convince him to come with you. You may however paralyze them while sneaking and let your conjured kill them instead. Ensure any followers are waiting in a structure or a good distance away from combat to avoid any bounties.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- It is not considered a crime to attack the disguised vampire despite being warned by Gunmar that it would be if you're caught.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the vampire will spawn inside of a buyable house meaning they cannot be reached unless it has been purchased.

## Quest Stages

| Hide and Seek (DLC1RH01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Gunmar has sent me to <Alias=Habitation>. I am to find and kill the vampire masquerading as a <Alias=Target>. I am to do so discreetly as the law is unaware of the threat and will assume I have murdered a citizen. *Objective 10:* Discreetly kill <Alias=Target> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Gunmar |
| 255 | ☑ | I found and killed the vampire masquerading as a <Alias=Target> in <Alias=Habitation>. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH01`.

# Skyrim:High Gate Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: High Gate Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:High_Gate_Ruins "Lore:High Gate Ruins")) | | |

High Gate Ruins

**High Gate Ruins** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)"). It contains three zones: *[High Gate Ruins](#High_Gate_Ruins)*, *[High Gate Ruins Catacombs](#High_Gate_Ruins_Catacombs)*, and *[Vokun's Throne Room](#Vokun.27s_Throne_Room)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell")**: Acquire [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang") and use it to get [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska")**: Help [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") trace her roots in High Gate Ruins.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

A [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush and a small rock formation are on the left side of an arch with two lit braziers just before the entrance. The statues of two birds' faces can be found just above the braziers, and the statue of a man's head is at the top of the arch.

### High Gate Ruins

The ruins are occupied by draugr. There are numerous [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") that can be looted throughout. Speaking with [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") near the entrance initiates the quest [A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska"). In the large room after the room where Anska is first found, there are three draugr, one on the ground level and two on the second level. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") toward the far wall, and some shelves against the east wall holding a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a few [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks. On the walkway above the chest is an altar and a bookshelf where a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a random one-handed [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), and four random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") may be found. Following the walkway around to the west brings you to a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")* near a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). An unlocked chest can be found by following the walkway all the way around to the east.

At the rear of the walkway is an iron door with a passage behind it descending several flights of stairs that are trapped with two [spear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"). At the bottom is a room guarded by three leveled draugr. There are many large and small shelving units holding a random weapon, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), five random potions, two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), two bowls of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a [luna moth wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing"), a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a large coin purse, and two [apothecary's satchels](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). There is also an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") at the rear of the room to the left of the passage onward.

A passage leads past a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap and an upright sarcophagus containing a leveled draugr to another two-tier room containing four levers. If Anska is with you, she will comment on the room being some sort of puzzle. True enough, set into the floor is a wooden spiral stairway under a trapdoor which is opened by pulling the levers in the correct order. The solution is carved into the rock high up on the walls of the room: **Eagle—Whale—Fox—Snake**. The solution is displayed on both the south and north walls of the room, although on the north wall, the third symbol is missing. At the bottom of the spiral stairway is a small catacombs, with a sideboard on the left holding a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and an iron door ahead leading to *High Gate Ruins Catacombs*.

### High Gate Ruins Catacombs

From the entrance into this area, a corridor leads deeper into the catacombs past an upright dormant draugr who awakens at your presence, before you descend a spiral stairway. At the bottom, the passage passes into a chamber with many alcoves on either side. There is a leveled draugr on the right before the passage turns. Pass some barrels to two more draugr at the next corner. Ahead is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from in front, and another draugr standing in an alcove to the left. The next area has a sideboard with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and a third random potion on top. Next is a leveled draugr in an alcove to the left, opposite a chest with a pressure plate in front that triggers a spear trap from behind the chest; eight loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") are also scattered on the ground in front of the chest. Around the corner are iron doors that open into a room with two upright sarcophagi and a plinth with a random soul gem atop a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"). Removing the soul gem will cause the sarcophagi to burst open, revealing two leveled draugr. There is an adept-locked door in the southeastern corner, behind which you can find a set of shelves holding an unlocked chest and a one-handed weapon. In the southwestern corner is a passage heading south, passing a sideboard with another couple random potions, then widening similar to the passages that normally approach puzzle doors. There are many pressure plates along this section: the first five trigger spear traps thrusting up from the floor, and the last three trigger dart traps. At the far end is a set of double doors.

Through these doors is another room similar to the room with the soul gem, but this one contains a lever in the center and two doorways in the corners blocked by large stones. Pulling the lever opens the right-hand door and releases a leveled draugr. In the alcove behind that draugr is a second lever that operates the other door. After dealing with a second leveled draugr, check their alcove for a third lever that opens the iron gate to the east, which leads to a very short passage. To the right along this passage is a set of shelves holding six random potions, a random two-handed weapon, a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"). An iron door to the east at the end of the passage leads to *Vokun's Throne Room*.

### Vokun's Throne Room

A short corridor leads to the set of double doors opening to the throne room proper. Along the corridor is a large stone bowl containing three leveled potions, one each of healing, magicka, and stamina. As you approach the double doors, they will automatically open to reveal Vokun rising from his sarcophagus. When dispatched, Vokun drops his eponymous [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(item) "Skyrim:Vokun (item)") and a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs").

On the far side of the throne room is a treasure chamber containing two unlocked chests (one of which contains good loot), several urns and burial urns, and a word wall which teaches a word for the Storm Call shout. The [scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealed_Scroll "Skyrim:Sealed Scroll") for the quest A Scroll For Anska will be sitting on the stone table in front of the word wall.

A shortcut back to the exit is found on the upper level of the treasure chamber, to the left of the room as you enter from the throne room. A passageway leads via a chain-operated gate to a balcony overlooking the room in which Anska was originally found. The balcony has two sets of shelves holding a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), a burial urn, a food sack, and a bowl of bone meal.

## Notes

- Two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") are 240 feet south-southeast of the ruins, on the hills behind the ruin.
- If *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* is installed, the ruins are a very short distance northeast of [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor").
- When the location respawns, no boss enemy spawns in Vokun's room to replace him, so the doors to the treasure chamber will not open, as Vokun's death initially triggers their opening. To work around this, see the [Bugs](#Bugs) section below.
- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush outside with the snow-covered version of the same plant.

## Bugs

- If a radiant quest ([Azra's Staffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Azra%27s_Staffs "Skyrim:Azra's Staffs"), [Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!"), or [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights")) has been accepted and directs you to High Gate Ruins, the staff or book will be in a chest in the treasure chamber behind *Vokun's Throne Room*. However, the chamber will be inaccessible if you have already visited High Gate Ruins and killed Vokun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be resolved by using [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands, either to resurrect Vokun and kill him again (select the body, not his ashes), or to simply pass through one of the closed gates (use `tcl` to turn clipping on and off).
  - *Vokun's Throne Room* may be accessed by using a follower to open the gate blocking you from the treasure chamber exit above the first room. This is accomplished by bringing a follower after clearing out the entire dungeon (it is not yet confirmed whether clearing the dungeon first is necessary), climbing up the pile of rubble in the first room beside Anska, and using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout or climbing the rubble at the left corner of the balcony to access the walkway leading to the exit from the treasure chamber. The follower will run through the dungeon, and eventually, in approximately 1-3 minutes, appear on the other side of the gate from you. The follower can then be instructed to pull the chain, thereby opening the gate and permitting you into *Vokun's Throne Room*.
    - Since the 1.4 patch, using the [wait](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping#Waiting "Skyrim:Sleeping") command while standing against the gate no longer works.
  - Another fight-fire-with-fire solution is to "kettle step" through the wall. It's a glitch where you set a kettle on the floor, mouth down and bottom up, then use Whirlwind Sprint over the top of the upturned kettle. If done right, you will go through the door.
  - You can clip through the gate by using Whirlwind Sprint while holding a bowl up to the gate in the throne room. Doing so will cause you to clip through the gate.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2 to open the gates if you returned after Vokun was dead failed to account for arriving in the location if you were there to kill Vokun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- When you first enter *High Gate Ruins Catacombs*, Anska will state, *"That gem looks suspicious to me."* This should be triggered when you enter the room with the soul gem on a pressure plate later in the zone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- When revisiting the ruins, the four puzzle levers used to open the trapdoor spring back, so the trapdoor will not open.
- In the puzzle room, pulling only the Eagle, Whale, and Snake levers (in that order) also opens the floor grating.

# Skyrim:High Hrothgar

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: High Hrothgar ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Hrothgar)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:High_Hrothgar "Lore:High Hrothgar")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| HighHrothgarExterior01, HighHrothgarExterior02, HighHrothgarExterior03, HighHrothgarEntrance, HighHrothgarEntrance02, HighHrothgar | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |

| Southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") Northwest of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | |

High Hrothgar

**High Hrothgar** is a small [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") roughly halfway up the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"). It is a major landmark and home to the reclusive [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), who are masters of [The Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Voice "Skyrim:The Voice").

Traveling to High Hrothgar requires scaling the "[7,000 steps](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps")" from [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). On the way up to High Hrothgar there will be at least one [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") on the path regardless of your level (though you can avoid fighting it), and you will potentially encounter several more cold-themed enemies like [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear") and [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"). In addition to enemy encounters, a few travelers will be seen on the way to the top - pilgrims who are exploring and reading the wisdom etched on the [ancient tablets](#Etched_Tablets). Reading all of the tablets grants the [Voice of the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_of_the_Sky "Skyrim:Voice of the Sky") effect for 24 hours, which prevents animals from either attacking or fleeing from you; the tablets do not need to be read in numerical order to obtain this effect.

## High Hrothgar Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") | | --- | | **[Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir")**  **[Borri](/wiki/Skyrim:Borri "Skyrim:Borri")**  **[Einarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Einarth "Skyrim:Einarth")**  **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)")**  **[Wulfgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulfgar "Skyrim:Wulfgar")** | |

### Main Quests

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").
- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Climb the Steps](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps")**: Deliver a load of goods up to High Hrothgar for [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek").
- **[The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power")**: Follow the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards")' advice to learn a [Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power") from a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Between the two curved exterior stairwells that lead up to the building itself, there is a blue chest, three large sacks, and a smaller sack which are all set as non-respawning containers and can thus be safely used for storage.

### High Hrothgar

Once you have completed [The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller"), you can safely take any items from within High Hrothgar. If you later kill Paarthurnax during the quest [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)"), taking items here will then be counted as stealing.

[Draught of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"),

[Potion of Haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"),

The etchings on each tablet

| --- | --- | --- |
| **Emblem I**    Before the birth of [men](/wiki/Lore:Men "Lore:Men"), the [Dragons](/wiki/Lore:Dragon "Lore:Dragon") ruled all  [Mundus](/wiki/Lore:Mundus "Lore:Mundus").    Their word was [the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Voice "Skyrim:The Voice"), and they spoke only for  True Needs.    For the Voice could blot out the sky and flood the  land. | **Emblem II**    Men were born and spread over the face of  Mundus    The Dragons presided over the crawling masses    Men were weak then, and had no Voice | **Emblem III**    The fledgling spirits of Men were strong in [Old  Times](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Era "Lore:Mythic Era")    Unafraid to war with Dragons and their Voices    But the Dragons only [shouted](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") them down and  broke their hearts |
| **Emblem IV**    [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne") called on [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Lore:Paarthurnax "Lore:Paarthurnax"), who pitied Man    Together they taught Men to use the Voice    Then [Dragon War](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_War "Lore:Dragon War") raged, Dragon against [Tongue](/wiki/Lore:Tongues "Lore:Tongues") | **Emblem V**    Man prevailed, shouting [Alduin](/wiki/Lore:Alduin "Lore:Alduin") out of the world    Proving for all that their Voice too was strong    Although their sacrifices were many-fold | **Emblem VI**    With roaring Tongues, the [Sky-Children](/wiki/Lore:Children_of_the_Sky "Lore:Children of the Sky") conquer    Founding the [First Empire](/wiki/Lore:First_Empire_of_the_Nords "Lore:First Empire of the Nords") with Sword and Voice    Whilst the Dragons withdrew from this World |

| **Emblem X**    The Voice is worship    Follow the Inner path    Speak only in True Need | | |

## Notes

- It seems that early in *Skyrim'*s development, you would have been able to freely enter High Hrothgar before [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") was completed, as Arngeir has unique dialogue should he be spoken to before that quest is finished. It is still possible to enter High Hrothgar early through the back doors by climbing the mountain around it on a horse.
- [Todd Howard](/wiki/General:Todd_Howard "General:Todd Howard") jokingly mentioned in an interview that he would count all the steps leading up to High Hrothgar to make sure it's 7,000.
- Despite being referenced by local NPCs including [Gwilin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gwilin "Skyrim:Gwilin") and [Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung") as the "7,000 steps," there are only around 700-800 steps on the path between Ivarstead to High Hrothgar. When walking, it takes approximately 2,400 footsteps from High Hrothgar to reach the base of the path. Walking 7,000 footsteps from High Hrothgar will actually bring you to the town center of Whiterun.
- There are banners hanging throughout the High Hrothgar interior with two separate phrases written on them; either "LOK BO" or "THUUM TUUM". Unfortunately, it is impossible to translate them completely as not enough of the [Dragon Language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language") is known. We DO, however, know that "Lok" means "Sky" and "Thuum" means "Shout" or "Voice". Therefore, the most likely translation is a phrase that [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") commonly says when you engage or exit conversation with him: "Sky above, voice within."
- The wind barrier in the courtyard deals 25 points of [cold damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") per second, making it impossible to pass without [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies"). Even with a high level of [frost resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost"), the magical wind can kill you quickly.
  - Although Clear Skies will blow the wind away, it will return after a few seconds, so you'll need to move quickly to traverse the path.
- You can ask all [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") residents what they know about High Hrothgar, except for [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi").
- If you bring [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") here, she will kneel and meditate the same way as the Greybeards.
- If you transform into a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") when you're here, the Greybeards will attack immediately.
- According to [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), High Hrothgar is neutral territory regarding the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War").
- The Greybeards can occasionally be seen shouting in the courtyard during the day.

## Bugs

- The compass directions inside High Hrothgar are turned 90 degrees counterclockwise compared to outside.
- The gate near the mountainous edge of the back courtyard of High Hrothgar has very odd collision issues. While it is opening, part of its left door will lose its hitbox and pass through you. This will also cause its hitbox to distort and move to the south a short distance, which will persist even after the gate is closed. **?**
  - It isn't possible to interact with the gate from the distorted hitbox, as you can only close it from where the model is.
  - These collision bugs don't occur with the right side of the gate.
- The end tables behind the beds have been placed such that the drawer of each one clips through the bed's headboard each time you open them. **?**
- When speaking to Einarth, Borri, or Wulfgar after The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller, the rumble as each one says "Dovahkiin" starts before the word is spoken.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. It will now start AFTER the word is spoken.

Highmoon Hall

**Highmoon Hall** is the residence of [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch").

## Related Quests

- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.
- **[Assist the people of Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Assist_the_people_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Assist the people of Hjaalmarch")**: Assist the people of the hold. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a guard standing to the right of the entrance at all times. There are snowberry bushes on either side of the stairs leading up to the entrance. To the right of the entrance is a lean-to, with two chicken's nests holding chicken eggs under it. Farther to the right is a nirnroot beside a pool of water, and a few paces away is a patch of giant lichen and a blue mountain flower.

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot")  2 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries")  1 [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Highmoon Hall

Highmoon Hall throne

Upon entering, you are in the main room, where the Jarl holds court. During the day, the Jarl will be sitting on their throne at the far end of the room, with their bodyguard standing beside them. On either side of the room are wooden benches, stairs leading up to two bedrooms, and a door and a doorway leading to two ground floor rooms. There is also a long fire pit in the middle of the room. There are a large number of mounted [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") on plaques around the building.

Armory inside Highmoon Hall.

The doorway to the southeast leads to the military advisor's room. This room consists of six weapon racks holding an assortment of [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") on the northwest wall to the left of the doorway. There are many straw bales around the room. To the right of the weapon rack is a practice dummy. In the northern corner of the room is an unowned single bed beside a pile of firewood. Against the southeast wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with a wall shelf above holding two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), two [potions of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Against the southwest wall is a long wooden table holding a map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") showing the progress of the civil war; the military advisor will spend a lot of their time studying this. To the right is a second unlocked chest, with a wall shelf above holding two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two minor healing potions, and two [potions of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka").

The sleeping quarters of the jarl.

Opposite the doorway is the door leading to the Jarl's bedroom, which consists of a large unowned double bed in the center of the room on a raised platform, and three wardrobes to your left as you enter, two tall and one small. On top of the small wardrobe is a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). To the right, still against the wall to the southwest, is a large round wooden table and two chairs holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and two goblets. Against the rear wall to the northwest are two long unlocked chests. In the northern corner of the room are two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and two sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). In the eastern corner is a small round wooden table and chairs. On the table is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), seven loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), two bottles of wine, a bottle of alto wine, and a goblet. There is a wooden bench to the right of the door against the southeast wall.

The stairs to the southeast lead to a balcony area and a door to Idgrod the Younger's bedroom. On the balcony is a small round wooden table and chair holding three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and at the other end is a larger round wooden table and chair holding a mead barrel, two bottles of Nord mead, and a bottle of alto wine. The bedroom consists of an unowned single bed in the eastern corner, with a small wardrobe to the left holding a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). To the left of the door is a set of shelves holding three potions of minor healing, two potions of minor magicka, two potions of enhanced stamina, a [draught of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Draught of Enhanced Stamina"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), three [hagraven claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and a wooden bowl holding three [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"). To the right of the door is another set of shelves holding a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two common books, four bottles of wine, and two bottles of alto wine. Against the southwest wall is a dresser holding two loaves of bread. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bottle of Nord mead, a medium coin purse, and three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"). To the left in the corner is a food barrel with five loose coins and a large coin purse. Against the southwest wall is a long unlocked chest, with another wall shelf above holding three bottles of Nord mead.

The stairs on the right lead to a matching balcony and a door to Joric's bedroom. On the balcony are several barrels of food, one of which has four bottles of Nord mead on top, with another holding a bottle of alto wine. There is a wooden bench and a small round wooden table and chairs. On the table are three more bottles of Nord mead, a bottle of wine, and a bottle of alto wine. The bedroom consists of a single unowned bed in the northern corner, as well as a set of shelves opposite holding three cheese wheels, three lockpicks, a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor magicka, two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), three [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), and copies of *[Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim")*, *[Dwemer Inquiries Vol II](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Inquiries_Vol_II "Skyrim:Dwemer Inquiries Vol II")*, *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*, *[Nords of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Nords of Skyrim")*, *[The Monomyth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Monomyth "Skyrim:The Monomyth")*, *[Walking the world, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, and the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Locked Room](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room")*. Against the southwest wall is a long unlocked chest, with a chair in front of it. On the southeast wall is a wall shelf holding a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"), two red apples, and three green apples.

## Gallery

- 

  The main hall of Highmoon Hall.
- 

  Joric's bedroom.
- 

  Idgrod the Younger's bedroom.

## Notes

- As you approach the door to Highmoon Hall for the first time, you may witness a conversation between some of the residents of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and [Aslfur](/wiki/Skyrim:Aslfur "Skyrim:Aslfur"), the Jarl's steward.
- Though it may seem like [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") is Morthal's [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard"), he is simply an ordinary spell vendor trying to make a living within [his shop](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House"), and the court of Morthal does not employ a court wizard.
- Due to how densely packed the hall is, Gorm the housecarl sleeps in the war quarters where the military advisor normally sleeps. This results in Highmoon Hall being the only Jarl's longhouse to not feature the usual military cot there, but instead a proper bed for Gorm. It also results in the advisor having to sleep [elsewhere](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse"), resulting in [some](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis#Bugs "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis") [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrald_Frozen-Heart#Bugs "Skyrim:Arrald Frozen-Heart").

## Bugs

- If the Stormcloaks take over Hjaalmarch, Pactur is supposed to move to the hall with Sorli and act as steward, judging from his dialogue and faction. However, due to an oversight, she will only bring Teeba-Ei to Morthal, while Pactur stays in [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"). This is fixed by the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- Joric is assigned a bed upstairs but seems to have trouble using it. When he's up there he cannot get into bed, and stays up all night, either sitting on the chair in the same room or occasionally popping from one spot to another.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. The bed was neither owned by Joric nor marked as a child's bed, which made it impossible for him to use it.
- You may not be able to wait or sleep inside the hall at night, and if you try, you will receive notifications that you cannot do so when being told to leave, even though the hall is marked in the game files as a public area and nobody is telling you to leave. This is because the sleep packages of the hall's occupants have "lock doors" and "warn before locking doors" checked when those in other Jarl longhouses do not.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=16831))
- If the Stormcloaks take over Hjaalmarch, Pactur may accuse Teeba-Ei of trespassing when they're here because Teeba-Ei was never assigned to the relevant [faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Longhouse_Faction_(Both_Sides) "Skyrim:Morthal Longhouse Faction (Both Sides)") like all the other possible occupants.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.

Highpoint Tower

**Highpoint Tower** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"), [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), and [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")'s former apprentice [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril"). It contains only one zone, *[Highpoint Tower](#Highpoint_Tower)*.

The fort will be inaccessible until after starting the quest [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends"); before starting the quest, ash blocks the entrance.

## Related Quests

- **[Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends")**: Find the source of attacks on [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

### Exterior

Highpoint Tower chest

The fort is mostly buried under a mound of rock and ash, with only the broken tower still visible. Several [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants and [trama roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") grow in the area. Southwest of the tower is a [heart stone deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit"), with a large rock to the north that can be used to jump onto the top of the tower to access a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Northwest of the tower at the base of the hill is a flight of stairs. At the top of the stairs is a tunnel guarded by two ash spawn leading to the entrance to the interior of the fort.

### Highpoint Tower

The entrance leads into a circular room partly filled with ash, debris, and skeletal remains. On the ground is a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with three food barrels partly buried in the ash to the west and southeast. To the south is a caved-in room containing four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), and two empty barrels. To the southwest is a spiral stairwell descending to a landing featuring two chairs, a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"), an open box containing a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a metal basin containing two pieces of firewood, a bucket containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and an open chest containing a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two small coin purses, and an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). Farther down the stairs, on the next landing is a chair and a table holding a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), another random potion, and *[Ildari's Journal, vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._I "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. I")*, in which she promises to exact revenge on her former master, Neloth.

At the bottom of the stairwell is a table holding two [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"), two food barrels, and two sacks, with a fish barrel, an empty barrel, another sack, and a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide") near and beneath the table. To the northwest is a broken archery target, with two [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") embedded in the target and a quiver of steel arrows next to the target. To the southwest is a corridor leading deeper into the fort.

Exploding spider eggs

The corridor opens into a cave with several spider eggs on the southwest wall, one of which is an albino spider egg which can be looted for [albino spider pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Albino Spider Pod") and [damaged albino spider pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Damaged_Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Damaged Albino Spider Pod"), and three of which are [exploding spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Exploding_Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Traps") that will burst open to release [flame spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiders#Flame_Spiders "Skyrim:Spiders") as you approach. On the ground is a pair of iron gauntlets to the right of the entry corridor, a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") in the middle of the cave, and a [steel plate helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Plate Helmet") next to a pillar to the west. To the southwest among the spider eggs are two tunnels from which two [flame cloaked spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Cloaked_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Flame Cloaked Spider (creature)") and two albino spiders will emerge. To the north is a short set of stairs ascending to a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Traps") and another corridor from which two ash spawn will emerge.

More spider eggs

The two tunnels to the southwest both lead to a passage with a [web sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Containers"), two albino spider eggs, and two [ruby geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Geode "Skyrim:Ruby Geode") along the walls, with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on the ground in the tunnel to the right. The passage is patrolled by an albino spider, and leads northwest past some clearable spiderwebs to another cave. To the northwest is a natural ramp descending to a lower level, with a pair of iron gauntlets, a steel dagger, and a small coin purse on the ground at the top of the ramp. To the left of the ramp are two [sapphire geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Geode "Skyrim:Sapphire Geode"), and to the right of the ramp is an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") and an [amethyst geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Geode "Skyrim:Amethyst Geode") (the only such geode in the game). To the west at the back of the cave is a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), an albino spider egg, an imp stool, an [emerald geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Geode "Skyrim:Emerald Geode"), and another natural ramp descending to the lower level. On the lower level are two exploding spider eggs which will release [jumping frost spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Jumping_Frost_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Jumping Frost Spider (creature)"), an albino spider egg, a piece of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), and a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe").

Returning to the first cave, the corridor to the north with the spellcaster trap leads past a food barrel and two sacks among some rubble to a doorway on the left. Beyond the doorway is a circular room. In the middle of the room is a sack next to some scaffolding. To the southwest is a naturally lit alcove beneath a hole to the outside, with a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") on the rocks. To the northwest are some ash piles from which two ash spawn will rise, with an open chest containing a [strong box](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Strongbox "Skyrim:Containers") partly buried in the ash. To the northeast is a set of shelves holding two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and a deer pelt, with a sack and four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") in front of the shelves and an unusable anvil to the left of the shelves.

Returning to the corridor, the path continues northeast past an empty barrel, a spellcaster trap, and a bottle of wine to a doorway flanked by four pieces of firewood and a sack on a pair of crates. Beyond the doorway is a circular room rigged with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Tripwire "Skyrim:Traps") that triggers a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Traps") trap, with an [elemental rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Traps") trap in the middle of the room. A wooden bridge crosses above from southwest to northeast, with a cage containing a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") hanging from the bridge. To the north is a torture rack and an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") holding three empty soul gems, with a basket containing a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") beneath the enchanter. To the southeast is a bloody wooden block with a woodcutter's axe on top. To the east is another corridor which continues past an open box containing a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a food barrel, and two sacks and a cow hide among a pair of crates to a junction. An elemental rune trap is on the wall ahead, and the path branches to the north and south.

Niyya

To the south is a doorway and a crate with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and a random book on top, with a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") in front of the crate. Beyond the doorway is a small room containing three prison cells. In the middle of the room is a chair and a small round table holding *[Ildari's Journal, vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._II "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. II")*, which chronicles her plans to experiment on the miners. On the ground next to the table is a lootable skeleton. The cells to the south and east are novice-locked and contain only skeletal remains, while the cell to the west is adept-locked and contains a hay pile and a prisoner named [Niyya](/wiki/Skyrim:Niyya "Skyrim:Niyya"). If you release her, she will briefly describe recent events before running to escape.

Chest on the ceiling

Returning to the junction, to the north among some rubble is a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), a medium coin purse, a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). Above the rubble is an open chest embedded upside-down in the ceiling containing a large coin purse, a small coin purse, and a [flawless diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Diamond "Skyrim:Flawless Diamond"); the chest's contents can be obtained by careful use of [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") or an explosive spell to scatter them. The path turns east to a wooden ramp descending to a wooden walkway above a natural passage. To the right on the walkway is a crate with a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") and a bottle of Nord mead on top, with an open box containing another bottle of Nord mead next to the crate. The walkway continues to two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") on the east and west walls.

At the bottom of the ramp, the passage turns north and leads past a broken cart containing a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") and then leads into a cave. In the middle of the cave is a pillar surrounded by scaffolding and a ramp, with a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") at the base of the pillar, a sapphire geode at the top of the pillar, and a broken cart containing two pieces of firewood and a woodcutter's axe beneath the ramp. To the east is an orichalcum ore vein. To the west is another sapphire geode. To the northwest is an opening leading to a larger cave.

Ash guardian device

The large cave features a platform surrounded by three pillars capped with white lights, with scaffolding and ramps ascending to a pair of damaged towers. As you enter the cave, Ildari will appear at the top of the tower to the northwest and criticize Neloth for sending a "low life" to finish her off. The pillars will then spark to life and cause an [ash guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian") to appear on the platform. A couple more steps into the room will cause five ash spawn to rise.

To the northwest behind the platform is a ledge with a Namira's rot. To the west is an archway, the top of which can be accessed by climbing the nearby rubble or with a single word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") from the wooden platforms. On the archway is an empty cart, a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), a woodcutter's axe, five pieces of firewood, a wood pile, a [philter of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Strength "Skyrim:Philter of Strength"), and an open box containing a sample of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a filled [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), and a copy of *[Souls, Black and White](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls,_Black_and_White "Skyrim:Souls, Black and White")*.

Beyond the archway is a small cave containing four [white caps](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), three imp stools, two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), two Namira's rot, and a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), with a pair of iron boots on the ground to the east. In the middle of the small cave is some scaffolding. At the base of the scaffolding is a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and a sample of imp stool on a crate, an open box containing four random hats, a [wedding wreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Wedding_Wreath "Skyrim:Wedding Wreath") (one of only two in the game), a [gold jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Jeweled Necklace"), a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace"), and a small coin purse, and a cart containing two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a bottle of wine.

Returning to the large cave, near the bottom of the ramp southwest of the ash guardian platform is a basket containing six [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and three [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). The ramp ascends to the top of the first tower, with a barrel of fish to the left and an open chest under the next section of the ramp to the right containing a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), a set of small antlers, a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a bowl of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), and two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). To the south partly buried in ash is a food barrel, an empty barrel, an empty open chest, a basket containing a pair of leather boots, and a crate with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a random book on top. The ramp continues to ascend past an open box containing a deer pelt to a walkway crossing to the top of the other tower.

On top of the other tower, to the east is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") holding two bowls of bone meal, with a bowl containing a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe") to the left of the lab and a bowl containing two samples of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers") and a [hawk beak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak") to the right of the lab. To the left of the alchemy lab is a chair and a small round table holding a strong box and *[Ildari's Journal, vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._III "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. III")*, in which she describes her plans for Neloth. To the southwest are three sets of shelves holding a [snow fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Fox Pelt"), a [beehive husk](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk"), a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), four [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), two empty [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a [torchbug thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax"), two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a sample of [tundra cottom](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random potion of stamina, a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a loaf of bread, an [Eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [flawless sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), three blue mountain flowers, a red apple, two bowls of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), two empty common soul gems, two [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), and a copy of *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*. To the northwest is another ramp. Beneath the ramp is a narrow table holding a bottle of alto wine and a random book, a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a food barrel, a fish barrel with a piece of bread and an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top, a crate with a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt") on top, and a basket containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd").

Ash spawn

The ramp connects to a natural passage leading southwest past two sacks and three turns to a ledge along the wall to the right, where an ash spawn will attack and three more will rise from the ground. At the top of the ledge is a lootable skeleton, a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat"), a [Skaal hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat"), a pair of [Skaal boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots"), a pair of [Skaal gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Gloves "Skyrim:Skaal Gloves"), and a strong box. The passage continues to a hole in the wall of the fort, with a bleeding crown to the left.

Ildari

Beyond the hole is a northeast-southwest corridor. To the northeast is an empty barrel and a cave-in, with an open chest among the rubble containing two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), and an imp stool. To the southwest is the wooden bridge crossing over the tripwire room to a twisting corridor leading past a sack and a crate with a leather strip on top. The corridor continues to the lower level of a room, with Ildari and two spellcaster traps on the upper level opposite the entry. She is a powerful mage armed with a [staff of lightning bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts"). Deplete her health until she kneels and cannot be damaged further; this is your opportunity to rip the [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") from her chest. Once the heart stone is removed, she will drop dead.

On the lower level of the room, in the north corner opposite the entry is a wood chopping block, a crate with a woodcutter's axe and two pieces of firewood on top, and a wood pile. Along the southeast wall is a raised platform with an open box containing a sample of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bowl of fire salts, and a bowl of bone meal, a crate with a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") on top, an open chest containing a deer pelt, an arcane enchanter, a sack, an open box containing an empty common soul gem, a food barrel with a set of small antlers and a sample of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") on top, and an ingredient barrel. Next to the pillar on the platform is an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), a crate with a random book on top, and an ingredient barrel with a bowl of bone meal on top. Southwest of the platform is a doorway leading to the stairs ascending to the upper level.

Still on the lower level of the room, along the northwest wall under Ildari's area is a kettle containing an iron helmet and a pair of iron boots, two crates, one of which has a deer pelt on top, and a bleeding crown growing between the crates. Along the southwest wall is a sideboard holding two sacks, a leather strip, and a cow hide, with three more sacks to the left of the sideboard. Next to the pillar near the sideboard is a crate with a leg of goat on top, four sacks, and two food barrels, one of which has a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") on top. Near the pillar is a wooden block, two pieces of firewood, and an open box containing an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), and a small coin purse, with a cage containing a lootable skeleton hanging from the ceiling.

On the upper level of the room, along the southeast wall is a balcony with a [dead rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a bunch of dried frost mirriam hanging from a rack, a fireplace, with a chair, a bottle of wine, and two pieces of firewood in front of the fireplace, two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and a garlic braid hanging from a rack, a crate with a deer pelt on top, and a doorway blocked by spears. A stone bridge crosses to the northwest to Ildari's area. In the west corner is a raised platform with a small table holding a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower and a bowl of glow dust, a boss chest, a set of shelves holding a [fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Fox Pelt"), a random potion of healing, a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a sample of hawk feathers, and a random potion of magicka, and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") on a short stone pillar at the edge of the platform. Along the northwest wall is a sack and a basket containing four samples of wheat. In the north corner is another raised platform with a small round table, a wall shelf holding an empty [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem"), a single bed, a bottle of wine, an Eidar cheese wedge, and a [rabbit haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch") next to and beneath the bed, and two [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flowers and a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower on two short stone pillars at the edge of the platform.

The lever to lower the spears to the southeast is next to the bridge. Beyond the previously blocked doorway is a stairwell ascending past a candlestick and an empty open chest to a concealed door with a pull chain to the left. Beyond the door is the caved-in room near the entrance.

## Notes

- If you trigger the falling boulders in the circular room and release Niyya without clearing all the boulders from her path, she is likely to die from damage caused by coming into contact with the boulders and not escape from the tower.
- When attacked in melee, one of the ash spawn in the final group may attempt to retreat, running all the way to Ildari. If the two spellcaster traps near Ildari have not been disabled, the explosions triggered by the ash spawn will dislodge the soul gems on the traps, disabling them.
- The rare [Telvanni robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Telvanni_Robes "Skyrim:Telvanni Robes") can be looted from Ildari Sarothril. Neloth wears a set as well, but you can only obtain Ildari's.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- The exterior chest and Ash Spawn respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "No Reset Zone". **?**

## Bugs

- Followers may get stuck on the platform the Ash Guardian appears on.
  - Solution: Knock your follower off the platform with [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), or sprint into your follower, forcing them out of the way.

# Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb

## Overview
