Hillgrund's Tomb

**Hillgrund's Tomb** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains only one zone, *[Hillgrund's Tomb](#Hillgrund.27s_Tomb)*.

The tomb is where [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir")'s dead ancestors are interred.

## Related Quests

- **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his ancestral barrow.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The path up to the barrow is at the west end of a bridge over a large tributary of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), near its confluence with the [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River"). Walking up the steps of the path, you'll pass under numerous stone arches before arriving at the tomb entrance, where Golldir fights an internal battle between fear and family honor. There is a firepit in the center of the room, with sideboards on either side of a locked iron door (key required) leading into the barrow itself. The sideboards hold three [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and four common books. In the eastern corner of the antechamber is a frostbite spider egg sac. A level-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") can be found behind the tomb's entrance, up against the cliff that overlooks the barrow. Just a few feet east of the chest, on the ground, is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Golldir will approach and ask for your help. Once you agree to help, he will unlock the door to allow access inside. This will start the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship").

### Hillgrund's Tomb

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image** **of:** *Interior image(s)* See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

Hillgrund's Tomb is fairly straightforward, but there are some side rooms and things that can be missed. A light source such as [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight") or [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") is preferable for navigating the fairly dark area, unless of course you have a form of [night vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(effect) "Skyrim:Night Eye (effect)"). There are countless [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") that are ripe for looting. If Golldir is with you, he will object to you looting his family's tomb, but then sigh and ultimately agree to you helping yourself as long as you help put a stop to [Vals Veran](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran").

The first room you enter has a central stone altar, two thrones against the side wall, and a dead draugr on the floor by the open door out of this room. Beyond this doorway is a narrow flight of stairs leading down to a corridor that continues down several flights of stairs to the southeast. There is a draugr patrolling the stairs near the top, with a second farther down. Opposite is a wooden door with an apprentice-leveled [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") behind the door. There are four sprigs of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") on the ground in front of the door. Behind the door is a small alcove containing a large urn, behind which are six small holes in the wall. Three of the holes contain draugr, but only the top right-hand one with the feet showing can be looted.

Descending the stairs to the southeast, after passing a broken throne and an upright sarcophagus on your left, you will reach a landing with a raised area on the left containing a sideboard with a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in a holder. There is a closed wooden door on the right, with a few [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and several bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") in front of the door. Behind the door is a small catacomb area, with a leveled draugr standing in an alcove, and more bottles of wine lying in an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") on the floor. Around the corner is a mead barrel and three dead draugr in small holes in the wall, two of which can be looted. There is a third lootable draugr on your left as you enter.

Returning to the main passage, descend a final flight of stairs to a lit area, with a novice-locked chest at a turn to the southwest leading to an iron door. Picking the chest's lock will cause Golldir to complain, as mentioned previously. Through the door is a room with two leveled draugr inside. You will also find the body of Golldir's aunt [Agna](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") in the middle of the room. There is a set of shelves to the east holding a bow and some [ancient Nord arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Arrow "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Arrow"). To the south are barred double doors with stone tables on either side holding a bowl with three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a garlic braid, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two pieces of bread, three cheese wedges, a bowl of bone meal, and a potion of minor healing. To the west is a wooden door. Golldir mentions a secret route to the central chamber that avoids the barred doors. The route is through an abandoned part of the barrow that contains disgraced ancestors. Before leaving this room, you can access a hidden alcove opposite the barred double doors by pulling a chain on the wall to the left of the movable stone. The stone will slide down to reveal an unlocked chest, a healing potion, and a second potion.

The way forward is through the western door, beyond which is a far more decrepit and dangerous catacomb. There is the occasional [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") growing, and several of the alcoves contain draugr that can be looted. At the bottom of two small flights of stairs is a caved-in section, a wooden door to the north, and two draugr that will rise and attack as soon as your presence is detected. Among the cave-in rubble is an unlocked chest.

Through the door to the north is another catacomb. In the second section are two draugr slumbering upright in alcoves opposite each other. Attacking one will alert the second, unless you have a sufficiently high [sneak skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"). After you have dealt with these, Golldir will warn you of a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Around the corner to the north is a T-junction with three leveled draugr, two of which are slumbering in alcoves to the west, with the third roaming. The pressure plate Golldir mentioned is to the west, between you and the draugr. As soon as you engage the first draugr, the remaining two will join the battle. Once they are all dealt with, you can investigate the area. To the east is an adept-locked chest and more draugr to loot. The path to the west then turns south and continues forward to a wooden door.

This brings you back out beyond the caved-in section. There is a slumbering draugr in front of you, and a gap to the west. Beyond the gap is a room with many cobwebs and an iron grating in the middle of the floor with water beneath it. A [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") will drop from the ceiling as soon as you enter. To the east up a few steps is an upright sarcophagus hidden behind webbing that houses a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") with a random enchanted [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") beside it. There is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") to the south, immediately to the right of the path onward. The only other item of note in the room is a web sac from which you can harvest a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail").

Continue through the catacombs until you pass a symbol of a whale on your left. Shortly past here, things can get quite hectic, as there are several high-level draugr that will join the attack as soon as any fighting starts. There is a brightly-lit area with a slumbering draugr in an alcove to the right of a large urn, a second around the corner in an upright sarcophagus, and several more in alcoves farther along the catacombs. Once you have dealt with all the draugr, Golldir will announce that it looks like the area his aunt told him about, and that "The bear will show the way". Looking around the area, you will find symbols on the walls similar to the [ancient puzzles](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Puzzle_Pillars "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") seen throughout [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). The bear is on the corner of a wall to the south, with a lit brazier and a chain hanging down beside it. To the right of the bear symbol is an alcove with a selection of growing fungi, including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and fly amanita.

Pulling the chain will punch out the cover to an upright sarcophagus to the east, revealing the way forward. Through the sarcophagus is a room with a sideboard holding a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), and several sarcophagi against the walls around the room. In the southwest corner is a leveled draugr sitting on a throne. There is an empty set of shelves in the middle of the east wall, and to the right is an arch through to another part of the room. This section features an apprentice-locked wooden door to the south, behind which is an alcove containing a sideboard holding an unlocked chest, a random healing potion, a random [magicka potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), and a leveled magicka potion.

To the northeast are double iron doors which, as Golldir comments, lead to the main chamber where Vals Veran is performing his necromancy. Beyond is a multi-leveled room with several flights of stone stairs, with Vals Veran on the highest level to the north. Unless you kill him with a single hit, he will teleport around the room while waves of draugr awaken and join the fight. Once the boss-leveled draugr rises, Vals Veran will stop teleporting. Once you've killed him, you will still have up to nine leveled draugr to face. At higher levels, this can become quite challenging, with the draugr all able to use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). There is a master-locked iron door to the north from the highest level; the door is unlocked by the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb_Crypt_Key "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb Crypt Key") carried by both Golldir and Vals Veran. Beyond this is a small room with the barred door found near the beginning of the barrow opposite, and an expert-locked chest to your right that is opened using a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Chest Key") given to you by Golldir if he has survived. To your left is a stone table holding a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [gold necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Through the barred door, you are led back to the room where Agna's body was found.

## Notes

- An adept-locked chest can be found 370 feet south of the entrance to the tomb, along with a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")*. They are all next to a rotten tree stump with a dead bandit nearby.
- If you continue past the chest to the south, you will come to a large tree that has fallen and now spans a large gorge, with a bandit standing in the middle and more on the other side. They will attack if you try to cross, although given their precarious position, using an Unrelenting Force shout on them will knock them off into the river below and a swift death. Assuming the corpse fell exactly under the tree down to the water, dive and you can find another bandit corpse beside a gold necklace.
- There is a small room east of the main chamber that can't be reached by normal means. This is where Vals Veran teleports between the waves of draugr. If he is killed while teleporting, his body can end up stuck in this room.
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* lists Hillgrund's Tomb as being located in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"); however, it is in fact located in the Pale per internal game data (see also [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Bugs

- Although Hillgrund's Tomb is geographically located within the borders of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), in the game data it is identified as being within [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- The exterior items may respawn despite Hillgrund's Tomb being classed as a "no reset zone".

# Skyrim:Hired Muscle

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Alfwyn](/wiki/User:Alfwyn "User:Alfwyn"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to bring a citizen back in line.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold |
| ID: | CR04 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms") | | |

*"I just need you to go out there, look tough, and scare this milk drinker into submission."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to the assigned target.
2. Brawl with them to send a message, but don't kill them.
3. Return to [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas").

## Detailed Walkthrough

:   *Note: it is best to complete this quest as soon as possible after receiving it, because many of the quest targets can possibly die (either through random or scripted events), at which point it becomes impossible to ever complete the quest or take any other jobs for the Companions.*

Farkas will send you to rough up one of over 400 different NPCs, encompassing nearly every citizen in Skyrim. The NPC will be located in a hold that you have previously visited, so early in the game you may only be given NPCs living in Whiterun Hold, but later in the game there are many more possible options. The NPC may live in a city, town, or a remote settlement.

Once you have traveled to the target's location, talk to them and select the dialogue option to [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl") with them. It is best to start the brawl in an area with as few other NPCs as possible. In particular, it is best to have any [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") wait in a different room. You may not use any weapons, magic, or shouts during a brawl (but using spells such as [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)") or [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh") before the fight is permissible). If anyone else becomes hostile as a result of your brawling, you should be able to run to a guard and yield, clearing any hostility.

If you kill the target, you will still complete the quest. The quest is marked as "Failed" in your quest journal, but it is no longer active, and you will be allowed to pursue other jobs in the Companions questline. Farkas will not be pleased, and you will receive a decreased amount of gold for your reward.

Return to Farkas for a gold reward.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- If your target is someone you can [fight for money](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!"), you can collect a reward from them after the fight, even if you've already won a bet with them previously.
- If your target is someone you can brawl for another quest (such as [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael")), winning a brawl will complete the objective for both quests simultaneously.
- There is a silent Intimidate check against the target as part of the quest's startup conditions. If it succeeds, you won't get the quest.

## Bugs

- When you should "Return to Farkas", he doesn't give you the option to complete the quest. **?**
  - Check whether you have quests from other Companions Council members and try completing those first. E.g. "Stealing Plans" from Aela will hinder you from completing "Hired Muscle".
- If one of the targets dies before you get the quest, you can no longer finish the quest or take any other jobs. **?**
  - You can reload a save before taking the contract.
  -  Type `Setstage cr04 20` into the console.
- Some targets reside in locations that require you to trespass. In these cases, your target's dialogue will constantly loop *"You're not supposed to be in here"* and not allow you to initiate the brawl, rendering the quest impossible to complete correctly. **?**
  - Assault the target and then run to a non-trespassing location out in public, where the target will follow you. You can then yield by sheathing weapons, calm the target by using the [Voice of the Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_of_the_Emperor "Skyrim:Voice of the Emperor") power, pay the fine for assault, or go to jail and hurry back to the target.
  -  Use the console commands `prid` and your target's RefID, then `movetoplayer` to move the target to you, and the brawl can be initiated without committing a crime.
  - You may clear the quest from your active quest list by killing the target and thus failing the quest. After killing the target, return to Farkas and he will give you a lesser amount of gold for your payment before allowing you to take another job.
- It is also possible to get a target that has disappeared from the game. For instance, [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar") after you have convinced him to leave. **?**
- Farkas may be selected as the target of the quest, which will result in the game telling you to leave and then re-enter Jorrvaskr in an unending loop. **?** [*verification needed — Is this true?*]
  -  Typing `Setstage cr04 20` into the console will allow you to skip the intimidation step and complete the quest.
- If the quest target doesn't have conversation topics then there will be no option to start a brawl and the quest won't be completeable. **?**
- If you wear the Ebony Mail, have a companion, a dragon decides to attack the settlement, and the settlement is in the Whiterun hold the target can end up dead, and the guards will become hostile, and continue to attack you. The Companions will also become hostile. Reloading the game will cause all the Companion NPCs to break. **?**
  - You can escape combat with the guards and un-equip the Ebony Mail, then return to the settlement and pay the fine, or go to jail, but only if you haven't reloaded the game.
- If the target has another possible response from a different quest they would use that instead and leave this one dangling. Sometimes this would result in brawl opponents paying off a reward a second time even though they aren't supposed to do that.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. This was due to the alias dialogue response being at the bottom of the available list of choices. It has now been moved to the top where it will function correctly.
- This quest may pick potential followers and hirelings as targets which then leads to brawls that take forever due to the high health that these NPCs get because they level with you. Brawls of sufficient length tend to risk turning into assaults the longer they run.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Hired Muscle (CR04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | <Alias=Brute> has been causing trouble for someone around <Alias=BruteTown>. I need to rough <Alias.PronounObj=Brute> up to remind <Alias.PronounObj=Brute> of <Alias.PronounPosObj=Brute> obligations. *Objective 10:* Intimidate <Alias=Brute> in <Alias=BruteTown> |
| 20 |  | <Alias=Brute> won't be causing as much trouble for <Alias=BruteTown>. *Objective 20:* Return to Farkas |
| 30 |  | I got carried away and killed <Alias=Brute>. *Objective 20:* Return to Farkas |
| 40 |  | <Alias=Brute> was killed, through no fault of my own. *Objective 20:* Return to Farkas |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| 105 | ☒ |  |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR04`.

# Skyrim:Hitting the Books

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |
| Location(s): | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") |
| Reward: | [Skill books](#Rewards) |
| ID: | MG03 |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | **Next →** [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | | → Next | [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") | | |

Urag gro-Shub giving directions on how to learn more about the orb

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
2. Make your way through [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep").
3. *(Optional):* Free [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn").
4. Find the three stolen books.
5. Return the books to the College.

### The Arcanaeum

After the discovery of the mysterious Orb in the depths of [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), a puzzled [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") decides to send you back alone to alert Arch-Mage [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"). Aren turns out to be quite uninterested in the whole affair. You will then be given the quest and prompted to go speak to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine"), who then sends you along to librarian [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") to research the subject. Locate Urag, who can usually be found behind his desk inside the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") where he functions as the librarian and keeps a close eye on the College's huge collection of ancient tomes. After warning you about touching any of the books in the library, the old Orc will mention that there may be relevant information in one of three tomes which are no longer in his possession. They were 'borrowed' by an Apprentice named [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") who recently, due to a dispute with the College, joined a group of renegade mages in [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep"). Urag can do nothing for you without the books, and says you'll have to find Orthorn to retrieve the books so the research of the Orb can begin.

On your way out the door you may be approached by [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") who tells you that the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") visitor, [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano"), wants a word with you. If you do not see Faralda, Ancano will actively seek you out and ask you questions about what was found in Saarthal. During this discussion you can choose to provoke him or not, but he will always get the answer he seeks. Proceed out the door and prepare for Fellglow Keep.

### The Dungeons

Fellglow Keep is a large fort located between [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). When you arrive it becomes clear that the residing mages are far from friendly as you will be attacked by two elemental mages and a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach"). Dispose of them and locate the entrance to [Fellglow Keep Dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep_Dungeons "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep Dungeons").

Upon entering, head down the stairs and follow the path as it twists and turns. The second flooded room is guarded by another hostile mage who has been experimenting with [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and will send them after you with the words: *"Ah, a test subject! Go, my pets! Attack!"* Fight the spiders and the mage, then proceed southeast and beware of the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Traps") triggering a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Traps") along the way. Before long, you will arrive in a room filled with cages containing some very unusual prisoners, specifically leveled [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). You can use the four handles to release them, or pick their cell locks, and they will cause havoc in the next room before leaving the dungeon peacefully. The next room reveals that several experiments were conducted on vampires as bodies are everywhere. Locate the northeastern tunnel and listen to the sound of [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") howling. In the next room are more cages and another hostile mage, seemingly another experiment chamber. Dispose of the mage and inspect the cages. Apart from the wolves, you will also find the renegade mage [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn"), seemingly imprisoned by the mages he thought of as friends.

### Orthorn

[Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") in action

As it turns out, Orthorn was imprisoned as yet another test subject by the mages, despite the fact that he came to Fellglow Keep to help them. You can choose to comfort him by saying Savos Aren sent you to rescue him, or you can simply be honest and say you are there solely for the books. In both cases, Orthorn will offer to help clear out the dungeon and find the missing books, so decide if you want him to tag along. Pull the lever in the middle and he will be released from the cage. He will proceed to explain that the books were taken by someone known as [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller"). If you accept his help you will have to put up with his comments for the rest of a very long trip, although he is a powerful [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and wields a [lightning bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") spell. If you decline, he will head out of the dungeon peacefully. Regardless of your choice, he is disabled later on and disappears from the game.

Unfortunately, the nearby door leading to [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") is locked (key required), so you will have to take the long path. Go through the wooden door and make your way through the trashed tunnels. The next chamber has three fire mages training destruction spells on a living [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") in a cage, so be on your guard when they notice you. You can find a copy of [The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle") on the table in the middle of the room. Take the northern path and you will reach the undercroft, which is guarded by [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). There is a pedestal with a copy of *[Spell Tome: Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Raise Zombie")* just before the stairs leading to the next zone, Fellglow Keep.

### Fellglow Keep

There is a small table at the end of the hallway before the stairs that has a coin purse and an easily missed [Black Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") behind a book. The first chamber of Fellglow Keep is guarded by a [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and an ice mage and has the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")* on a pedestal. Open the eastern door and fight the patrolling necromancer, then proceed through the chambers and fight all the enemies in the room with multiple paths. A locked door (key required) leads outside while the eastern door leads to the sleeping quarters and more enemies. Check all the shelves for rare books, then head up the stairs. The room to the west holds an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") so make sure to pick it up. Take the adjacent path and head upstairs to a room filled with shelves and the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")* on a table. Proceed forward and make sure to check behind the closed doors for some extra loot. One of the doors is locked but pick the lock and find a [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrines") to [Julianos](/wiki/Lore:Julianos "Lore:Julianos") and a wealth of ingredients. Open the wooden door to the north and start climbing the tower. Before long you will reach the Fellglow Ritual Chamber and an encounter with [the Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller").

### The Caller

The Caller waiting in the ritual chamber

You arrive in the ritual chamber right away and the Caller awaits you, right in the center. She will, however, remain calm and greet you: *"So, you're the one who barged into my home and laid waste to my projects. How nice to meet you."* You will have two dialogue options to choose from; either ask her who she is or ask for the three books. The first option will make her respond, *"Names no longer matter. You may refer to me as The Caller. Now, do you have a reason for making such a mess?"* When you ask her for the books she will be disappointed: *"So you're just one of Aren's lackeys? That's disappointing. You show real promise. You come here, kill my assistants, disrupt my work... You've annoyed me, so I don't think I'll be giving you anything."*

At this point it is actually possible to persuade her to let you have the books. Alternatively, if you brought Orthorn along with you, you can negotiate with her for the books. She will then say, *"An arrangement? After you've destroyed so much? Fine. Leave me the elf. You may go with your books."* You have to walk up to the Caller and start a conversation. Agree to her conditions, then pick up the book. If you simply pick up a book without doing this she will attack you. If you didn't bring Orthorn, she will say, *"I'm afraid you don't have anything worth trading."* Dispose of her and claim the three books (two of the books are behind the Caller on pedestals; lifting either will spawn a Flame or Frost Atronach, depending on your level). If Orthorn is still there, you can have a brief conversation with him which he ends with: *"You'll be going back to the College, then? I, uhh... I think perhaps I'll wait a bit before venturing there myself. Let this whole thing blow over, you know. Give certain parties a chance to forget what I may have done. Still, you've gotten me out of that cage, and I won't forget it. Thank you again, and good luck to you."* Find the exit and leave Fellglow Keep. You may still need to kill the Caller to obtain the key to the exit.

### Night of Tears

When you arrive back at the College, you will find that [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") has returned from Saarthal and placed the Orb in the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"). Head into the Arcanaeum and locate Urag gro-Shub. Out of the three books, *[Night of Tears](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_of_Tears "Skyrim:Night of Tears")*, *[The Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:The Last King of the Ayleids")*, and *[Fragment: On Artaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment:_On_Artaeum "Skyrim:Fragment: On Artaeum")*, he will be particularly interested in the first one, as it has some interesting implications. The quest ends with him handing you a bunch of books as reward (see [this section](#Rewards)) and asks you to speak to Tolfdir. The next quest, [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), will then start.

## Rewards

Upon returning the books to Urag gro-Shub, he will give you several [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), one for each school of magic. The books are:

- [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"): *[Daughter of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Daughter_of_the_Niben "Skyrim:Daughter of the Niben")*
- [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"): *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")*
- [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"): *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")*
- [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"): *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*
- [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"): *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")*
- [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"): *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")*

## Notes

- At stage 60 of this quest, the Eye of Magnus is invisibly moved from [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal") to the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"). [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") also returns to the College at this time, allowing you to start [his quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir_the_Absent-Minded "Skyrim:Tolfdir the Absent-Minded").
- There is another book called *[Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:Last King of the Ayleids")*. You need to find *[**The** Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:The Last King of the Ayleids")*. The text is the same, but the other book will not work for this quest.
- Even if you didn't kill anyone by sneaking through the dungeons, the Caller will still blame you with the same dialogue.
- While the Caller will not accept a dead Orthorn in exchange for the books, it is possible to trick her into accepting the deal even if he dies. If Orthorn's corpse is reanimated prior to entering the Ritual Chamber, he will follow the player in as normal, and the quest can proceed as if he is still alive.
- Using the "Persuade" option when speaking with the Caller while Orthorn is accompanying you results in the same outcome as trading him for the books. He will return to his cell, and approaching or interacting with him will be met with "How could you just leave me here?"

## Bugs

- [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") was originally supposed to play a part in this quest, at stage 10 and 20 specifically. For unknown reasons, she was skipped and Tolfdir now asks you to go directly to Savos Aren from Saarthal. However, the in-game text still describes the original journal intro including Mirabelle Ervine.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- The College students are supposed to gather next to the Eye of Magnus and play out a scene. Unfortunately, due to issues with the scene trigger, this would never happen because the trigger would be encountered prior to this portion of the quest being reached since the trigger box has no conditions and would become disabled upon first entering the Hall of the Elements.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.
- Once you clear the fort, trying to enter it again will cause a crash. This can happen even during the quest if you try to backtrack from the Ritual Chamber. If you are on the quest just leave by the exit to the exterior in the chamber.
  -  To avoid this, enter `coc FellglowKeep03` in the console to move to the Ritual Chamber, complete the quest, and use the console again to exit the keep (`coc WinterholdExterior01`).
- There is a possibility that the stairway leading up to the Caller's room in Fellglow Keep is blocked off with boulders, and the door leading up to her room is removed.
  -  Enter `coc FellglowKeep03` in the console to bypass the boulders.
- If you collect the books before talking to Orthorn he may not recognize it when you free him. Messing with the levers can eventually trigger a quest update for him being freed.
- If Orthorn is killed before reaching the Caller and she accepts your "Persuade" offer, the door to the exit may remain locked with a "Requires Key" status.
  - Killing the Caller will allow you to obtain the key from her corpse.

| Hitting the Books (MG03) | | |

| 30 |  | I've been asked to find more information on the object found in Saarthal. Urag suggested that useful books may have been stolen from the Arcanaeum by Othorn *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, a former Apprentice at the College. His last known location was Fellglow Keep. *Objective 30:* Find the stolen books (<Global=MG03BooksFound>/3) |

He's now a prisoner, and has begged me to free him. *Objective 50:* (Optional) Free Orthorn |

I've found the books and now need to see them returned to the College. *Objective 60:* Return the books |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Stages 10 and 20 are unused.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG03`.

Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp

**Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), located south of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and northwest of [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills").

This camp will only be present if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") hold [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and the rest of Hjaalmarch, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Legate Taurinus Duilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis"), except during the related quest, when [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") takes command. Like similar Imperial camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has neither a [quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster") or any [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Taurinus Duilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis") (commander)  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)")**: Retake [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

## Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp

It is a typical Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. There is an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside the fire. To the northwest is the Legate's tent, with the command tent to the right and the hospital tent to the left. The Legate's tent contains an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and a dresser beside it. The command tent contains an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. The hospital tent contains four bed rolls, three of which are occupied by wounded soldiers, a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). To the left of the hospital tent is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), while to the right is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and some barrels. Northeast of the campfire are three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. To the south of the campfire is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").

Any time [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents.

## Notes

- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp

**Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), located east of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and west of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").

A Stormcloak quartermaster working at the bench

The camp is normally commanded by [Arrald Frozen-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrald_Frozen-Heart "Skyrim:Arrald Frozen-Heart"), except during the related quests, at which point [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will assume command.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") cooking over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Around the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. West of the campfire are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. To the north is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, a round table, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. To the northwest is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the left of the commander's tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). East of the campfire is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Beside the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") and some barrels. To the south is the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table and a crate hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor").

Any time [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

The salt marshes of Hjaalmarch

**Hjaalmarch** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in northern [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with its capital in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). It is initially affiliated with the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), though the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") laments the war and reportedly co-operates with the Empire only as far as their goals align. It can, however be captured by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") after completing [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)") and [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)").

Despite its position just east of the capital of Skyrim, [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), Hjaalmarch is remote and isolated. The enormous, festering swamp dominating the northern part of the hold could be a factor, as could be the tall, snowy mountains in the south, and the ancient, cursed city of [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") blocking a possible trade route to [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").

Hjaalmarch is one of the poorest holds in Skyrim, second only to [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), and is sustained by the Morthal lumber mill and the mining town of [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"). [Jarl Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") takes a hands-off approach to leadership; her people are unhappy with her governance and several will complain openly.

Map of Hjaalmarch

Morthal, the capital of Hjaalmarch

## Topographical Overview

Swamp fungal pods are endemic to Hjaalmarch

Hjaalmarch is well known for the salt marshes which dominate the north and central areas of the hold, stretching from [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") in the west to [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") in the east, formed by the River Hjaal breaking into many tiny streams. Much of the rest of the hold more resembles neighboring holds, for example, in the south and east of the hold, the terrain is more resemblant of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") along the border with that hold - snowy pine forest and plains broken up by crags around [the Stormcloak camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp") and Ustengrav. The southern half is mountainous terrain above the snow line, although in the west, the mountains give way to the Hjaal river valley, where the climate is more resemblant of neighboring [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). Beyond Fort Snowhawk, in the hold's western extremities lie pine forests and meadows, much like those found just across the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

### Flora and Fauna

The swamp boasts the highest numbers of wild [deathbell plants](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") in Skyrim, as well as being the only place to find [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") and [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"). These ingredients all boast powerful poison effects for [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), making Hjaalmarch an ideal place to visit for assassins wishing to brew deadly poisons. Other plants include [canis roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") and a few scattered [nightshade plants](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"). The snowy areas have few usable plants besides the humble [snowberry bush](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry"), but there are some [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") to be found, with the blue variant especially abundant around Morthal.

As for fauna, all manner of beasts roam the swamp; even [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") might ambush you at night, but more commonly [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") lurk between the trees. Of course, [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") are always in abundance, from the swamp to the banks of the River Hjaal. Your typical predators, [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") and [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"), and their prey, [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") and [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), roam the south, but there are also more trolls to watch out for. Passive creatures include large amounts of [fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") in the shallow waters with [dragonflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonfly "Skyrim:Dragonfly") circling above.

### Routes and Pathways

A single paved road runs from the west near [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), past [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") (where [the residents](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") may attack you even if you stay on the path) and [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), curving north around the [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") area before entering the Pale.

The most notable pathway starts southwest of Stonehills and ends in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") between [Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest") and [Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp"), passing through the ruins of Labyrinthian along the way. Other paths run from the road east of Fort Snowhawk south to [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite"), and north from Morthal to [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair"). Beyond that the swamp is pathless, however, so beware of getting lost.

## Places

All locations in Hjaalmarch with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal")** — A city in the north of Skyrim, and the capital of Hjaalmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morthal)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack")** — An isolated [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") in Hjaalmarch, east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Shack)
-  **[Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty")** — A small run-down [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") on the [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crabber%27s+Shanty)
-  **[Meeko's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Meeko's Shack")** — A run-down [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") owned by the canine follower [Meeko](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko "Skyrim:Meeko"), who has inherited the home from his unfortunate [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead)#Nord1 "Skyrim:Nord (dead)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Meeko%27s+Shack)
-  **[Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills")** — A small mining [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stonehills)
-  **[Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — A piece of property in Hjaalmarch, north of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and east of the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windstad+Manor+%28HF%29)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in Hjaalmarch, located south of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and northwest of [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in Hjaalmarch, located east of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and west of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge")** — A small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave west-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Robber%27s+Gorge)
-  **[Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Talking+Stone+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Brood Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Brood_Cavern "Skyrim:Brood Cavern")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brood+Cavern)
-  **[Chillwind Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillwind_Depths "Skyrim:Chillwind Depths")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Chillwind+Depths)
-  **[Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forebears%27+Holdout+%28DG%29)
-  **[Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") led by [Movarth Piquine](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth_Piquine "Skyrim:Movarth Piquine"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Movarth%27s+Lair)
-  **[Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") that is home to bandits intent on poaching [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orotheim)

### Dragon Lairs

-  **[Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak")** — A mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eldersblood+Peak)
-  **[Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar")** — A mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") east-southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skyborn+Altar)

### Mines

- **[Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine")** — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in eastern [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rockwallow+Mine)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

The ruined city of Labyrinthian, once home to the [dragon cult](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Cult "Lore:Dragon Cult") in ancient times

-  **[Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary")** — A hidden location reached by equipping the [wooden mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Mask "Skyrim:Wooden Mask") while inside a building in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian").
-  **[Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Men%27s+Respite)
-  **[Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and the draugr [Mikrul Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikrul_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Mikrul Gauldurson"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Folgunthur)
-  **[Kjenstag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjenstag_Ruins "Skyrim:Kjenstag Ruins")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") east-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kjenstag+Ruins)
-  **[Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"), [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(creature) "Skyrim:Morokei (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
-  **[Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northeast of [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valkygg)
-  **[Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft")** — A medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzinchaleft)
-  **[Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ustengrav)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") initially occupied by [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Snowhawk)
-  **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") — A mage tower player home east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Myrwatch+%28CC%29)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[The Apprentice Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Apprentice_Stone "Skyrim:The Apprentice Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Apprentice+Stone)
-  **[The Lord Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lord_Stone "Skyrim:The Lord Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lord+Stone)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Great Lift at Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft")** — A Dwarven lift to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") located south of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Mzinchaleft)
- **[River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal")** — The main river that flows through the center of Hjaalmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=River+Hjaal)
-  **[Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner")** — An Imperial ship which will run aground east of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") and the assassin [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Icerunner)

### Unmarked Places

- There are three [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in Hjaalmarch.
  - South of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").
  - West of [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite").
  - West of [Meeko's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Meeko's Shack").

## Hjaalmarch Quests

All quests that are started in or are related to Hjaalmarch (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)")**: Find and deliver some forged documents to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk")**: Silence a [terrible bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk"), permanently.
- **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")**: Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.
- **[Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril")**: Kill [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril") in [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").

### Bards College

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").

### Side Quests

- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.
- **[Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn")**: Track down [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") to rid yourself of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

### Creation Club Quests

- **[Let Sleeping Wolves Lie](/wiki/Skyrim:Let_Sleeping_Wolves_Lie "Skyrim:Let Sleeping Wolves Lie")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf"): Stop a necromancer from raising undead wolf minions.
- **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch"): Locate and enter a [mysterious tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)").

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in Hjaalmarch. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

Hjerim

**Hjerim** is the [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") you can purchase.

Main Reception

Secret Room

Located in the Valunstrad district, the name translated from the ancient Nordic language means "Home of Frost". The property once belonged to Friga Shatter-Shield, daughter of [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield"), but it was abandoned after Friga was killed.

Purchasing the house before completing [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") will begin that quest as soon as the house is entered for the first time. Prior to purchasing any of the upgrades, Hjerim features little more than a wardrobe, poor quality double bed, and a chest. However the upgrades available for Hjerim include a large armory with many display cases, weapon and shield plaques, mannequins for displaying items, and a number of bookshelves. Hjerim also features a secret chamber hidden behind a false-backed wardrobe, which can be turned into an [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") and [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") room. It is also one of only two houses where purchasing the children's bedroom doesn't remove any of the other upgrades (the other is [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor")).

Hjerim can be purchased having sided with either the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). Once allied with the Stormcloaks, the [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") quest must be completed before [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") will make the house available for sale. However, if [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") has been given to the Stormcloaks as part of [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), it may be necessary to liberate [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") before Jorleif will make this house available. If the Imperial Legion is chosen as an ally, then the defeat of the Stormcloaks is required before it is available to buy.
