## Related Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.

## Exterior

The manor is found in the far northwest corner of the city, next door to [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") and opposite [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea"). Once you have completed the [reputation quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), in the yard, to the right of the entrance is a barrel marked with the  "Cache") Cache [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)").

## Hjerim

Prior to purchasing any upgrades, when entering the house you will find blood stains on the floor, a few bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and various pieces of clutter scattered on the floor of the first floor. In an alcove to the south is an empty [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the west is a separate area with a doorway connecting it to the main room. In this area is a small unit where you find the pile of [leaflets](/wiki/Skyrim:Beware_the_Butcher! "Skyrim:Beware the Butcher!"), a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal_1 "Skyrim:Butcher Journal 1"), and a [strange amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Strange_Amulet "Skyrim:Strange Amulet") all relating to the related quest. There is also a normal tall wardrobe containing a selection of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") and the tall wardrobe with a false back giving access to the room where the butcher performs his disgusting rites in an effort to raise his sister who died several years ago. The room contains many skulls and bones scattered all across the floor and on the table, some of which are cleaned while others are still covered in gore and blood.

Upstairs is mostly empty, with exception of the master bedroom, which contains a poor quality, large king-sized bed, coming out from the north wall, slightly away from the wall. There is a square wooden table and two chairs against the south wall. Against the east wall is a small wardrobe containing more fine clothes and boots.

**When purchasing upgrades, it's best to start with getting the house cleaned** (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

With each upgrade purchased, decorations will include several floor coverings and goat horn lights on stands, walls, chandeliers and shelves, etc. The exception is the hidden room that is now used for alchemy and enchanting as it gets neither additional light nor floor coverings. For details of what is included in each room see [below](#Upgrades.2C_by_Room).

[††](#note_Childroom)Child's Bedroom only available if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed. Choosing this upgrade will create a new room in the hall outside of the hidden enchanting/alchemy room, making the entrance to the hidden room inside the children's room.

### Clean Up That Murderer's Mess

The house is cleaned throughout, removing all blood stains, and the chest that was against the south wall is removed (make sure you aren't storing anything in the chest before purchasing this upgrade). All the clutter, etc gets removed, while in the secret room, this is fully cleaned, the bones, skulls and even the table that Calixto Corrium's sister was laid out on. A set of shelves against the west wall is added. All the items in the master bedroom remain.

### Kitchen

Kitchen

This furnishes the room that is immediately on the right when entering the house. There is a fire pit in the northwestern corner, while in the middle of the north wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging in front. To the left is an ornamental cauldron with a low table in front, and a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), four [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), two sprigs of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs all on top. To the right of the fireplace is a pile of firewood with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") sticking out of it. Above the wood, hanging from three racks are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), two bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

Against the east wall, to the right of the fireplace is a small square table and two chairs. The table holds fine crockery including [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), etc. There is a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") contained in a bowl, a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and two bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

Further to the right of the table set back in an alcove are two sets of shelves, they hold three bottle of alto wine, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), four bottles of Nord mead, two goblets, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), two [potions of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), five random [potions of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), and two random [potions of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"). Against the south wall are a pair of wall shelves, the lower shelf holds a pile of sacks, while the top shelf holds two salt piles and several wedges of cheese.

On the far side of the doorway is a small, empty bookcase, beside this is another set of shelves which holds a raw venison haunch, an eidar cheese wheel and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Against the west wall is a table that appears to be used for preparing the food. There is a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, four bottles of Nord mead, a bowl containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a raw joint of [beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), a couple of pieces of cheese, several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a bowl overflowing with [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). On the floor beside the fire pit is a cast iron pot containing five tomatoes.

### Master Bedroom

Master bedroom

There is a wooden bench on the left as you enter the master bedroom. To the right is an alcove with a tall wardrobe in the corner containing fine clothes. To the right is a small square table and two chairs with fancy crockery on the table. In the other corner of this alcove is a wash basin. The large king-sized bed is now made with fine linens an have an end table on either side, it is still coming out from the north wall, and a foot or so away from the wall. There is a shield plaque on the wall behind the bed holding twin crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") with an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") over them. In a small alcove on the east wall is a corner shelving unit holding an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), with a pile of food sacks underneath. There is a second small alcove further to the right containing a large round wooden table. On the table is a [draught of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Draught of Vigor"), a [solution of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Solution of Enhanced Stamina"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). Between the two alcoves, against the east wall, is a small set of shelves behind it. The shelves hold a [potion of extreme magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Magicka"), a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), a [potion of vigorous healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Healing") and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and copies of *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")* and *[Feyfolken I](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_I "Skyrim:Feyfolken I")*. However the original small wardrobe may get left behind--(see [bugs](#Bugs)). To the right are a set of three wall shelves. Against the south wall is a tall bookcase with a tall set of shelves to the right. These hold a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine and two dagger display cases.

### Living Room

Main reception

To the right of the door as you enter is a small wardrobe with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel in the corner beside this and a chair on the other side of the barrel. On the left as you enter is a matching small wardrobe, both of which hold fine clothes, this second wardrobe has a bottle of wine on top and a pile of food sacks beside it. To the right in an alcove is a set of shelves holding a [solution of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Solution of Extra Magicka"), a bottle of Nord mead, a [solution](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Health "Skyrim:Solution of Health") and a [philter of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Health "Skyrim:Philter of Health"), a [solution of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Solution of Regeneration"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a bottle of alto wine. There is also a drum on the floor beside the shelves. In the southeastern corner of the room is a large round wooden table and a chair, holding a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of Nord mead and a goblet. In the alcove that originally held the chest on the south wall, it now holds a set of shelves. On the shelves are three bottles of Nord mead, two goblets and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). Further to the right of this wall is a small unit holding a bottle of wine, with a large fancy vase and empty open crate beside it. There is a corner shelving unit is the southwest corner holding a bottle of alto wine. Beside the side of the stairs that leads up to the top floor are a set of shelves and a small empty bookcase. On the shelves are some pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), a woodcutter's axe—(see [bugs](#Bugs)), a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. To the left of the doorway into the kitchen is a long wooden table that holds a [solution](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength") and a [philter of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Strength "Skyrim:Philter of Strength"), a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of wine, a jug and a pile of food sacks, with more sacks under and in front of the table.

In the middle of the room is a very long wooden table laid with fancy crockery and a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, two bottles of Nord mead, a raw venison haunch, two carrots, a portion of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") fungus, a salt pile, a baked potato, a portion of grilled leeks, a salmon steak, a cabbage, a goat cheese wedge, a loaf of bread, a honey nut treat and a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide").

### Alchemy & Enchanting Laboratory

Crafting chamber

Both the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") are installed into the hidden room where [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") performed his grisly experiments and rites, the alchemy lab is against the west wall in the southwest corner. To the right of this is a set of shelves holding various [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") listed below and two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"). Against the north wall is a small empty bookcase. The arcane enchanter is in the northeast corner of the room, three weapon plaques are to the left, on the north wall and two tall sets of shelves are to the right, against the east wall. These hold two empty [black soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), two empty [greater soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem"), four empty and four filled [lesser soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), one empty and two filled [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem").

#### Ingredients

| Ingredients | | |

| 2 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal")  3 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs")  1 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell")  2 [Ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm")  2 [Falmer Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear")  3 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") | 2 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust")  1 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade")  2 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg")  1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile")  3 [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg")  2 [Spider Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") | 2 [Torchbug Thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax")  2 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat")  2 [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust")  3 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") |

### Armory

Display area

At the top of the stairs on the north wall is a set of shelves with two dagger display cases and a mannequin in the northwest corner. Against the west wall is a large display case as a weapon rack, above this on the wall is a shield plaque holding twin crossed iron greatswords with an iron shield over them. A second mannequin is in the southwest corner, while on the south wall in two alcoves are two more large display cases for displaying a weapon in each. Between the alcoves on the east wall are a row of five weapon racks. To the left of the second alcove is another mannequin in the corner with a small bookcase beside it. In the corridor outside the bedrooms are a total of four weapon plaques and two wall shelves, two on each side.

### The Child's Bedroom

Child's bedroom

The area where the wardrobe with the false back that opens into the hidden room, now containing the alchemy lab and arcane enchanter is converted into a small children's bedroom. There is a chest on the left as you enter with a practice dummy beside it. Against the south wall is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes with a set of shelves on top. These hold a flute, copies of *[Trials of St. Alessia](/wiki/Skyrim:Trials_of_St._Alessia "Skyrim:Trials of St. Alessia")*, *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*, *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")* and *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")*, a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") containing a few [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). There is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") on the floor beside the wardrobe. Two children's beds come out from the west wall with a chair and end table between them. On the end table is a copy of *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")* and some charcoal sticks. While above the left-hand bed is a wall shelf holding a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), copies of *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*, *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")* and *[Ahzirr Traajijazeri](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzirr_Traajijazeri "Skyrim:Ahzirr Traajijazeri")*, and two [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum").

- Adopted children living here will have unique dialogue comments about [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"):
  - *The Argonians at the docks say they can breath underwater. I wish I could do that...* (girls)
  - *Rolff says I shouldn't go to the Grey*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Quarter anymore. He said it's not safe there.* (girls)
  - *Grimvar said [a boy](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") used to live in that abandoned house, all alone, 'til the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") came 'n got him. Scary, huh?* (boys)
- If you ask your spouse "How are the kids?" they will reply with one of the following, depending on their [voicetype](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Adoption_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue"):
  - *Hmph. This city's crawling with filth. It's everything I can do*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *keep the children safe.* (Arrogant)
  - *Well, love, very well. There's so much history in this city, so many things we can do here.* (Neutral)
  - *Great. There's so much history in Windhelm, so much to learn about our ancestors and our land.* (Nord)
  - *Good. This is a city that respects strength. Honors it. A good lesson for children to learn.* (Orc)

### Housecarl's Bedroom

Housecarl's bedroom

Once you become Thane of Eastmarch, entering the second bedroom upstairs, there is a square wooden table and chair in an alcove on the east wall laid for one with fancy crockery. A single bed is against the south wall in another alcove, while in a third alcove on the west wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Against the north wall is a dresser also containing clothes and having a solution of strength and a [philter of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Philter of Haggling") on top.

## Notes

- The list of upgrades in the house guidebook given to you by Jorleif after purchasing the house lists incorrect upgrades.
- Even before Hjerim has been purchased as your house, resting on the main bed will render you well-rested. With the added bonus of four safe storage containers, it can be used as a home before it has been purchased.
- Hjerim used to belong to the now deceased Friga Shatter-Shield - this can be confirmed during the quest [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"), where you can ask [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") for the key to Hjerim, referring to it as "your daughter's house".

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses, see the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.

  

  Main reception upgrade, without cleaning
- The option to buy "Clean up the murderer's mess" may disappear if you purchase the Living Room upgrade first, but the "mess" will still be there. This seems to be a scripting error, as the living room option disables the cleaning option, which does not disable itself. It should reappear after the next purchase.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4.15, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `DF492.Disable` to clean up the mess.
- Due to incorrect conditions, the steward may prematurely tell you there are no more improvements that can be made to Hjerim even if the killer's mess is still present.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- When purchasing the option to clean up the murderer's mess, entering the house can cause a black screen and full freeze if the chest had anything added to it, even if it was the original contents.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The chest has now been unlinked from the enable parent marker and will remain behind when the mess is removed.
- It is possible that the chest near the master bed will not be present, even though it is listed as included.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  You can fix this issue by entering Hjerim, opening the console, and typing the following: `prid 10FD82`, press enter, then `enable`. This should make the chest appear.
  - This can be caused during [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"). If you confront [Wuunferth](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") directly instead of going to [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") with your suspicions, the chest will not appear when you buy the property later.
- The [Windhelm Home Decorating Guide](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Home_Decorating_Guide "Skyrim:Windhelm Home Decorating Guide") talks about a guest room which is not an available purchase option for Hjerim.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- The two dagger display cases in the master bedroom are buggy:
  - Most daggers placed in the lower case cannot be retrieved (Dragon Priest style daggers have been reported to be removable).
  - Daggers placed in the upper case are extremely difficult to retrieve (Daggers with unusual thicknesses, such as Keening, may be removable by facing the case from just the right angle).
  - Multiple daggers can be placed in the same case.
    -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
    -  Opening the console and typing `tcl` can be used to retrieve the daggers.
    -  If the previous solution doesn't work: Open the console, click the dagger that is stuck in the case, enter `getpos z`, note the decimal number that is shown, enter `setpos z N` where N is the decimal number +10. For example, if `getpos z` prints 216.06, then you should enter `setpos z 226.06`. This command moves the dagger so it's floating above the case, where you can easily grab it. It works for the top and bottom cases.
- The option to buy the house may exist but you are unable to actually purchase it even after completing the prerequisites as the dialogue still says it is unable to be purchased due to unpleasantness.
  -  If the quest to become thane has started and this dialogue option exists, opening the console and typing `setstage a7b33 10` buys the house (for 12000 gold).
- It is possible that after the Battle of Windhelm, Brunwulf Free-Winter may not appear in the Palace of the Kings, preventing you from being named Thane of Eastmarch and preventing the purchase of Hjerim.
  - To fix this, use Unrelenting Force on the former Stormcloak-supporting Jarls ousted by the Imperials in the Palace of the Kings. This will give you a bounty in all of the Jarls' former holds. Fast-travel away from Windhelm and return; Brunwulf should be there.
- The master bed may still say "investigate bed and chairs" when you point at parts of it. Just move the pointer to another part of the bed and the option to sleep on it will appear.
- The housecarl bed is not owned by the Housecarl faction. **?**
- The display case closest to the bedrooms can hold large weapons such as battleaxes or warhammers, but staves will disappear if placed on it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- In the master bedroom, the small wardrobe may get left behind causing it and the set of shelves to occupy part of the same space against the east wall. This obscures the bottom shelf that holds a potion of vigorous healing and a potion of plentiful stamina making them inaccessible. The old bed as well as the old table and chairs may also still be there, in the same place as the new ones. This will not inhibit your use of them however.
- If you break into Hjerim after Blood on the Ice has officially begun, but enter the building too soon, the quest would update an objective with no explanation for what's going on. Similarly, if you break into Hjerim BEFORE the latter officially begins, then either pick up a "Beware The Butcher!" flier or the amulet, the quest will initiate, but there will be no journal entry made to explain what's going on.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You may be unable to interact with the woodcutter's axe.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

Hlaalu Farm

**Hlaalu Farm** is a small farm east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

This farm is owned by [Belyn Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu") who lives in Windhelm, but is worked by [Adisla](/wiki/Skyrim:Adisla "Skyrim:Adisla"), a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") woman who lives in the single-room farmhouse on the property.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Adisla](/wiki/Skyrim:Adisla "Skyrim:Adisla") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

As you approach the property there are several [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [snowberry bush](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). Only six bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") are grown, however the farm also supports two [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") and three [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken"). Behind the house, there is a chicken coop, with a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone").

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 6 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  2 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Hlaalu Farm

The interior of Hlaalu Farm

Upon entering the farmhouse, there is a cupboard against the northwest wall holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), and two [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"). There is a flower basket containing four [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") on the floor to the left of the cupboard, with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and basket containing a selection of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") to the right. Against the northeast wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot beside a pile of firewood, and hanging above from the ceiling are two garlic braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Opposite the cupboard, against the southeast wall are a long wooden table and bench. On the table are two chicken's eggs, two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and several pieces of cheese. Hanging from a rack above the table are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)").

To the right of the table, opposite the entrance is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") and three [iron daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on the mantelpiece. To the right on a small pile of firewood is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and to the right of that is another cupboard holding mainly clutter along with copies of *[The Windhelm Letters](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Windhelm_Letters "Skyrim:The Windhelm Letters")*, *[Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")* ,*[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")*, *[Of Crossed Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Crossed_Daggers "Skyrim:Of Crossed Daggers")*, and *[The City of Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_City_of_Stone "Skyrim:The City of Stone")*. Hanging above this cupboard are three more bunches of dried elves ear and two more bunches of dried frost mirriam. Coming out from the middle of the southwest wall is an unowned single bed with an end table to the left which holds a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. To the right of the bed is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") on top. To the right of the dresser against the northeast wall are another unlocked chest and a round wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, and a loaf of bread on top.

Hob's Fall Cave

**Hob's Fall Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Hob's Fall Cave](#Hob.27s_Fall_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows")**: Find [Isabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine"), [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") lost love.
- **[The Lost Library](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Library "Skyrim:The Lost Library")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories"): Locate a huge collection of powerful spell tomes.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold").
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").
- **[Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Totems of Hircine")**: Journey to the given location to find a Totem of Hircine.

### Exterior

Hob's Fall Cave is at the end of a path enclosed by sheer walls of ice, which starts at the shoreline to the northeast and ends at the entrance. Usually, a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") will be found by the shore where the path begins. Several [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") and [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants, and a few blood splatters, are along the path. Another leveled animal is on the ice above and to the west of the entrance. A [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush can also be found nearby.

### Hob's Fall Cave

Isabelle Rolaine

Wooden palisade

If you are on the quest [Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows"), upon entering, [Isabelle Rolaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine") lies dead in front of you. She carries a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Isabelle's Letter"). Past her, the tunnel turns north then opens into a two-level chamber. This chamber contains several small empty cages, a cart filled with bones and a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") scattered all over the floor. Above you to the north is a ledge with a wooden palisade along the edge. The tunnel to the west is the apparent way forward, though it is possible to climb the ledge with difficulty (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

The tunnel twists and turns before continuing to the north. There is a skeleton patrolling this section. Shortly after the tunnel turns to the west, a necromancer sits at a table on the right with their back to you. There is a copy of *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")* in front of them, along with an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"). To the right is an unlocked chest in front of a bookcase containing copies of *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_Prince "Skyrim:Beggar Prince")* and *[The Bear of Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bear_of_Markarth "Skyrim:The Bear of Markarth")*, and another copy of *The Book of Daedra*. The tunnel continues on until it turns west and you see a lit brazier; take care, as around the corner to the right, a skeleton and a necromancer lurk.

Wooden bridge

The tunnel continues up a steep incline then turns east, where a wooden bridge spans a deep cavern. There's another necromancer and skeleton pair on the far side. Sounds of fighting may draw a patrolling necromancer from the tunnel beyond the bridge. When you turn due east again and see a descending slope in front of you, beware, as there are two necromancers and a skeleton in the room at the bottom.

Just before the entrance to the room, a tunnel branches off to the left. After a few twists, you'll find two skeletons in the tunnel. At the end, it opens into the chasm you previously crossed; the bridge is above you. Below, accessible by an earthen ramp to your left, is a room with a necromancer. The cupboard here holds an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") needed for the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), two random [potions of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and several common books. Below the ramp is an alchemy lab, and on the table to the right of that, at the bottom of the ramp, you'll find the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Exodus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Exodus "Skyrim:The Exodus")*. In the pit under the bridge right above the cupboard with the unusual gem, there is a chest on a ledge with an adept-level lock.

Backtrack to the deep cavern with two necromancers and a skeleton. On your left are two sets of shelves. The first contains a random magicka potion, a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion, and a copy of *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")*. The second contains three bottles of Nord mead, three bottles of wine, and an apothecary's satchel. To the northeast, on another raised section, are an apprentice-locked chest and a bookcase containing a random magicka potion and a random healing potion, another apothecary's satchel, and copies of *[The Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wispmother "Skyrim:The Wispmother")*, *[Aedra and Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Aedra_and_Daedra "Skyrim:Aedra and Daedra")*, *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, *[Frontier, Conquest](/wiki/Skyrim:Frontier,_Conquest "Skyrim:Frontier, Conquest")*, *[The Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Oblivion_Crisis "Skyrim:The Oblivion Crisis")*, and *[Gods and Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Gods_and_Worship "Skyrim:Gods and Worship")*. With the [Arcane Accessories](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, an "Ancient Tome Chest" containing all 16 [new spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories_Items#Books "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories Items") can be found here. Against the wall on the other side of the room is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") with a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Enchanter's Primer](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Primer "Skyrim:Enchanter's Primer")* on top. To the east in the middle of the wall is a tunnel barred by spears; the chain to lower them is to the right.

In the next room are three [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that shoot [Frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite "Skyrim:Frostbite") spells at you as you pass. It's easy enough to approach from the side and grab the gems safely, as they only shoot straight ahead. Continue to the south to find another necromancer patrolling the tunnel near a rise. At the end, the tunnel turns to the west by two barrels and then immediately to the north, rising up into a large two-leveled room with three more necromancers on the upper level.

The final room

On the bottom level is a ramp leading up to the left of a lit brazier and a wooden bench against the back wall. On the upper level is a table being used as an altar, with several benches arrayed in front. The corpse of [Larina](/wiki/Skyrim:Larina "Skyrim:Larina"), who you heard shouting when you first entered the cave, will be on the altar if she was not raised during the boss fight. The altar also holds a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") and a random [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"). Beside the altar is a small wooden table holding a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a random magicka potion. There is a boss chest to the left of the altar which will contain [Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Pantea.27s_Flute "Skyrim:Quest Items"), a quest item for the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"), among other loot (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

To the west are two hanging cages and a large, expert-locked cage containing two more corpses that may be raised. Past these is the ledge with the wooden palisade seen earlier, providing a shortcut back to the exit.

## Notes

- If you are at least level 30, you can start the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") by reading *Boethiah's Proving*.
- [Hobs](/wiki/Lore:Hob "Lore:Hob") are hairless monkey-like creatures sometimes used as servants.
- After Larina has been sacrificed, if you approach the altar, you can overhear the necromancers carrying out a ritual to the [God of Worms](/wiki/Lore:God_of_Worms "Lore:God of Worms") to create a black soul gem:

:   :   *"We offer this soul to The Revenant: he who watches over the opponents of Arkay and his power over life and death. Fie upon Arkay and his followers! Fie!"*
    :   *"Yeah, fie!"*
    :   *"Fie. We beseech you. Darken this gem so that we may use its power to restore The [Order of the Black Worm](/wiki/Lore:Order_of_the_Black_Worm "Lore:Order of the Black Worm"). The Order shall rise. Grant us this power so that in your name we may vanquish our enemies."*
:   Interrupting the ritual does nothing, as the soul gem is already black.

- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush outside with the snow-covered version of the same plant.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- If you take Pantea's Flute before you are given the quest, you may be unable to complete the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- This cave has a broken navmesh with two triangles twisted underneath the main grid which can cause NPCs to be confused and get lost while they're here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to climb the ledge in the first two-level chamber, though it is difficult and requires going right and left on the stones multiple times. You can then open a cage, talk with Larina (who will only greet you), and take Pantea's Flute without a fight, as nobody will be present except Larina.

# Skyrim:Hod and Gerdur's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Hod and Gerdur's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hod+and+Gerdur%27s+House)) | | |

| [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Hod and Gerdur's House

**Hod and Gerdur's House** is a residence in the southern part of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), located behind the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader") and across from [Faendal's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal%27s_House "Skyrim:Faendal's House").

It is the home of local lumber mill owners [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur") and [Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod"), and their son [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar"). It consists of one zone, *[Hod and Gerdur's House](#Hod_and_Gerdur.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar")  [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur")  [Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod")  [Stump](/wiki/Skyrim:Stump "Skyrim:Stump") ([dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"))  [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") † |

**†** Only if you side with him in [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound").

## Related Quests

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow")  1 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 1 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

## Hod and Gerdur's House

Cooking and dining area

Hod and Gerdur's house is laid out in an L-shape, with the front door entering to an open cooking and dining area along one side of the "L", and a bar and the bedroom areas situated on the other. None of the areas are separated by walls or doors. To the left of the door as you come in is a dining table set with two loaves and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). North of the table, a respawning food barrel sits in the corner. A [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") sits atop another respawning food barrel to the left of the fireplace, which is directly across from the front door. The fireplace mantel holds three gold coins, while a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") sits at its base. A kettle containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") rests on the floor to the right, next to a large table holding two more potatoes, a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, three servings of [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), three loaves of bread, three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). Above the table are some hanging ingredients, including dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two garlic braids, and two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Next to these hanging ingredients are two hanging racks, one of which holds two freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") while the other holds two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Two bottles of alto wine and three bottles of wine can be found on the bottom of a set of shelves to the right. A non-respawning cupboard across from the food table holds various kitchenware on its shelves, along with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and one sample of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") at the top.

Bar and bedroom area

The first bedroom area of the home starts with a single bed in the southwest corner, resting between a non-respawning dresser on one side and a non-respawning end table on the other. A respawning chest sits atop the dresser, along with a copy of *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*, and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") rests on the end table. The next area of the home includes the bar, atop which sit one bottle each of wine and alto wine, four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two [wedges of goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and some sliced goat cheese. Behind the bar is a respawning food barrel, as well as an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") on the bottom shelf. Across from the bar is a small round table with two bottles of Nord mead. The final bedroom area can be found past the bar, in the northwest part of the home. A double bed sits at the middle of the wall, flanked by a non-respawning end table on either side and with a non-respawning chest at the foot of the bed. The left end table holds a farm [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000330b3 "Skyrim:Hat"), a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), and a copy of *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*, while the right one holds a basket and four gold coins. A pair of farm [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots") sits on the floor in the left corner, in front of a medium-sized [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). An [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") is stashed beneath the bed on the left side. Along the left wall is a non-respawning wardrobe, atop which lie a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") and a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and along the right wall is a single respawning food barrel.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice-level lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Gerdur's House") to which is carried by Frodnar, Gerdur, and Hod. You will obtain a copy of the key if you followed [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound").

## Bugs

- Stump may be stuck inside the house, with no way to get him out. **?**
- Frodnar's bed isn't a child's bed, causing him to either sleep in his parents' bed or stay up all night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. His bed wasn't marked as a child's bed, making it impossible for him to use it.

# Skyrim:Holds

## Overview

Map showing the different holds

This page lists the nine **holds**, or regions, of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), each governed by a [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") who lives in the region's capital [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities").

In the absence of a High King, the holds have effectively split from one another, with some even at war with each other. As a consequence, [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") in each hold only care about [crimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") you have committed within that hold, with any bounties you acquire tied to a specific hold. In addition, the [Tribal Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribal_Orcs "Skyrim:Tribal Orcs") faction and [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") track their crime separately from any of the Nord holds.

Many of the holds have distinct climates, such as the Rift being an aspen forest, Falkreath Hold being a pine forest, and Eastmarch being tundra. Snowy mountain environments are also found in most holds.

:   **[Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch")** — A hold in eastern Skyrim, with its capital in Windhelm.
:   **[Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold")** — A hold in southern Skyrim, with its capital in Falkreath.
:   **[Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")** — A relatively small hold in northwest Skyrim, containing the provincial capital Solitude.
:   **[Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Morthal.
:   **[The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Dawnstar.
:   **[The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach")** — A hold in western Skyrim, with Markarth as its capital.
:   **[The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")** — A hold in southeast Skyrim, with its capital in Riften.
:   **[Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold")** — A hold in central Skyrim, with its capital in Whiterun.
:   **[Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)")** — A hold in northeast Skyrim, with its capital in the city of Winterhold.
